Starting Level: 12-13, 12   , 12-13, 9-10 , 12


```
Recommended       |   Gryz   |   Alys   |   Chaz   |   Rika   |   Hahn   |
Equipment   |¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|
            |Head |CRMC-HELM |GRPT-CROWN|CRMC-HELM |GRPT-CROWN|CIRCLET   |
            |Right|STRUGGL-AX|TITNSLASHR|CRMC-SWORD|SABER-CLAW|CRMC-KNIFE|
            |Left | /2-HAND  |TITNSLASHR| /2-HAND  |SABER-CLAW|CRMC-KNIFE|
            |Body |CRMC-MAIL |CRMC-MAIL |CRMC-MAIL |CRMC-MAIL |GRPT-SUIT |
 // DUNGEON #7  ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\
```

|/  Passageway             \_________________________________
   Enemies: Meta Slug, Speard, Zol Slug
  Treasure: DIMATE, CURE-PARAL
Go straight up, turning left along the way. Take the first turning down
when you reach it, and follow it to its end to get the DIMATE. Return to
the top, then continue on to the left all the way to the end. Go down and
ignore the passage to the right and the following one to the left, and
continue down and right to acquire a CURE-PARAL. Go back up and take the
left passage you skipped just now, following it around and down until you
reach another junction. Take the path to the left and continue down until
you reach the exit. You will now be in a different area.

Enemies around Kadary: Scorpirus, Speard, Tech User


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

Head a little southeast and enter the village of Kadary.

________


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\
Kadary  |Inn            |Per person     40 MST /
_______/|_______________|______________________/
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\
        |Tool Store     |MONOMATE       20 MST /
        |               |DIMATE        160 MST \
        |               |ANTIDOTE       10 MST /
        |               |CURE-PARAL    120 MST \
        |               |TELEPIPE      130 MST /
        |               |ESCAPIPE       70 MST \
        |_______________|______________________/
```

Most people in this village seem to be either under the evil spell of Zio,
or mortally afraid of him (the ruin you passed on the way here being a
village before he came along). There is a church dedicated to him here, and
a possessed man convulsing in front of it. You won't find much of any value
in terms of information here, but there is a weapon worth getting.
Go to the very bottom of town and step just outside the gate. Head to the
left and then up, hugging the wall. Take the entrance to the left, and
enter the right-hand building. There is an opened chest in here, and the
other one contains a LASRSLASHR, which you should give to Alys.

Rest at the Inn if you like, and purchase any more supplies you need, then
leave Kadary. Wander around outside, returning when you need to, until you
have got everyone in the party up to at least Level 14, preferably Chaz and
Gryz up to Level 15. If you have completed the first Hunters' Guild job,
you should already be well on the way to achieving this. Once you have
finished, fully restore your party before going south to Zio's Fort. Save
and then enter.

<a id="s6-2-4"></a>

> 🥈 **Beyond the Sand Sea** — Defeat a wild Sand Worm in east Motavia. _(RetroAchievements · 10 pts)_


### 6.2.4. Castle in the Sands

Starting Party: Gryz , Alys , Chaz , Rika , Hahn
Starting Level: 14-15, 14   , 14-15, 14   , 14


```
 // DUNGEON #8  ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\
```

|/  Zio's Fort             \_________________________________
   Enemies: Ripper, ShadowSabr, Speard, Tech User
  Treasure: 2000 MST, MOON-DEW, LASR-SWORD, DIMATE, LASRBARRIR
            LASR-CLAW
 \
  \   Boss: Juza, Zio
   \______________________________

Head up through the entrance corridor, and you will see a yellow forcefield
protecting the door to a room in the centre of this large chamber. You can
examine this 'invisible' barrier if you wish, but there is no way to get
past it at this stage. Walk to the left or right around this structure and
through the door at the top. There are two staircases here. The one on the
right doesn't lead to anything at all, so take the one on the left.

Head left and down, then turn upwards and take the staircase down to grab
2000 MST. Return up the stairs, then continue down the passage and turn
left. Drop down the large black hole here, then pick up the MOON-DEW from
the right side of the room. Exit the fort through the door on the left,
then go back into Zio's Fort and make your way back through until you are
back at the hole again. Take the stairs to the left.

Head through the opening to the right and walk through the corridor that
follows. When you are out, walk up to the top of the room and collect the
LASR-SWORD. Equip this to Chaz, then return through the corridor and go
back down the stairs.

Head right, around the bottom side of the hole, then take the thin passage
to the right. Don't bother taking the path below you, as there is nothing
there. Continue along the thin passage, ignoring the hole and the stairs
for the moment, and continue around them and down the passage. Take the
stairs at the very bottom, and then head up to obtain a DIMATE. Go back up
the stairs and up along the corridor, then drop down the hole you passed
a little while ago. Retrieve the LASRBARRIR from the left, then exit the
castle through the door on the right.

Go back to Kadary and rest up, then save and re-enter Zio's Fort. Return
all the way upstairs and back round to the hole you just dropped down, and
ascend the stairs to the right. Take the door to the left and follow the
corridor that follows until you are in another chamber. Pick up the
LASR-CLAW from the top of the room and equip it to Rika, then head down
and around to the left. Walk up the central passage until you are standing
in front of the dark-robed man. Heal up anyone who needs it, then address
the man to learn that his name his Juza and that you will need to get past
him if you intend to see Zio. A battle then ensues.


```
 __________
```

| BOSS #3  \____________  ____________________


```
| Juza                  ||                    |
|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|| Recommended Level: | 
|  HP: 1523             ||                    |
| EXP: 5150   MST: 800  || Gryz: 15-16       /
|                       || Alys: 14-15      /
| Weak: Energy          || Chaz: 15-16     /
| Res:  -               || Rika: 14-15    /
| Imm:  -               || Hahn: 14-15   /
|                       ||              /
```

This guy is pretty tough compared to what you have faced so far. In the
first round, have Alys use VORTEX, Chaz use CROSSCUT, Hahn use WAT, Gryz
use WAR CRY and Rika use DBLSLASH. This will inflict a fair amount of
damage and increase Gryz's ATK for the rounds to come. In the rounds that
follow, use the same attack strategy. Let Gryz just attack each round, and
Chaz use TSU if he runs out of CROSSCUT.

Juza only uses magic, so have Hahn or Rika heal when a character is hit by
a targeted spell. If Juza uses ZAN, CORROSION or FORCEFLASH (especially the
latter), it may be best to let both of them heal, and maybe even get Chaz
to lend a hand if necessary. Although Gryz has the most HP at this time,
give him priority over other characters as he will take the most damage
from Juza. If you are unlucky and one of your characters falls in this
battle, get a fast character to use the MOON-DEW and a slower one to follow
this up with GIRES or a DIMATE. This should restore them back to a decent
level of health.

If you keep the pressure on Juza, and heal when necessary, this battle
shouldn't last more than four or five rounds.
After you defeat Juza, a staircase will appear to the left. Heal up if you
need to (you're not out yet), then ascend the stairs. Go down and around to
the right, and take the next set of stairs up to the top floor. Remove all
of Alys' and Hahn's equipment (you'll see why in a little while), then head
up and approach the unusual-looking object to begin a cut-scene.

Rika identifies the being as Demi, the android you've been looking for.
Alys cuts her free, and then introduces herself. Demi is very grateful, and
uses her Medical Power to heal the party before telling them that she is
responsible for controlling Nurvus. While Gryz and Hahn are awed by her
human likeness, Alys asks if Demi can stop Nurvus from supplying energy to
the system. Demi begins to explain that she had already tried to do so,
when she is interrupted by an unseen voice. Zio appears in his menacing
way, and accuses the group of breaking into his property. Chaz suggests
that Zio looks at his own actions before judging others, although Zio
doesn't seem to see anything wrong with what he has done. He taunts Gryz
a little, before Alys points out that if Zio continues to do as he has
done then the whole of Motavia could be destroyed. Zio seems pleased with
this, pointing out that his god wants there to be no life in Algo, and then
he sees red. He makes a short speech, vowing to destroy them all in the
name of his god, Dark Force, and begins another battle.


```
 __________
```

| BOSS #4  \____________  ____________________


```
| Zio                   ||                    |
|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|| Recommended Level: | 
|  HP: N/A              ||                    |
| EXP: N/A    MST: N/A  || Gryz: N/A         /
|                       || Alys: N/A        /
| Weak: -               || Chaz: N/A       /
| Res:  -               || Rika: N/A      /
| Imm:  -               || Hahn: N/A     /
|                       ||              /
```

You will not win this fight, and you are not meant to. Before you get a
chance to do anything, Zio will use MAG.BARRIR, reducing any magical damage
you inflict to 1 (you won't even hit him with regular attacks).

The simplest way to get through the battle is to let everyone attack each
round (use Macro A if you haven't changed it). In the first round, Zio will
set his hands on fire (no effect), and do nothing in the second round. In
the round that follows he will summon NIGHTMARE, then use BLACK WAVE on
Chaz in the round after that. The battle ends abruptly with a cut-scene.
Alys jumps in front of the wave to protect Chaz, then Hahn and Rika suggest
they retreat. Chaz uses HINAS to escape, and they all appear outside Zio's
Fort. Rika attempts to use GIRES on Alys but it has no effect, so Hahn
decides that they should go back to his village. A RYUKA later, and the
party are back in Krup.

<a id="s6-2-5"></a>

### 6.2.5. New Transportation

Starting Party: Gryz , Alys , Chaz , Rika , Hahn
Starting Level: 15-16, 14-15, 15-16, 14-15, 14-15
The party meet Saya in Krup, and take Alys to a bed at the Inn. Her
condition has not improved. Chaz notes that Zio was unlike anything he has
ever fought, and Rika diagnoses that Alys seems to be possessed by an evil
force. Demi explains that Zio built his fort upon Nurvus, and Chaz realises
that Nurvus must be behind the barrier they couldn't cross before. Alys
then mentions that Rune may be able to help, pointing out that there is no
way they can get past Zio's magical barrier with what they have now. Rika
asks who Rune is, and Chaz replies with his opinion, reluctantly agreeing
that they may need his help after all. As Rune went off with Grandfather
Dorin, Gryz decides that they must have gone to a place called Ladea Tower,
located on a small island across the quicksand to the east. While Hahn and
Gryz try to work out how they will cross, Demi suggests that they can use
the Land Rover, an all-purpose, armour-plated car. Apparently, there should
be one located at the Machine Centre to the south. They decide to leave,
although Chaz asks Hahn to stay behind and look after Alys. Hahn isn't too
happy about the idea at first, but he agrees in the end. You are then free
to go.

> **Alys leaves the party**


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

> **Hahn leaves the party**


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

> **Demi joins the party (Level 12)**


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

Demi is an android, and is therefore knowledgable in the use of advanced
technology. This, coupled with her regenerative powers, makes her a very
useful ally. As Demi restores HP between battles, it is best to place her
at the front of the party, followed by Gryz, Chaz and then Rika.


```
Recommended       |   Demi   |   Gryz   |   Chaz   |   Rika   |
Equipment   |¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|
            |Head |HEAD-GEAR |CRMC-HELM |CRMC-HELM |GRPT-CROWN|
            |Right|IMPACTER  |STRUGGL-AX|LASR-SWORD|LASR-CLAW |
            |Left | /2-HAND  | /2-HAND  | /2-HAND  |SABER-CLAW|
            |Body |TITN-ARMOR|CRMC-MAIL |CRMC-MAIL |GRPT-SUIT |
```

Make your way downstairs and leave Krup. Don't bother staying at the Inn
unless you desperately need to, as you can heal for free in a moment.

Enemies around Krup: Crawler, Locusta, Mini Worm, MonsterFly, Sand Newt


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

Head south along the coast, continuing until you stop and view a metal
structure rise from the ground ahead. Chaz is shocked, and Demi says that
they are free to enter. Continue south and enter the Machine Centre.

There are no monsters in the Machine Centre, so simply walk up and take
the elevator to the floor below. Pick up the CONTROLKEY from the left side
of the passage and use the Regen Platform on the right to restore yourself
to full strength. When ready, continue down the passage and through the
door to a huge chamber.

Demi approaches the panel, using the control key to access the computer. As
she stands at the terminal she notes that there are many machines housed in
the centre, although most of them are quite old and will need repairs. Chaz
is impressed, and asks Demi if Zio caught her while she was trying to get
the system back under control. She concurs, but then goes on to state that
getting rid of Zio won't solve the problem. It seems that Zelan, the main
control system for Motavia's environment, is the source of the malfunctions
on the planet, but the fact that Zelan is an orbiting satellite makes this
fact a little useless at present. After this, a huge vehicle rolls into
view. A little while afterwards, the party are outside the Machine Centre
and in their very own Land Rover.

<a id="s6-2-6"></a>

> 🥉 **Gryz** — Recruit Gryz. _(RetroAchievements · 5 pts)_


### 6.2.6. Gryz Quakes in his Boots

Starting Party: Demi , Gryz , Chaz , Rika
Starting Level: 12   , 15-16, 15-16, 14-15
The Land Rover is a vehicle that can traverse quicksand and makes travel a
lot faster. It counts as an item in your inventory. While you are outside,
select LAND-ROVER from the item list to use the vehicle, and press the
cancel button to get out again.

Enemies in a vehicle on Motavia land: Forced Fly, GrassHound, DesrtLeach
Now that you have the Land Rover, the second job will be available from the
Hunters' Guild. It won't provide you with any experience points, but you
can earn a little cash. See '7.1.2. Tinkerbell's Dog' for more details.

Head north past Krup, turning right when you reach the entrance to Valley
Maze. Continue east until you reach the quicksand. Drive the Land Rover
northeast across the quicksand and then head a little north and into the
village of Monsen.

________


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\
Monsen  |Inn            |Per person     45 MST /
_______/|_______________|______________________/
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\
        |Tool Store     |MONOMATE       20 MST /
        |               |DIMATE        160 MST \
        |               |ANTIDOTE       10 MST /
        |               |CURE-PARAL    120 MST \
        |               |TELEPIPE      130 MST /
        |               |ESCAPIPE       70 MST \
        |_______________|______________________/
```

Head up and follow the path to the east side of the village. You will
notice a large crack in the ground surrounded by a fence to the south.
There is a sign blocking entry to the crack. It reads:
'Danger: No Trespassing Cracks In The Ground'

Speak to the man on the right, and he will tell you that Monsen has been
suffering from earthquakes recently. As if on cue, the ground then shakes
violently. Gryz gets into a panic, and Rika teases him for being afraid.
Demi supposes that the Plate System, to the north, must be the cause of
the problem, and Gryz proposes that they shut it down. This attracts the
attention of the villagers nearby, and they gather to thank the party for
their help. Although Chaz isn't entirely happy about it, he doesn't seem to
have much choice.

Rest at the Inn and stock up on any items you may require, then head out of
Monsen. It would be best to get Chaz and Gryz up to Level 16, Rika up to at
least Level 15 if you haven't already, and get Demi up to Level 13.

Enemies around Monsen: Caterpillr, Depcen, Fanbite, InfantWorm, Sand Worm


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

Be extremely wary of Sand Worms while on foot, as you are yet nowhere near
powerful enough to overcome one of these beasts. If you encounter any, my
advice is to flee.

Once you are prepared, spend a night in Monsen then head northeast around
the mountains to the Plate System. Save and enter.

<a id="s6-2-7"></a>

> 🥈 **Tectonic Tech** — Solve Plate System's earthquake malfunction. (Missed upon leaving Motavia.) _(RetroAchievements · 10 pts)_


### 6.2.7. A Tectonic Diversion

Starting Party: Demi , Gryz , Chaz , Rika
Starting Level: 13   , 16   , 16   , 15-16


```
 // DUNGEON #9  ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\
```

|/  Plate System           \_________________________________
   Enemies: Gunner Bit, Loader, Seeker, Slave, Worker Pod
  Treasure: REPAIR-KIT, CRMC-ARMOR, TITN-GEAR, PHONON (Skill),
            LASR-AXE, LASRBARRIR, LASR-KNIFE, STUN-SHOT
Head up the passage, and turn right at the junction. Head down the short
passage and pick up the REPAIR-KIT from the end. Ignore the passage leading
up as this is a dead end, and head all the way to the left along the
corridor. Go up and use the elevator.

Go left and then up the thin corridor, then go to the right side of the
large room you come to. Head along the passage to the right, then take the
upper path at the junction. Walk up to the upper left corner and procure
the CRMC-ARMOR. As noone else can use this, equip it to Demi. Go back down
and then take the junction below you, continuing to the bottom to get the
TITN-GEAR. Again, equip this to Demi. Head back up and then return to the
large room, Make your way across the room, take the passage on the left,
then head up and then right and take the elevator to the next floor.

Head down and then left at the junction. When you reach the left wall, go
down the passage, ignoring the path to the right, and then turn right at
the bottom. Descend in the elevator. Go left and then all the way up to
the top, then go a little to the right and open the chest.

Chaz states that the chest is full of weird machines, and Demi points out
that they are internal weapon units for androids. She asks for everyone to
look away, then the screen goes black. A few upgrade noises later, and Demi
is fully equipped with her new weapon, Phononmezer.

Demi acquires the PHONON Skill
Return to and use the elevator, the go back up to the passage until you
reach a path to your right. Follow this all the way to the right until you
hit the wall, then head down. Turn left at the bottom and descend to the
next floor in the elevator.

Head a little right and then all the way up to the top of the passage,
then go left. Turn down at the corner and pick up the LASR-KNIFE on the
right. Head over to the left of this area and collect the LASR-AXE. Make
sure you equip this to Gryz, as it is his best weapon so far. Now, go
right, down then right and pick up the LASRBARRIR. With all of these new
possessions, follow the bottom wall to the left and take the elevator down.

Head right, ignoring the junction above you, and continue to the end to get
the STUN-SHOT. Hand this to Demi, then return to the junction and walk up
the passage. Examine the panel on the top wall.

Demi accesses the panel and shuts down the controls for the Plate System.
This makes Gryz quite happy, but Demi points out that it hasn't solved the
problem. They still need to shut down Nurvus, and perhaps even Zelan.

Now you are done here, RYUKA, TELEPIPE or walk out of the Plate System, and
return to Monsen to recuperate.

<a id="s6-2-8"></a>

### 6.2.8. The Furthest Point East

Starting Party: Demi , Gryz , Chaz , Rika
Starting Level: 13-14, 16-17, 16-17, 16-17
After a good night's sleep, leave Monsen and get in your Land Rover. Head
northeast towards the Plate System, then continue past it to the east until
you reach a mountain range. From here, head south through the quicksand and
head into the village of Termi.

________


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\
Termi   |Inn            |Per person     50 MST \
_______/|_______________|______________________/
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\
        |Armour Store   |PSY-CROWN    2800 MST|  +13 DFS   +3 MTL         /
        |               |PSY-CIRCLT   1800 MST|   +3 DFS   +5 MTL         \
        |               |PSY-MAIL     7400 MST|  +35 DFS   +2 MTL         /
        |               |PSY-SHIELD   4600 MST|  +21 DFS   +1 MTL         \
        |_______________|_____________________|___________________________/
        |¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|                          _\
        |Bayamare       |ALIS-SWORD    500 MST|   +1 ATK           ___/¯¯
        |Gift Store     |PEROLYMATE     40 MST \       _______/¯¯¯¯
        |               |PENNANT       600 MST /¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
        |               |WOODCARVIN   3000 MST \
        |_______________|______________________/
```

Termi is a village steeped in legend, as it is the hometown of Alis, a
legendary heroine from two thousand years ago. Most of the inhabitants are
proud of this, and look after their village well.

By now, you are probably carrying a lot of excess equipment, so go to the
Armour Store and sell the TITNDAGGER, two TITNSLASHRs, SABER-CLAW, two
CRMC-KNIFEs, CRMC-SWORD, STRUGGL-AX, LASR-KNIFE, LASRSLASHR, IMPACTER,
CRMCSHIELD, two LASRBARRIRs, CIRCLET, GRPT-CROWN, HEAD-GEAR, TITN-MAIL,
GRPT-SUIT, CRMC-MAIL and the TITN-ARMOR to free up your inventory.

Next, unequip Rika's GRPT-CROWN and the three CRMC-MAILs and sell these to
the Armour Store as well. You may also have some other redundant equipment
that you won from enemies, so sell all of this too. This, in total, should
net you a tidy sum of at least 26000 Mesetas.

Using this new income, you shouldn't have too much trouble purchasing a
PSY-CROWN for Rika and three PSY-MAILs for Chaz, Gryz and Rika, and still
have made a profit of over 1000 Mesetas from your sales. You may also want
to sell any MONOMATEs and other old curative items that are cluttering up
your item list.


```
Recommended       |   Demi   |   Gryz   |   Chaz   |   Rika   |
Equipment   |¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|
            |Head |TITN-GEAR |CRMC-HELM |CRMC-HELM |PSY-CROWN |
            |Right|STUN-SHOT |LASR-AXE  |LASR-SWORD|LASR-CLAW |
            |Left | /2-HAND  | /2-HAND  | /2-HAND  |SABER-CLAW|
            |Body |CRMC-ARMOR|PSY-MAIL  |PSY-MAIL  |PSY-MAIL  |
```

Unfortunately, there isn't a Tool Store in Termi, so if you need to stock
up on any supplies you will need to teleport to another village. You really
only need a few DIMATEs, a couple of ANTIDOTEs and CURE-PARALs, and perhaps
a TELEPIPE and an ESCAPIPE just in case.

Once you are fully prepared, spend a night at the Inn to refresh the party,
then leave Termi. Chaz, Gryz and Rika should now be safely into Level 17,
and Demi should be at least Level 14. If they are not, spend a little time
in the area earning them some experience points until they are.

Rest at the Inn at Termi again if you need to, then get in the Land Rover
and head southwest towards the coast until you reach a large white tower.
This is Ladea Tower. Save your game, then enter.

<a id="s6-2-9"></a>

> 🥈 **Psychic Nullification** — Recover the Psycho Wand. _(RetroAchievements · 10 pts)_


### 6.2.9. Work for a Wizard

Starting Party: Demi , Gryz , Chaz , Rika
Starting Level: 14   , 17   , 17   , 17


```
 // DUNGEON #10 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\
```

|/  Ladea Tower            \_________________________________
   Enemies: Centaur, FlyScreamer, Haunt, Ripper, ShadowSabr
  Treasure: DIMATE, STAR-DEW, ESCAPIPE, FRADEMANTL, STAR-DEW
            1000 MST, PSYCO-WAND
 \
  \   Boss: Gy-Laguiah
   \______________________________

You are in a huge chamber whose sole feature is a staircase. Head up the
room until you find the stairs, then ascend them. Head through the thin
passage to the left and take the first turning above you. Walk to the end
to collect the DIMATE then go back to the passage.

Continue left until you reach the wall, then head up and take the junction
on the left. Keep walking down and to the right, then take the staircase up
to the next floor. Head around the path to the left, continuing upwards
past the alcove to the right, and collect the STAR-DEW from the top of the
passage. Now return back to the stairs and take them back down.

Head left and up to the junction, then return down and right to the area
below the first staircase. Continue along the right-hand corridor, ignoring
the passage above you and turn up along the passage at the end. Go right at
the junction and follow the path down and around to the left to take the
staircase at the end.

You will see Rune a little to the right, so go and talk to him. Rune teases
Chaz, but Chaz hasn't got time for games. He asks for Rune's help, and Rune
notices that Alys is missing. Chaz explains what has happened, and Rune
reassures him that everything will be fine once they get the Psycho-wand.
He goes on to say that the Psycho-wand is the only thing that can break
through Zio's magical barrier, and that he had come to Ladea Tower to get
it. Apparently, it is on the top level, so Rune agrees to help them deal
with Zio once they get it.

> **Rune rejoins the party**


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

As Rune is not so powerful compared to the rest of the party now, keep him
at the back of the party, as he is a useful character to keep alive.


```
Recommended       |   Demi   |   Gryz   |   Chaz   |   Rika   |   Rune   |
Equipment   |¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|
            |Head |TITN-GEAR |CRMC-HELM |CRMC-HELM |PSY-CROWN |PSY-CIRCLT|
            |Right|STUN-SHOT |LASR-AXE  |LASR-SWORD|LASR-CLAW |FORCE-CANE|
            |Left | /2-HAND  | /2-HAND  | /2-HAND  |SABER-CLAW| /2-HAND  |
            |Body |CRMC-ARMOR|PSY-MAIL  |PSY-MAIL  |PSY-MAIL  |PSY-ROBE  |
```

Follow the passage left and up, past the alcove on the left, and then head
left and down the thin corridor. Turn left at the corner and enter a small
room. Go through the passage on the left, then head up and around to the
right to pick up the ESCAPIPE. Return to the small room and take the
staircase to the next level.

Head all the way down the thin corridor below you and turn right at the
bottom. Continue left and up around the path, then take the stairs to your
left. Head left into a large chamber and retrieve the FRADEMANTL from the
centre of the room. Replace Rune's PSY-ROBE with this new armour, then go
down through the thin corridor to the left, turning left at the bottom and
then descending the stairs that follow.

Head left and then up and around to the right, and take the STAR-DEW and
1000 MST from the small alcove below you. Return back left and down to the
staircase, then go back along the right passage into the large room. Head
to the bottom of the room and take the staircase at the bottom.

The next floor is a lot more decorative. Before taking the steps above you,
fully heal your party. When you are ready, head up and approach the chest
surrounded by a blue shield. Chaz supposes that it is the Psycho-wand, so
Rune steps up and breaks the barrier. At that moment, one of Zio's servants
appears, obviously having been waiting for the Psycho-wand to be released.
The party are not going to let the monster take the wand, so battle begins.


```
 __________
```

| BOSS #5  \____________  ____________________


```
| Gy-Laguiah            ||                    |
|¯¯¯��¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|| Recommended Level: | 
|  HP: 2580             ||                    |
| EXP: 10000  MST: 1224 || Demi: 14-15       /
|                       || Gryz: 17-18      /
| Weak: Water,Engy,Lght || Chaz: 17-18     /
| Res:  Fire            || Rika: 17-18    /
| Imm:  -               || Rune: 20      /
|                       ||              /
```

Not a particularly difficult opponent, as both of its attacks only affect
one character. In the first round, have Chaz use GITHU (if he is not Level
17 yet, which he should be, use CROSSCUT), Gryz use WAR CRY, Rika use SANER
(to ensure that Gy-Laguiah acts last in the round), Demi use her one round
of PHONON, and Rune use GIWAT.

In the subsequent rounds, have Chaz continue to use GITHU or CROSSCUT, let
Gryz just attack, get Rika to heal whoever was attacked in the round before
(unless it was Demi), get Demi to just attack, and keep Rune using GIWAT.
If Demi is attacked, have her use RECOVER in the following round. If any of
your party fall (due to a critical strike), let Demi use MEDIC PW and
follow this up with a curative Technique.

If you keep on top of things, there shouldn't be a problem in this battle,
and it should be over in about five to seven rounds.
Walk up and procure the PSYCO-WAND to begin a cut-scene.

They have the Psycho-wand, and Gryz is confident that nothing can stop them 
now. Suddenly, Rune and Rika have a strange feeling. Rune tells Chaz that
they must go to Krup immediately. A split second later, and they're there.

<a id="s6-2-10"></a>

### 6.2.10. Dearly Departed

Starting Party: Chaz , Gryz , Rika , Demi , Rune
Starting Level: 17-18, 17-18, 17-18, 14-15, 20
The party enter Alys' room at the Inn, and Hahn informs Chaz that Alys'
condition has worsened. A cut-scene then begins.

Alys doesn't look too good. Chaz implores Rune to help her, but he cannot.
Rune explains that the 'Black Energy Wave' contains an evil power created
by something more than just Zio, and that it is beyond his powers to cure.
Alys tries to speak, asking Rune to take care of Chaz, and then tells Chaz
to come closer so that she may take one last look at him. Alys tells him
that from now on he must carve his own destiny, and with her dying breath
Alys thanks Chaz. Rika begins to cry. A short while later, a funeral is
held for Alys, attended by her friends.

That evening, Chaz is looking up at the stars alone, when Rune comes out to
talk to him. Chaz explains that, before he met Alys, he was living in a far
off country where he did some pretty bad things. When he became a hunter,
he was finally able to earn some money and live a good life. With Alys
gone, Chaz doesn't know what to do. He wants to avenge her death, but he
wouldn't understand why he was fighting anymore. Rune chastises Chaz,
asking if Chaz really thinks that Alys was only fighting for money. He
tells Chaz to think about it, then Rune returns indoors.

Rika comes outside to see Chaz, and tells him how glad she has been since
leaving the Bio-Plant. She learned a lot from Seed, but explains there's
a big difference between studying and experiencing. Chaz understands, and
puts his arm around Rika as they both look up at the stars.

The next day, Hahn tells the others that he is going to return to the
Academy and try to convince them to come up with a plan of action. Chaz
agrees and wishes him luck, then Hahn leaves. The rest of the party decide
to get going too.

Now that you can control the party again, your next destination is Nurvus.
Since you haven't had the chance yet, equip your new PSYCO-WAND to Rune.
You are already fully healed from your journey through Ladea Tower, so
teleport to Kadary. Chaz, Gryz and Rika should all be at least Level 18,
and Demi should be at least Level 15 by now. Rune may also have reached
Level 21. If not, try to get the characters up to these Levels before
heading into the next dungeon.

When you are fully prepared, save and enter Zio's Fort. Examine the
barrier just up from the entrance, and Rune will approach it. Using the
Psycho-wand, Rune breaks the seal, and Demi tells the group that below them
is Nurvus, the central control system. Chaz asks if Zio is down there, and

Rune reminds him that their first priority is shutting down Nurvus. When
you regain control, head up and descend the staircase.

<a id="s6-2-11"></a>

### 6.2.11. An Act of Nurves

Starting Party: Chaz , Gryz , Rika , Demi , Rune
Starting Level: 18-19, 18-19, 18-19, 15-16, 20-21


```
 // DUNGEON #11 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\
```

|/  Nurvus                 \_________________________________
   Enemies: Balduel, Blauzen, Centaur, FloatMine, Greneris,
            Tarantella, TechMaster, Tower, Zios Guard
  Treasure: WAVE-SHOT, REPAIR-KIT, CRMC-GEAR, SPACEDARMR,
            PLSM-CLAW
 \
  \   Boss: Zio
   \______________________________

This is the largest and most difficult dungeon you have faced so far. You
may get dangerously low on HP and TP, so you may need to use HINAS or an
ESCAPIPE on occasion to rest up at Kadary before venturing back in.

You start in a green antechamber. Head up through the door and notice the
usual hi-tech décor. Continue along the passage and examine the panel at
the junction. Rika suggests Demi sends an interrupt command from there,
but Demi points out that the system isn't accepting any commands from the
outside. Apparently, they're going to have to get into its nucleus.

Turn left and head around and up through the doorway. Go up to the end of
this small passage and collect the WAVE-SHOT. Equip this new firearm to
Demi, replacing her STUN-SHOT in the process. Return back to the computer
terminal and take the right path, then head through the door at the top.
Follow the corridor upwards, turning left at the top, then take the top
path at the next junction and follow it to the elevator. Take it.

Head down the passage and turn left at the corner. Walk left until the end
then take the path downwards at the junction. Head along the walkway and
retrieve the REPAIR-KIT at the bottom. Return up to the junction then go
up and descend in the elevator.

Take the elevator immediately to the left, then go down through the short
passage. Turn a little right then continue down the long platform, and
pick up the CRMC-GEAR from the end. Equip this new head protection to Demi,
then go back up and around to the doorway. Go through and take the elevator
back up to the level above. Go right then down, and follow the path near
the right-hand wall all the way to the bottom. Turn left and head down at
the junction, then use the elevator to the left.

Head down and the right, and go through the doorway on the upper wall.
Cross the bridge that follows, then go right and then upwards at the next
corner, following the line on the floor until you reach another walkway.
Continue up this path until you are back in a corridor, then head up at the
following junction. Take the elevator to the floor below.

There will be an elevator to the right, but ignore it for the time being.
Instead, head down and aroung to the left, then take the left passage at
the junction. Keep going left and then turn up at the corner to enter a
small room. The chest on the left is empty, so open the one on the right to
obtain the SPACEDARMR, which should be equipped to Demi. Go back down, then
right and up towards the elevators, and then enter the one on the right
that you ignored earlier.

Go down through the short passageway, then head down and around to the left 
and continue all the way down the long platform that follows. When you
enter a small area with a door on the left and an elevator just below and
to the right, head left and go through the door. Walk across the bridge
and out into a small area, where a walk around to the left will take you to
a PLSM-CLAW. Equip this to Rika alongside her LASR-CLAW and then go back
around and cross back over the bridge. Once you have returned, head down
and take the elevator to the right.

Head down and around to the left, then follow the passage all the way to
the end. If Chaz, Gryz and Rika are not at least Level 19 (preferably Level
20), Demi is not at Level 16 or 17, and Rune is not safely up to a minimum
of Level 21 yet, spend a little time in this corridor until they are. It
would also be a good idea to use HINAS or an ESCAPIPE to get out and
return to Kadary to fully refresh the party, then head all the way back
down to this passageway a little better prepared.

Once all the characters are at the right Level and are completely healed,
enter the doorway to the left of the corridor to find yourself in the main
control centre of Nurvus. Set up the following Macro, in the order given:
Rune:  Use Item  - PSYCO-WAND
Gryz:  Skill     - WAR CRY
Demi:  Skill     - BARRIER
Rika:  Technique - DEBAN
Chaz:  Skill     - CROSSCUT
Head up the walkway towards the main computer terminal, just before which
point the party will automatically stop and Zio will appear.

Zio seems to be a little impressed by your arrival, but informs you that
you shall be going no further. He calls upon his god for power, then the
true battle with Zio begins.


```
 __________
```

| BOSS #6  \____________  ____________________


```
| Zio                   ||                    |
|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|| Recommended Level: | 
|  HP: 2889             ||                    |
| EXP: 25999  MST: 1    || Demi: 16-17       /
|                       || Gryz: 19-20      /
| Weak: Energy,Light    || Chaz: 19-20     /
| Res:  Water           || Rika: 19-20    /
| Imm:  -               || Rune: 21-22   /
|                       ||              /
```

As before, Zio will set up his MAG.BARRIR at the very beginning of combat,
nullifying all of your attacks. However, this time you have a trick up your
sleeve. Go to the Macro menu and select the Macro you made above. In the
first round that follows, Zio will summon NIGHTMARE, Rune will cancel the
magical barrier with the PSYCO-WAND, Gryz will enhance his ATK, Demi will
create your own barrier, Rika will further amplify this by increasing the
party's DFS, and Chaz will start the ball rolling with an attack.

From this point Zio will begin his offensive. His arsenal includes Hewn,
Corrosion, Black Wave, and a nameless red energy beam. The first two of
these inflict damage on all the characters (although little on Rune), and
Black Wave and the red beam deal a lot of damage to one character.

In the second round, let Chaz use CROSSCUT again, have Gryz attack, get
Rika to use SANER to make sure everyone gets to act before Zio, have Demi
use her PHONON, and let Rune use GIFOI. In the following rounds, Chaz
should continue using CROSSCUT (or GITHU if he runs out), Gryz should
attack constantly, Rika should use GIRES, Demi should attack, and Rune
should keep on firing GIFOI.

Get Rika to heal characters low on HP, taking into account Zio only uses
magic and that Gryz has very poor magic defence and Rune's magic defence is
very good. Always use Demi's RECOVER Skill if her HP gets low, and in dire
circumstances it may be a good idea to use some DIMATEs and let Chaz do
some healing, or even use Demi's MEDIC PW or a STAR-DEW. Whatever happens,
try to keep your characters conscious. Losing a character means that in the
following round both they and the character that revives them lose a turn.

If you watch your health and keep bearing down on Zio, there's no reason
for the battle to last more than eight to ten rounds.
A cut-scene follows the battle that begins with the demise of Zio. He is
confused by this as he was under the impression that he was immortal, but
it seems that Dark Force has abandoned him. Gryz is delighted, and Chaz
thinks about Alys.

<a id="s6-2-12"></a>

### 6.2.12. Upward Mobility

Starting Party: Chaz , Gryz , Rika , Rune , Demi
Starting Level: 19-20, 19-20, 19-20, 21-22, 16-17
Demi informs the party that they she won't be able to shut down Nurvus by
normal means, and that she must connect to it directly to access it. She
bids farwell to the group, and then accesses Nurvus. A few seconds later
and the operation is a success, and all of the control systems on Motavia
have been stopped. She points out, however, that without the systems
operational Motavia will soon become uninhabitable and barren, and so all
of the controls must be sorted out individually and reset. Rika then points
out that in order to do that something must first be done about Zelan, the
artificial satellite that is sending abnormal signals. She suggests that
they go to Zelan, and Chaz concurs. Gryz then notes that Zelan is in outer
space, a location that may be quite difficult to reach. This doesn't really
pose a problem, as Demi informas them that Nurvus is equipped with a
shuttle. She tells the group that she cannot go with them, but that they
should seek her master, Wren, who is aboard the satellite. Demi then wishes
them the best of luck, and they depart.

The next thing you see is a spaceport rising from the sand a little to the
northwest of Zio's Fort. A bright, shiny shuttle glints in the sun, and
the party marvel at it for a while. But one of them won't be going. Gryz
can't leave his little sister, and apologises to Chaz, who understands.
You'll also notice that Zio's Fort has disappeared.

> **Gryz leaves the party**


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

> **Demi leaves the party**


```
Recommended       |   Chaz   |   Rika   |   Rune   |
Equipment   |¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|
            |Head |CRMC-HELM |PSY-CROWN |PSY-CIRCLT|
            |Right|LASR-SWORD|PLSM-CLAW |PSYCO-WAND|
            |Left | /2-HAND  |LASR-CLAW | /2-HAND  |
            |Body |PSY-MAIL  |PSY-MAIL  |FRADEMANTL|
```

Two new jobs have now become available at the Hunters' Guild. It would be
best to do them now as you won't be coming back to Motavia for a while. See
'7.1.3. The Missing Student' and '7.1.4. Fissure of Fear' for more details.

Head north and enter the Spaceport. Use one of the Regen Platforms that are
to the left and right of the entrance, then head up the passage and go
through the door.

A map of the Algo star system appears, and a single destination is shown at
the right-hand side of the screen: Zelan. Select it to begin the launch.
Watch the scene that follows and land at the artificial satellite.

<a id="s6-2-13"></a>

> 🥈 **Dark Satellite** — Resolve Kuran's communications problem. _(RetroAchievements · 10 pts)_


### 6.2.13. Artificial Satellite

Starting Party: Chaz , Rika , Rune
Starting Level: 19-20, 19-20, 21-22
Head up the corridor and ascend in the elevator at the top. Turn left and
follow the short passage into a room. Collect the PLSM-SWORD, PLSM-CLAW and
PLSMDAGGER, then head back to the right, around the central column and
through the next passage to acquire the PLSM-FIELD, PULSE-LASR and the
CANCELLER. Equip the PLSM-SWORD to Chaz, and the PLSM-CLAW to Rika to
complete her set. The other items have little use right now.

Head back to the left and then around and up the corridor above the
elevator. Keep going until you reach a tall silver-clothed person. This is
Wren, so talk to him and begin the next cut-scene.

Wren introduces himself to the party. He then goes on to explain that Zelan
controls the environmental systems for all the planets in Algo, and that he
manages the system. He then asks Rika who the rest of the party are. She
introduces Chaz and Rune, telling him they are great friends, but Chaz
seems to disagree with that remark. Rika goes on to say that Demi informed
them that the problem with Motavia's systems was supposed to have been
caused by Zelan. Wren then explains that Zelan is not behind the systems
running out of control, but that Zelan has no control at all. It seems that
Kuran, the support satellite to Zelan, has somehow usurped Zelan's control
and is sending Motavia's systems the abnormal commands. The fact that Zelan
was at the top of the command chain led Demi to believe that it was the
cause, as Zelan's communications had been down for the last six months.
Chaz then suggests they go to Kuran, and Wren asks if he may accompany the
party, as there is nothing that he can do from Zelan. Rika vouches for
Wren, telling Chaz that Wren and Seed were her teachers. After another
little argument between Chaz and Rune, the party decide to leave.

> **Wren joins the party (Level 20)**


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

This new android has a high DFS and a huge quantity of HP, so make sure to
put him right at the top of the marching order, followed by Chaz, then Rika
and then Rune as before.


```
Recommended       |   Wren   |   Chaz   |   Rika   |   Rune   |
Equipment   |¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|
            |Head |CRMC-GEAR |CRMC-HELM |PSY-CROWN |PSY-CIRCLT|
            |Right|PSLM-RIFLE|PLSM-SWORD|PLSM-CLAW |PSYCO-WAND|
            |Left | /2-HAND  | /2-HAND  |PLSM-CLAW | /2-HAND  |
            |Body |SPACEDARMR|PSY-MAIL  |PSY-MAIL  |FRADEMANTL|
```

Head back down and around the central column to take the elevator to the
floor below. From here, head all the way down the passage and out onto the
shuttle again. Kuran was originally in Stealth Mode, making it undetectable
to radar, but using the CANCELLER they found earlier the party are able to
disable the Stealth Mode and locate Kuran. Select Kuran as the destination,
and the shuttle departs. A cut-scene then follows.

Chaz notices something is wrong, and then an alarm sounds. Wren reports
that there is an unidentified energy reaction coming from the engine room,
so the party decide to investigate. A short while later, and they discover
an uninvited guest playing around with the controls. It didn't expect to be
found out so soon, but it decides that it doesn't matter whether it
sabotages the engines or kills the party immediately, so long as they don't
get to Kuran. The Chaos Sorcerer then initiates a battle.


```
 __________
```

| BOSS #7  \____________  ____________________


```
| ChaosSorcr            ||                    |
|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|| Recommended Level: | 
|  HP: 460              ||                    |
| EXP: 18380  MST: 1200 || Wren: 20          /
|                       || Chaz: 19-20      /
| Weak: Energy          || Rika: 19-20     /
| Res:  -               || Rune: 21-22    /
| Imm:  -               ||               /
|                       ||              /
```

A break in the pattern of increasing boss difficulty, the ChaosSorcr is
exceptionally easy to defeat. The ChaosSorcr will either use a laser beam
attack, Flaeli, Hewn or ShadowBind (a target-all Skill that has a small
chance of reducing the Agility of each character). Have all the characters
use their standard attacks, and the ChaosSorcr will go down in the second
round, probably only getting the chance to act once in the entire battle.
The saboteur is dead, but it seems he did his work well. The ship is in
trouble, and Wren points out that they are off their intended flight-path.
He suggests that they make a crash landing on Dezolis, and asks the party
for their opinion. Chaz replies, rather alarmingly, that they don't have a
choice, and Wren makes preparations to crash. Rika seems to be enjoying
herself, and Chaz gets panicky, asking if she's thinking straight. Wren and
Rune tell Chaz to calm down, but Chaz can't understand how everyone can be
so relaxed about it all. The ship begins to descend.

<a id="s6-3"></a>

## 6.3. Cold New World

<a id="s6-3-1"></a>

### 6.3.1. Crash Landing

Starting Party: Wren , Chaz , Rika , Rune
Starting Level: 20   , 20-21, 20-21, 21-22
A short introduction to the planet of Dezolis begins this next section of
the game, after which a scene follows where you see the shuttle crashing
onto the snowy surface. The door opens and the party steps out, and Chaz
comments on their flamboyant landing. A green-faced old man approaches,
and jokes that it is raining machines. He seems to be a Dezolisian, and he
asks who they are, pointing out that they've destroyed his temple. Chaz
apologizes, and the Dezolisian notices his unusual-looking companions, Rika
and Wren. He figures they're from Motavia, then makes a joke about how they
came to arrive. Rika seems to find him quite amusing. Chaz doesn't share
her humour. Wren then approaches and informs them that the shuttle is
beyond repair. Rika asks the old man, who tells her that his name is Raja,
if there is anywhere they can fix the ship. He tells her there isn't, but
goes on to say that there is another space ship on the planet. Chaz asks
where, but Raja only agrees to say if they allow him to accompany them.
Chaz doesn't seem to keen on the idea, but Rika thinks he is interesting.
Rune makes the valid point that they have no choice, so they accept his
proposal. Raja then explains that Parmanians landed on Dezolis many years
ago, and that their spaceship is still in Tyler, the town of their
descendants, a short distance to the northwest. They then decide to leave.

> **Raja joins the party (Level 25)**


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

Raja is a weak character like Rune, so leave him at the back of the party
where he starts. Keep the rest of the party in the same order they were.
Before going anywhere, equip the PULSE-LASR to Wren. It is less powerful
than his LASR-RIFLE but it damages all enemies in one attack.


```
Recommended       |   Wren   |   Chaz   |   Rika   |   Rune   |   Raja   |
Equipment   |¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|
            |Head |CRMC-GEAR |CRMC-HELM |PSY-CROWN |PSY-CIRCLT|SILVCIRCLT|
            |Right|PULSE-LASR|PLSM-SWORD|PLSM-CLAW |PSYCO-WAND|SILV-ROD  |
            |Left | /2-HAND  | /2-HAND  |PLSM-CLAW | /2-HAND  | /2-HAND  |
            |Body |SPACEDARMR|PSY-MAIL  |PSY-MAIL  |FRADEMANTL|SILV-MANTL|
```

Walk out of Raja's Temple, and you'll find yourself outside in the middle
of a massive snowstorm. A short conversation will then follow that begins
with Chaz commenting on the weather. Raja tells them that the storm has
been going on for three months, and even though Dezolis has a cold climate
he has never seen it so bad in all his life. Wren suggests that it must be
the Dezolisian climate control centre, but Raja thinks otherwise. He talks
of a place called the Garuberk Tower, which he thinks is responsible for
the snowstorm. He cracks another joke that only Rika finds funny, and then
you are given control again. Your next destination is Ryuon, so save and
and either get into your Land Rover or stay on foot, then head north.

Enemies between Raja's Temple and Ryuon: Dezo Owl, Helex, Mistralgec,


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯  Rajago, Snow Mole
```

Enemies in a vehicle on Dezolis: Lw-Addmer, Owltalon, ProtectBit
After a short distance you should find the village of Ryuon. Enter it.

<a id="s6-3-2"></a>

### 6.3.2. Tales of Tyler

Starting Party: Wren , Chaz , Rika , Rune , Raja
Starting Level: 20   , 20-21, 20-21, 21-22, 25


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\
Ryuon   |Inn            |Per person    100 MST /
_______/|_______________|______________________/
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\
        |Tool Store     |MONOMATE       20 MST /
        |               |DIMATE        160 MST \
        |               |ANTIDOTE       10 MST /
        |               |CURE-PARAL    120 MST \
        |               |TELEPIPE      130 MST /
        |               |ESCAPIPE       70 MST \
        |_______________|______________________/
        |¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\
        |Weapon Store   |FORCE-CANE   2500 MST|  +26 ATK                  /
        |               |SILV-ROD     2700 MST|  +18 ATK   +2 MTL         \
        |_______________|_____________________|___________________________/
        |¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\
        |Armour Store   |SILV-MANTL   7300 MST|  +49 DFS   +3 MTL         /
        |               |SILVCIRCLT   3000 MST|  +10 DFS   +3 MTL         \
        |_______________|_____________________|___________________________/
```

There are some weapons and armour here, but none of it is worth buying as
it will all be available with much more equipment at the next town.
Instead, head over to the building directly north of the Inn to the right,
and enter. You'll notice the same music that played when you first met
Grandfather Dorin all the way back in Tonoe. This is not surprising, as you
are about to meet his Dezolisian counter-part, whose name is Gyuna. Go to
the bar and speak to Gyuna. He will see you are friends of Raja, and will
answer some questions for you. Reply 'no' to knowledge about the snowstorm,
the Garuberk Tower and Raja, but reply 'yes' to finding out about the
whereabouts of the space ship. He will tell you that the ship will be found
underground in Tyler, and that examining the grave will open up the path.

With this unusual information, head out of the building and buy whatever
supplies you may need. Dezolis is home to some tough enemies, so it might
be a good idea to stock up a little more than usual. Rest at the Inn to
recover the party, then leave Ryuon.

Continue north and then head around the mountains to the west and you
should soon reach Tyler. Walk on in.

________


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\
Tyler   |Inn            |Per person    110 MST /
_______/|_______________|______________________/
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\
        |Tool Store     |MONOMATE       20 MST /
        |               |DIMATE        160 MST \
        |               |ANTIDOTE       10 MST /
        |               |CURE-PARAL    120 MST \
        |               |TELEPIPE      130 MST /
        |               |ESCAPIPE       70 MST \
        |_______________|______________________/
        |¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\
        |Weapon Store   |CRMC-SWORD   3600 MST|  +34 ATK   +7 DFS         /
        |               |CRMC-KNIFE   1600 MST|  +14 ATK                  \
        |               |SILV-ROD     2700 MST|  +18 ATK   +2 MTL         /
        |               |SILV-MAIL   13200 MST|  +49 DFS                  \
        |               |SILV-MANTL   7300 MST|  +49 DFS   +3 MTL         /
        |               |SILVSHIELD   7200 MST|  +25 DFS                  \
        |_______________|_____________________|___________________________/
        |¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\
        |Armour Store   |SILVCIRCLT   3000 MST|  +10 DFS   +3 MTL         /
        |               |SILV-HELM    3800 MST|  +14 DFS   +2 MTL         \
        |               |SILV-CROWN   5000 MST|  +16 DFS                  \
        |_______________|_____________________|___________________________/
```

First things first, sell all the old equipment you can. Also, sell any old
curative items that have no real use any more. Once you have done this,
you need to buy some new equipment. Purchase two SILV-MAILs for Chaz and
Rika, a SILV-MANTL and a SILV-CIRCLT for Rune, a SILV-HELM for Chaz, a
SILV-CROWN for Rika, and four SILVSHIELDs (two each for Rune and Raja).
This shopping bill will come to 74300 Mesetas, which you may find a little
more than you can afford. If so, buy as much as you can (leaving the
SILVSHIELDs till last), then equip the items and rest at the Inn.

Just to the north of the entrance to Tyler, head west and then ascend the
short flight of steps to the north. In the centre of this little hill is a
headstone. Examine this.

"Here lies the great leader Tyler...
 Touch us... Listen to our voice...
 Entrust that body to us..."

It is Tyler's grave, so Chaz inspects the stone as Gyuna suggested. While
examining the inscription again the plate moves, so Chaz pushes it and the
gravestone splits apart revealing a staircase below. Save, then descend.

<a id="s6-3-3"></a>

> 🥉 **This Luster! This Massiveness!** — Discover the Land Rover. _(RetroAchievements · 3 pts)_
> 🥉 **Space Sledding** — Discover the Landale. _(RetroAchievements · 3 pts)_
> 🥉 **Algo Legend** — Inspect the Alis Landale statue. _(RetroAchievements · 2 pts)_


### 6.3.3. Leaving in the Landale

Starting Party: Wren , Chaz , Rika , Rune , Raja
Starting Level: 20   , 20-21, 20-21, 21-22, 25


```
 // DUNGEON #12 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\
```

|/  Hanger                 \_________________________________
   Enemies: Gerotlux, Helex, Snow Slug
  Treasure: DIMATE, ZIRC-GEAR
This is a relatively short dungeon for a change. Head down and then left at
the corner, then continue left by the top wall until you come to a small
chamber at the end. Pick up the DIMATE just to the left of the pool, then
go back to the right and head downwards a little way. Head through the
passage to the right and follow it until the end to acquire the ZIRC-GEAR.
Equip this to Wren, then return to the main passageway. Continue heading
down until you reach the bottom wall, then go left and down around the
corner that follows. Continue down and exit through the door at the bottom.

You have found the space ship, and Chaz is quite impressed. Rune takes a
closer look and realises that it is called the Landale. Raja tries to make
a funny remark, but Chaz ignores him and asks Wren about its condition.
Wren replies that it has been preserved almost perfectly, and that it will
only take a little maintenance to be up and running. Chaz tells Wren to
prepare for take-off, and the next thing you see is a Spaceport (identical
to the one on Motavia) rise from the ground just to the southwest of Tyler.

Take the party to the Spaceport and use one of the Regen Platforms, then
check the party's status. You ideally want everyone to be up to at least
Level 22 before taking the Landale to Kuran, so spend some time in the area
around Tyler to acquire enough EXP to achieve this. If you want more of a
challenge and more EXP you can head through the mountains north of Tyler.
The enemies there are more powerful.

Enemies in the area north of Tyler: Biter Fly, Gerotlux, Helex, Red Mole,
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯  Skytiara, Snow Slug, Snow Worm

Once everyone is up to a minimum of Level 22 and you have made sure that
they are all equipped with the correct gear, you are almost ready to leave.


```
Recommended       |   Wren   |   Chaz   |   Rika   |   Rune   |   Raja   |
Equipment   |¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|
            |Head |ZIRC-GEAR |SILV-HELM |SILV-CROWN|SILVCIRCLT|SILVCIRCLT|
            |Right|PULSE-LASR|PLSM-SWORD|PLSM-CLAW |SILVSHIELD|SILVSHIELD|
            |Left | /2-HAND  | /2-HAND  |PLSM-CLAW |SILVSHIELD|SILVSHIELD|
            |Body |SPACEDARMR|SILV-MAIL |SILV-MAIL |SILV-MANTL|SILV-MANTL|
```

Get a good night's rest at the Inn in Tyler, and buy a good supply of items
from the Tool Store. You'll want to have at least five or six DIMATEs and
an ESCAPIPE just in case. Don't bother getting any ANTIDOTEs or CURE-PARALs
as you won't need them on Kuran.

When you are completely set, head into the Spaceport, use a Regen Platform,
then head up and enter the Landale. Select Kuran from the destination list
on the right, and watch your new spaceship fly to the next dungeon.

<a id="s6-3-4"></a>

### 6.3.4. Malign Manifestation

Starting Party: Wren , Chaz , Rika , Rune , Raja
Starting Level: 22   , 22-23, 23-24, 23-24, 25-26


```
 // DUNGEON #13 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\
```

|/  Kuran                  \_________________________________
   Enemies: CommndBall, C-Ray Tube, FloatMine, Piercer,
            Sat.Minion, Siren386
  Treasure: HIJAMMER (Skill), REPAIR-KIT, ZIRCOARMER, 3000 MST,
            REPAIR-KIT, NAPALMSHOT
 \
  \   Boss: Dark Force
   \______________________________

After the short dialogue, head up the passageway and take the elevator at
the top to the floor above. Follow the platform to the left and take the
door around the corner. Go all the way along the corridor to the left and
then head up and open the chest in the small room. Chaz asks what's in
there, and Wren replies it is an internal weapon unit for androids. He
surmises that it is a Hyper-Jammer, a device that temporarily scrambles
the AI of machines using electromagnetic waves. Wren then installs it.

Wren acquires the HIJAMMER Skill
Go back down and head around the wall section to the passage below the
elevator. Walk down and pick up the REPAIR-KIT, then return to the elevator
and take it down to the floor below. Go right, up and then right along the
long corridor, taking the door on the bottom wall at the end. Continue
right, ignoring the path below you, and head around the bend in the path
to reach another junction. Here, follow the line leading down and go
through the door at the bottom. Now go down, around the central column to
either the left or right, and ascend in the elevator.

Go left or right, then up around the elevator shaft and continue up along
the walkway. Turn left at the corner and keep going to the next corner
leading upwards. Follow the walkway all the way to the top then head right
and use the elevator in the wall above you.

Head left, down, left and then down again, and retrieve the ZIRCOARMER from
the small alcove to the left. Replace Wren's SPACEDARMR with this new
hardware, then return back up to the elevator. Continue right, down, right
and then all the way down past the open chest on the right. Head a little
to the left and the go down and through the door on the right.

Follow the passage all the way to the right, ignoring the elevator for the
moment, and then head up at the junction at the end. Go around into a small
room and collect the 3000 MST, then return to the junction and head down to
procure another REPAIR-KIT. Go back up to the junction again and go back
left along the corridor to the elevator you ignored just now. Take it.

Head right in the next passageway, and keep going along it, turning down
and then right at the end. Pick up the NAPALMSHOT, but don't equip it to
Wren just yet. His PULSE-LASR is far more useful at the moment. Go back up
and all the way along the corridor to the left, and then take the door in
the bottom wall opposite the elevator. Go down and then left, ignoring the
path below you, and then head up at the next corner. Continue up this
platform, shimmying left on the way, and turn left when you reach the top.
There are a few paths branching off here, but ignore all of them and enter
the elevator instead.

Go a little down and then either left or right along the walkway, and keep
going down and then around into the elevator to the floor below. Go around
to the left or the right and then up, ignoring the side branches, and
follow the line at the top of the room. The party will then stop and have
a short conversation. Chaz realises that they are in the main control
centre, and Wren says that he will look for the cause of the malfunction.
At that moment, however, Rika notices something in the shadows ahead.

Make sure all of the characters are up to at least Level 24. This will
likely mean that Chaz and Rune should be Level 25, Rika should be Level 26,
Wren should be Level 24 and Raja should be Level 27. If they are not, spend
a little time in Kuran (not the area you are currently in as there are no
enemies here), and build up your characters until they are. It may also be
a good idea to HINAS or ESCAPIPE out, return to Motavia or Dezolis
Spaceport, and use a Regen Platform to restore your party, then go back
through Kuran until you are back into this area.

Get Raja to heal everyone (except Wren who can heal himself by walking or
using RECOVER), and equip the NAPALMSHOT to Wren. Once you are completely
prepared, head up and approach the strange object covering the computer
terminal. The party stops just before, and Rika feels a great sense of
oppression. Rune recognizes the creature as Dark Force, the being that Zio
had revered as a god. Wren, in his unemotional way, diagnoses that Dark
Force seems to be the cause of the problem, and that they must remove it.
Rune remarks that it may be easier said than done, but Chaz has no fear.
He tells the party to go for it, and so a battle begins.


```
 __________
```

| BOSS #8  \____________  ____________________


```
| Dark Force            ||                    |
|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|| Recommended Level: | 
|  HP: 4540             ||                    |
| EXP: 32600  MST: 1    || Wren: 24          /
|                       || Chaz: 25         /
| Weak: Energy,Light    || Rika: 26-27     /
| Res:  Force           || Rune: 25       /
| Imm:  -               || Raja: 27      /
|                       ||              /
```

Dark Force is, without a doubt, the most powerful enemy you will have faced
yet, and it's appearance certainly hints at this. However, if you are smart
in this battle you may find that it is easier than the fight with Zio.

In the first round, let Chaz use GITHU, Rika use SANER, Rune use NAFOI (or
NAWAT if he is Level 26), Wren use BARRIER and Raja use BLESSING. This
should inflict a decent 400-500 HP of damage on Dark Force, and also
prepare you for the rounds to come.

Dark Force will use either FLARE SHOT (an extremely powerful laser attack
that targets one character), PHONONMASR or BURSTROC (both of which are
fairly damaging hit-all spells).

In the rounds that follow, keep Chaz using GITHU, let Rika use DBLSLASH,
have Rune continue to use NAFOI or NAWAT, continue attacking with Wren,
and get Raja to maintain the party with healing Techniques.

If Dark Force uses FLARE SHOT in the previous round, get Raja to use
GIRES on the victim (or get Wren to use RECOVER if he was hit). If Dark
Force uses one of his party attacks, have Raja use SAR. In the unfortunate
event that a character should fall, have a fast character use REVER or a
MOON-DEW (if you have any) and get a slow character to heal them with GIRES
or a DIMATE. If Wren is the flatlined character, use a REPAIR-KIT.

If you are in a situation where Wren is using RECOVER to heal and everyone
else is at maximum HP, let Raja throw out a ST. FIRE, as this Skill hurts
Dark Force a lot.

Use this strategy, keeping your party's HP levels high and continually
pummelling your opponent, and Dark Force should crumble to dust after a
mere six or seven rounds.
Dark Force explodes in a display of light. Chaz tells Wren to get Kuran
back to normal, and Wren efficienly obliges. Chaz then asks Rune how he
knew that the creature was Dark Force, and Rune replies that he has seen
it before. Chaz then asks where he saw it, but Rune doesn't seem in the
mood for answering. Both Chaz and Rika get a little suspicious, but this
is interrupted by Wren approaching and informing them that all of Kuran's
functions have been properly restored. He also tells them that all they
need to do now is to make some final adjustments at Zelan, so they go.

<a id="s6-3-5"></a>

> 🥉 **Musk Cat, Tusk Cat** — Receive the Silver Tusk. _(RetroAchievements · 5 pts)_


### 6.3.5. Crushed Ice and Musk Cats

Starting Party: Wren , Chaz , Rika , Rune , Raja
Starting Level: 24-25, 25-26, 26-27, 25-26, 27-28
A little while later, Wren has done his stuff and tells the party that all
of the maintenance systems for Algo's environment are working properly
again. Everything seems to be sorted out. But wait... It appears that
Dezolis' perpetual snowstorm still hasn't stopped. Chaz asks if their
systems have been restored, and Wren confirms that they have. Raja then
claims that he told them so, and that the demons in Garuberk Tower are
causing the blizzard on Dezolis. He moans that they never listen, and Wren
points out that if the snowstorm doesn't stop then the Parmanians and even
the Dezolisians may perish. They all decide to go back to Dezolis, but
Rune points out that it is covered with walls of ice, and they won't be
able to get anywhere on the surface. Wren suggest that they can use the
Ice Digger, a car that he had purposely built in preparation for any action
required on Dezolis. He then loads it onto the Landale.

Head down to the elevator, use it, then head out of Zelan. Select Dezolis
as the destination, then sit back and wait till the party arrives. Use one
of the Regen Platforms to restore yourselves after the battle with Dark
Force, then go outside.

The ICE-DIGGER is permanently in your inventory, and you can use it at any
point outside. It has the unique ability to clear snow that lays in its
path, and this will come in handy very soon. Apart from that it functions
in exactly the same way as the Land Rover.

Before anything else, equip Wren's PULSE-LASR, replacing the NAPALMSHOT.
Save your game then get in the Ice Digger. Head a little east then north
through the gap between the mountain range above. Continue north until you
reach an ice wall, then drive through the ice northwards, keeping to the
west as much as possible. Once you come out the other side, head a little
further north until you reach a cave entrance. Get out of the Ice Digger
then go into the cave.


```
  ______________
 // DUNGEON #14 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\
```

|/  Mysterious Valley      \_________________________________
   Enemies: HungryMole, Skytiara, Tech-Plant
  Treasure: TRIMATE, STAR-DEW, SILVR-TUSK
Head up and left, following the passage until you reach a turning to the
right. From here, head right and go past the steps above you to collect
the TRIMATE from the small area near the wall. Head back to the steps and
go up them, then head through the door above and a little to your right.

Continue upwards, keeping close to the right wall, then head right and go
up through another doorway above. Head up the short passage that follows
and turn left at the corner, then pick up a STAR-DEW from the alcove in the
top wall. Continue left and then go down, and head through the door at the
bottom of the corridor. Head left, passing around the protruding wall, and
address one of the cats guarding the next doorway. They welcome you to the
valley, and Chaz is surprised that they talk. They then explain that they
are musk cats, and hence they can talk. The musk cats say that they get a
special feeling from Chaz, and suggest he sees the old man. They then let
the party pass. Go through the door.

The next corridor is filled with several musk cats. If you speak to these
cats you will learn that they seem to have a fond remembrance of you, that
the valley is the only warm place in Dezolis, that no human has ever set
foot in the valley, and that the old man has a treasure. Go through the
door on the far right of the passageway.

Head up the passage into the large chamber that follows and speak to the
huge winged musk cat sitting on the raised platform above. He introduces
himself as the chief of the valley. He notes that there is good in Chaz's
eyes, and that he has a feeling that it is not the first time they have
met. He says he feels safe about giving something to you. It is a treasure
that has been passed down from generation to generation of the musk cats.
He then gives you the Silver Tusk.

Don't equip the SILVR-TUSK to Rika just yet, but do not sell it either.
It is far from the strongest claw in the game, but it is the most useful
against the Darkness. With your prize, use a HINAS or an ESCAPIPE or walk
out of the Mysterious Valley.

<a id="s6-3-6"></a>

> 🥉 **Pengo Land** — Take a walk with a penguin. _(RetroAchievements · 3 pts)_
> 🥉 **Penguin Power** — Summon a penguin. _(RetroAchievements · 4 pts)_


### 6.3.6. Food Fit for a Penguin

Starting Party: Wren , Chaz , Rika , Rune , Raja
Starting Level: 24-25, 25-26, 26-27, 25-26, 27-28
Jump into the Ice Digger and head south through the ice wall, then head
east at the first opening on the right. Continue east a short distance then
drive into the village of Zosa.

________


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\
Zosa    |Inn            |Per person    120 MST /
_______/|_______________|______________________/
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\
        |Tool Store     |DIMATE        160 MST /
        |               |ANTIDOTE       10 MST \
        |               |CURE-PARAL    120 MST /
        |               |TELEPIPE      130 MST \
        |               |ESCAPIPE       70 MST /
        |               |PENGU-FEED    800 MST \
        |_______________|______________________/
        |¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\
        |Weapon Store   |FLAMESWORD  12900 MST|  +81 ATK  +15 DFS  +4 STR /
        |               |THUNDRCLAW   8500 MST|  +37 ATK   +2 STR         \
        |               |TORNDDAGGR   8300 MST|  +34 ATK   +2 STR         /
        |               |DREAM-ROD    5400 MST|  +20 ATK   +4 DFS  +2 MTL \
        |_______________|_____________________|___________________________/
        |¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\
        |Armour Store   |PHANTAROBE   8400 MST|  +52 DFS   +5 MTL         /
        |_______________|_____________________|___________________________/
        |¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\
        |Penguin Man    |Hire Penguin  500 MST \
        |_______________|______________________/
```

This Dezolisian village is home to a number of Dezolis Penguins. There is
a man on the west side of the village who rents out Penguins, and for 500
MST you can have the party followed by a Dezolis Penguin. The Penguin
leaves the party if they go in a building or leave the village, and it does
nothing of any value, so there isn't much point renting one.

There is also an item that may be bought in the Tool Store called the
PENGU-FEED. This item can cure Poison, although the result text says that
the character's HP have increased. However, if the party try to leave the
Tool Store with a PENGU-FEED in their possession, a Dezolis Penguin runs
across the front of the Store and steals the PENGU-FEED from them. Again,
a completely pointless thing to do.

On a more practical note, it is time to buy some new equipment for the
characters. You'll want to get a FLAMESWORD for Chaz, two THUNDRCLAWs to
replace Rika's PLSM-CLAWs, and a PHANTAROBE for Rune. You could buy a
PHANTAROBE for Raja, but this is a waste of money, as you shall soon find
out. These few items will set you back 38300, which should be easily
affordable after your visit to Kuran. Equip them, then rest at the Inn if
you need to, and purchase whatever other items you may need.

Once you are done, leave Zosa and get back in the Ice Digger. Continue to
the east, heading a little north until you reach another ice wall. Plough
through it to the northeast, then continue a little east on the other side
and stop just before the metal structure. Get out of the vehicle, swap
Chaz's FLAMESWORD back to the PLSM-SWORD, save the game, then enter.

<a id="s6-3-7"></a>

> 🥉 **A Doomed Vessel** — Inspect the computer system in Wreckage. _(RetroAchievements · 5 pts)_
> 🥈 **Weather Watch** — Investigate Climate Control for any weather malfunctions. (Missed upon the snowstorm ending.) _(RetroAchievements · 10 pts)_


### 6.3.7. The Weather System

Starting Party: Wren , Chaz , Rika , Rune , Raja
Starting Level: 25-26, 26-27, 27-28, 26   , 28


```
 // DUNGEON #15 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\
```

|/  Climate Control Centre \_________________________________
   Enemies: Arthropod, Debugger, Dragerduel, ProtectBit, Wiredine
  Treasure: REPAIR-KIT, PULSEVULCN, 5000 MST, COMPO-GEAR,
            REPAIR-KIT, COMPO-ARMR
 \
  \   Boss: Gy-Laguiah, D-Elm-Lars
   \______________________________


```
 __________
```

| BOSS #9  \____________  ____________________


```
| Gy-Laguiah            ||                    |
|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|| Recommended Level: | 
|  HP: 2580             ||                    |
| EXP: 10000  MST: 1224 || Wren: 25          /
|                       || Chaz: 26         /
| Weak: Water,Engy,Lght || Rika: 27-28     /
| Res:  Fire            || Rune: 26       /
| Imm:  -               || Raja: 28      /
|                       ||              /
```

You have to fight this guardian as soon as you enter the Control Centre.
Technically, this guy isn't really a boss this time, as the music is just
normal battle music. However, the battle is unavoidable and inescapable, so
I thought it should be categorized as a boss battle. Besides, you only have
to fight the Gy-Laguiah twice in the entire game, and this is his final
chance in the spotlight, so I figured that he should go out in style.

As the Gy-Laguiah is no different from his debut fight, this battle should
be very easy. Don't bother with defensive preparations. Just have Chaz use
GITHU, Rika use DBLSLASH, Rune use NAWAT, Wren use FLARE, and Raja use RES
on the character hit in the round before. Ignore Wren getting damaged, as
the Gy-Laguiah will not be able to kill him before it is defeated.

Without needing to deviate from this pattern, the battle will conclude
after three or four rounds.
Wren will announce that they are in the control system for the Dezolis
climate, and Chaz notes that the monsters have been making a nest. Wren
says that, as they suspected, the centre must be the cause of the abnormal
weather conditions, but Raja is adamant that it is the Garuberk Tower.

Head up the passageway until you reach an elevator, but instead of going in
it, head right until you reach the wall. Walk up and then head right at the
top, turning down at the corner that follows. In the room at the bottom,
collect a REPAIR-KIT, then head back up and left to the elevator shaft in
the centre of the room. Continue up the corridor until you reach the very
top. Turn left at this junction, and then head down at the corner. Continue
down the corridor, all the way to the bottom, and pick up the PULSEVULCN.

Equip this new hit-all weapon to Wren, then head back up and right to the
junction. Ignore the path to your right as it leads to a dead end, and go
back down around the central column. Take the elevator.

Walk all the way down the walkway until you reach a junction at the bottom.
Turn left, ignoring the elevator fot the moment, and walk left and then up
at the corner. Turn right when you need to, then go up to the end of the
walkway to procure 5000 MST. Return down, left, down and right to the
elevator you passed on the way, then ascend in it back to the surface.

Head a little left and pick up the COMPO-GEAR, then equip this to Wren. Go
back to the elevator and take it to the floor below. Turn right to the
junction, then head right and take the elevator here. Walk right in the
small corridor and enter the elevator in the upper wall on the right.

Head left along the walkway, turning up when you reach the corner. Keep
going up, then go left and then up again. When you reach the choice of the
