wide walkway to the left and a thin path to the right, take the thin path
and then head up to the end to obtain another REPAIR-KIT. Go back down and
then left, and keep heading left until you reach the hole in the walkway.
Walk up from here and enter the elevator in the top wall.

Ignore the path to the right as it leads to a dead end, and instead follow
the line right and downwards, continuing down until you reach the bottom.
Head right and then up, still following the line, and descend in the
elevator at the top. Now, go down to the junction and turn left, then pick
up the COMPO-ARMR from the small alcove at the end. Replace Wren's old
ZIRCOARMER with this new protective outfit, then return to the junction and
head up, near to the elevator. Next, check your characters' Level status.
Chaz and Rune should be at least Level 27 by now, Rika is likely to be at
least Level 28, Wren should be around Level 26 or 27, and Raja should be
at Level 29. If this is not the case, spend a moment getting those last few
EXP for the characters falling behind.

Go around the elevator to either the left or the right, then walk up the
passage the is above you. There will be a blue-cloaked figure in front of
the computer panels, but don't approach him yet. First, fully heal your
party and check your recently acquired items are all equipped properly,
including replacing Wren's PULSEVULCN with the trusty NAPALMSHOT and
swapping one of Rika's THUNDRCLAWs with her SILVR-TUSK. Also, change the
PLSM-SWORD in Chaz's possession for the FLAMESWORD.


```
Recommended       |   Wren   |   Chaz   |   Rika   |   Rune   |   Raja   |
Equipment   |¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|
            |Head |COMPO-GEAR|SILV-HELM |SILV-CROWN|SILVCIRCLT|SILVCIRCLT|
            |Right|NAPALMSHOT|FLAMESWORD|SILVR-TUSK|SILVSHIELD|SILVSHIELD|
            |Left | /2-HAND  | /2-HAND  |THUNDRCLAW|SILVSHIELD|SILVSHIELD|
            |Body |COMPO-ARMR|SILV-MAIL |SILV-MAIL |PHANTAROBE|SILV-MANTL|
```

Once you are prepared, approach the sinister witch. He will laugh, and
call you foolhardy for coming here, as it is a trap. He then says it will
be a waste of time fighting stupid people like you, but he has to follow
orders. Chaz asks whose orders, pointing out they've defeated Zio and Dark
Force, but the witch disagrees. He will then engage you in battle.


```
 __________
```

| BOSS #10 \____________  ____________________


```
| D-Elm Lars            ||                    |
|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|| Recommended Level: | 
|  HP: 777              ||                    |
| EXP: 3919   MST: 500  || Wren: 26          /
|                       || Chaz: 27         /
| Weak: Energy*,Light   || Rika: 28-29     /
| Res:  -               || Rune: 26-27    /
| Imm:  -               || Raja: 29      /
|                       ||              /
```

This fellow is ridiculously easy. All you need to do in this battle is
have Chaz, Rika and Wren attack, and let Rune and Raja just defend. Even
doing this, the battle will only last a couple of rounds.
After the combat, Chaz will be uneasy about the fact that Dark Force may
still be alive, and Wren informs the party that there is nothing wrong with
the climate control system. Again, Raja says that it is the Garuberk Tower
that is behind it all.

Back in control, refit Wren with his PULSEVULCN and Rika with her other
THUNDRCLAW (keep the FLAMESWORD equipped), then use HINAS or an ESCAPIPE or
make your way out of the Climate Control Centre on foot.

<a id="s6-3-8"></a>

> 🥉 **Raja** — Recruit Raja. _(RetroAchievements · 1 pts)_


### 6.3.8. Raja's not Laughing

Starting Party: Wren , Chaz , Rika , Rune , Raja
Starting Level: 26   , 27   , 28-29, 26-27, 29
Use RYUKA or a TELEPIPE to go back to Zosa, or pile into the Ice Digger.
Return west, back through the ice wall, then head south and west again, and
drive into Zosa.

Stay a night in the Inn and restock your inventory if you wish, then leave
Zosa and get in the Ice Digger. Head east, keeping to the south this time,
and pass east and south around a snow-topped forest. Just to the east of
this, below a mountain range, is a village. This is Reshel, but at the
moment there is nothing there but Zombies. Enter this place if you wish,
but the only things of value you will find are EXP and Mesetas.

Head a little south of Reshel, then continue east alongside the mountains
until you see another village tucked into the mountain range below. Unlike
Reshel, this village is inhabited, but it is not without problems. Drive
into the village of Meese.

________


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\
Meese   |Inn            |Per person    140 MST /
_______/|_______________|______________________/
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\
        |Tool Store     |DIMATE        160 MST /
        |               |ANTIDOTE       10 MST \
        |               |CURE-PARAL    120 MST /
        |               |TELEPIPE      130 MST \
        |               |ESCAPIPE       70 MST \
        |_______________|______________________/
        |¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\
        |Weapon Store   |FLAMESWORD  12900 MST|  +81 ATK  +15 DFS  +4 STR /
        |               |THUNDRCLAW   8500 MST|  +37 ATK   +2 STR         \
        |               |TORNDDAGGR   8300 MST|  +34 ATK   +2 STR         /
        |               |DREAM-ROD    5400 MST|  +20 ATK   +4 DFS  +2 MTL \
        |_______________|_____________________|___________________________/
        |¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\
        |Armour Store   |RFLC-MAIL   26800 MST|  +53 DFS                  /
        |               |RFLCSHIELD  15600 MST|  +23 DFS                  \
        |_______________|_____________________|___________________________/
```

As soon as you enter the village, remove all of Raja's equipment. He won't
be needing it any more. Meese is a Parmanian village, like Tyler, although
speaking to the villagers will reveal that the Meese seems to be overrun by
a terrible sickness. Those inflicted with the illness ofter die within a
month, and then return from the grave as zombies (explaining what happened
in Reshel).

Go to the Armour Store and sell all of the excess equipment you have been
carrying (including Raja's old equipment and Wren's NAPALMSHOT, as by the
time you will be fighting a boss again he will have a better single-target
gun). With the large sum of Mesetas you will have received, you shouldn't
have too much trouble buying two RFLC-MAILs, one for Chaz and one for Rika.
Equip their new armour and sell the old SILV-MAILs, then wander over to
the southeast corner of Meese. This used to be the Inn, but the owner had
made it into a public clinic since the disease outbreak. Go in.

There are a lot of sick people in this place, under the care of a group of
people known as Espers. They have been sent from Esper Mansion, a building
southeast of Meese, to try to help the villagers. Head up from the entrance
and then left along the corridor. Go upstairs, then go right and into the
right-hand room. Speak to the Esper here to learn that the illness started
as soon as the Garuberk Tower appeared, and Raja says that he told them
that the Garuberk Tower was the cause of everything. Suddenly, Raja feels
very dizzy and he collapses to the floor. Chaz thinks he's joking, but
Rika points out that he's got a tremendous fever. They carry him to a bed.

Chaz is still convinced that Raja is fooling around, but Rika chastises him
by saying that it's no laughing matter. Rune and Rika both sense something,
and Rune says that he has sensed it since they arrived on Dezolis, only it
is much stronger here. Chaz asks what they are talking about, and Rune
explains that the cause of the illness is the Black Energy Wave. He
surmises that it is coming from the Garuberk Tower, and that it must be
pretty close. At that moment, an Esper runs up into the room and shouts
that a girl named Kyra has gone to the Garuberk Tower all by herself. Chaz
asks who she is, and the Esper explains that she is a very courageous
person from their group. However, the Garuberk Tower is surrounded by a
forest of carnivorous trees. Chaz decides that they should go and save her,
and asks where the Garuberk Tower is. The Esper tells them that it is to
the northeast of Meese.

> **Raja leaves the party**

<a id="s6-3-9"></a>

### 6.3.9. Bi-Millennial Man

Starting Party: Wren , Chaz , Rika , Rune
Starting Level: 26-27, 27-28, 29   , 27
Head downstairs and out of the clinic, then stay at the Inn to the left.
Leave Meese and pull out the Ice Digger. Drive north until you reach a
small wooded area, then head east and through a gap in the mountain range.
From here, head north between the mountains and drive straight into the
forest at the top. This immediately takes you out of the vehicle, and
Chaz points out that even with a vehicle they can't break through. Rika
then spots someone being attacked by the trees, and a battle then ensues.


```
 __________
```

| BOSS #11 \____________  ____________________


```
| Carnivorous Trees x3  ||                    |
|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|| Recommended Level: | 
|  HP: 240              ||                    |
| EXP: -      MST: -    || Wren: N/A         /
|                       || Chaz: N/A        /
| Weak: Fire,Engy,Light || Rika: N/A       /
| Res:  Water           || Rune: N/A      /
| Imm:  -               ||               /
|                       ||              /
```

There are three Carnivorous Trees. Individually, they are not particularly
dangerous enemies. The only thing they do each round is attack (sometimes
inflicting Poison). However, each time a Carnivorous Tree is defeated it is
replaced with a new one. This cycle never, ever ends, and eventually the
party will be wiped out. Unlike all other boss battles, you can run from
this battle, and this is exactly what you should do. Don't do anything in
the first round except escape. There is no point fighting at all, as you
cannot possibly win. Just run.
After escaping, a cut-scene begins. The girl thanks you the party for
rescuing her, and introduces herself as Kyra Tierney. She asks who they
are, and Rika explains that they were sent by Kyra's friends to save her.
Chaz says it was reckless of Kyra to go out on her own, but Kyra tells
them that she felt that she had to do something, as she couldn't stand
seeing all those people in pain. Chaz asks if there may be a better way
to get past the carnivorous trees, to which Kyra suggests that they see
the Esper leader, Lutz. She then tells the story of how the wizard Lutz and
a heroine named Alis saved Algo from an evil force two thousand years ago.
Chaz questions how Lutz can still be alive, and Kyra goes on to say that he
is hidden in the deepest depths of Esper Mansion, and that only top-ranking
people may be granted an audience with him. Kyra claims to have seen Lutz
from afar once, and that she could recognize it was him by how intelligent,
classy, graceful and generally wonderful he is. Chaz still can't understand
how Lutz could still be alive after 2000 years, but Kyra explains that he
is an unparalleled magician and a legendary hero, who may have even found
the secret of immortatility. Wren hypothesizes that it must involve
cryogenic hibernation. Kyra then tells them that she can't leave the people
of Meese in misery, and that they should go and meet Lutz. The rest of the
party agree, and then it's back on the road.

> **Kyra joins the party (Level 27)**


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

Kyra is the party's new Alys, as she also uses slashers. This means that
you now have two characters that can attack all enemies at once, which
should make battles much easier. Place Kyra just after Rika, as she is not
as strong as the physical characters but tougher than Rune.


```
Recommended       |   Wren   |   Chaz   |   Rika   |   Kyra   |   Rune   |
Equipment   |¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|
            |Head |COMPO-GEAR|SILV-HELM |SILV-CROWN|SILV-CROWN|SILVCIRCLT|
            |Right|PULSEVULCN|FLAMESWORD|SILVR-TUSK|LACOSLASHR|SILVSHIELD|
            |Left | /2-HAND  | /2-HAND  |THUNDRCLAW|RFLCSHIELD|SILVSHIELD|
            |Body |COMPO-ARMR|RFLC-MAIL |RFLC-MAIL |RFLC-ROBE |PHANTAROBE|
```

Kyra is the party's new Alys, as she also uses slashers. This means that
you now have two characters that can attack all enemies at once, which
should make battles much easier.

Return south and then west out of the mountains, continuing west and south
until you are back near Meese. Next, drive south through the ice wall just
to the east of Meese and then east when you come out the other side. Head
east and south around the forest, then go back north and then northeast
through the next ice wall. When you come out the other side, you should see
a large mansion to the east. This is Esper Mansion, so go on in.

<a id="s6-3-10"></a>

### 6.3.10. A Surprising Revelation

Starting Party: Wren , Chaz , Rika , Kyra , Rune
Starting Level: 26-27, 27-28, 29   , 27   , 27
Address the guards blocking the entrance to Esper Mansion, and they will
see Kyra and let you pass. Walk into the building, and head down the
corridor to the right. Turn up at the corner and then turn right again,
passing the corridor above you and going through the door at the end of the
passage in the upper wall. Pick up the LACO-ROD, RFLC-ROBE, SOL-DEW and
10000 MST from this small room, and equip the RFLC-ROBE to Rune. You can
also equip the LACO-ROD if you wish, but his two SILVSHIELDs will be more
useful in the long run.

Leave the room then go left and up the long passage you passed earlier,
until you come to two doors. Head through the door on the left and continue
up the corridor, turning left at the corner at the top. Follow the passage
a little further left and then turn down to speak to one of the guards
standing in front of the doorway below you. The guard will tell Kyra that
she may not enter without permission. She gets agitated by this but the
guard will remain constant. At that moment, Rune cuts in and demands that
the guards let them pass. The guard begins to refuse but suddenly realises
who he is speaking to. He apologises profusely to Rune, and lets the party
through. Chaz is more suspicious than ever.

Go down through the door to find yourself in a courtyard. Go either left or
right and then down around the large central building, then head up and
walk through the doorway. Speak to the old man on the left and he will
welcome Rune back, saying that he is glad that Rune is safe. Rune says that
the old man can forget the formalities, and that he is going in. The old
man complies.

Walk towards the staircase and the party will stop. Rune will explain that
they are in the inner sanctuary and that, just beyond, there is a chamber
called Lutz's room. Kyra confirms this, and then gets anxious about meeting
Lutz, asking if her clothes are clean and her hair is alright. The party
will then head down the stairs automatically, and approach a small sphere
on a table in the centre of an otherwise empty room. Kyra looks around,
wondering where Lutz is, and a cut-scene begins.

Rune explains that Lutz is not here, having left this world long ago. Wren
adds to this by saying that no human could live for two thousand years, but
Kyra doesn't accept it, telling the party that she saw Lutz with her own
eyes. She also says that she believes in the legend of the Espers and of
Lutz, and that is why everyone is trying so hard. Rune tells Kyra to calm
herself down, telling her that even if Lutz's body is no more, his spirit
lives on. He adds that before Lutz died, he left his will and memory in the
Telepathy Ball, the sphere on the table. Rika asks Rune if he is saying
that the ball is Lutz, but Rune tells her that Lutz is not there now. He
says that if the chosen person appears, the Lutz's will and memory are
transferred into that person. In a grand gesture, Rune points at his own
head, and the party realise that Rune is Lutz.

The old man appears again, and confirms this. He explains that Rune Walsh
is the fifth-generation Lutz, and Kyra is left a little bewildered. Rune
then speaks to Chaz, telling him that since ancient times there has been a
cycle where disasters occur every thousand years, due to a personification
of evil called Dark Force that appears every thousand years. He adds that,
up until now, a courageous person would defeat the evil and bring peace
back to the world. Rika points out that they definitely did defeat Dark
Force on Kuran, but that the abnormal conditions are still continuing.
Rune goes on to say that Algo was shaken a thousand years ago by the
explosion of the planet Parma, upsetting the delicate balance they have
tried so hard to maintain. He surmises that this may be the cause. Chaz
asks Rune if that means that Dark Force is still alive. Rune replies that
doesn't know, but he is certain that the root of all evil is not yet
destroyed, and it must be defeated.

Rune then tells Chaz that he has chosen him as the soldier to fight the
final battle, explaining that he sensed from the start that Chaz had great
potential. In a more light-hearted manner, Rune apologises for keeping it a
secret all this time, and jokingly asks if they'll keep on cooperating.
Chaz, a little confuses, sort of agrees, then Rune announces that they have
to go to the Garuberk Tower. The old man then says that there is a forest
of carnivorous trees surrounding the tower (which you already know), but if
they use the 'Eclipse Torch' they will be able to destroy it. Rune then
states that their next destination is the Gumbious Temple, and the old man
tells them that it can be found in the valley to the west. Rune tells Chaz
to stop looking so dazed, and Kyra expresses her disappointment that Lutz
would be so insensitive. Rune apologises, telling her that he's always been
like that, but it doesn't seem to make Kyra any happier.

After that extensive and quite illuminating cut-scene, you finally have
control of the party again. Ascend the staircase out of Lutz's room (no
form of teleportation works in this room - it must be magically protected).
You can't use HINAS or an ESCAPIPE here as it isn't a dungeon, but a quick
way to get out of Esper Mansion is to use RYUKA or a TELEPIPE and select
EspMansion as the destination. Your next task is now set.

<a id="s6-4"></a>

> 🥉 **A Library for the AGES** — Read 3 certain books in a school. _(RetroAchievements · 1 pts)_


## 6.4. Quest for the Torch

<a id="s6-4-1"></a>

### 6.4.1. Dezolis' Largest Town

Starting Party: Wren , Chaz , Rika , Kyra , Rune
Starting Level: 26-27, 27-28, 29   , 27   , 27
Get in the Ice Digger, then head southwest through the ice wall and return
west and south around the forest. Keep to the southwest, and head south
through the next ice wall. Head west out the other side, then drive a
little north and continue west until you see a large town to the north of
a mountain range. Drive into the town of Jut.

________


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\

        |               |ANTIDOTE       10 MST \
        |               |CURE-PARAL    120 MST /
        |               |TELEPIPE      130 MST \
        |               |ESCAPIPE       70 MST \
        |_______________|______________________/
        |¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\
        |Weapon Store   |LACO-SWORD  20400 MST| +103 ATK  +19 DFS  +10 DEX/
        |               |LACODAGGER   9400 MST|  +39 ATK                  \
        |               |LACO-CLAW   10200 MST|  +51 ATK                  /
        |               |LACOSLASHR  21600 MST|  +30 ATK                  \
        |_______________|_____________________|___________________________/
        |¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\
        |Armour Store   |RFLC-MAIL   26800 MST|  +53 DFS                  /
        |               |RFLC-ROBE   18400 MST|  +58 DFS                  /
        |               |RFLCSHIELD  15600 MST|  +23 DFS                  \
        |_______________|_____________________|___________________________/
```

This will be the last batch of equipment that you will be buying for a
while, but it is a mighty expensive one. Sell any equipment that is
cluttering your inventory (which will be hardly any since you wiped it
in Meese only a little while ago). Next, you should buy a LACO-SWORD, a
LACO-CLAW and a LACOSLASHR. Although this is only a few weapons, the bill
will come to a whopping 52200. If you can't afford this yet, buy what you
can, leaving the LACO-CLAW until last.

Equip the LACO-SWORD to Chaz and replace Kyra's RFLCSHIELD to set her up
with a pair of LACOSLASHRs. Once this is done, sell the FLAMESWORD and the
RFLCSHIELD. Don't equip the LACO-CLAW yet, instead replace the SILVR-TUSK
with Rika's other THUNDRCLAW, as this is more useful in the area to come.


```
Recommended       |   Wren   |   Chaz   |   Rika   |   Kyra   |   Rune   |
Equipment   |¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|
            |Head |COMPO-GEAR|SILV-HELM |SILV-CROWN|SILV-CROWN|SILVCIRCLT|
            |Right|PULSEVULCN|LACO-SWORD|THUNDRCLAW|LACOSLASHR|SILVSHIELD|
            |Left | /2-HAND  | /2-HAND  |THUNDRCLAW|LACOSLASHR|SILVSHIELD|
            |Body |COMPO-ARMR|RFLC-MAIL |RFLC-MAIL |RFLC-ROBE |RFLC-ROBE |
```

Get a night's sleep at the Inn and get a few TRIMATEs and other items if
you wish, then make your way out of Jut and jump into the Ice Digger. Drive
westwards until you reach a large forest, then head south into the ice wall
below. Head through the ice, turning to the west along the way, and get out
of the Ice Digger near the metal building on the other side. Save your game
and then enter.

<a id="s6-4-2"></a>

> 🥉 **Initiate: Burst Rockets** — Recover the Burst Roc parts in Weapons Plant. _(RetroAchievements · 5 pts)_


### 6.4.2. Factory for Firearms

Starting Party: Wren , Chaz , Rika , Kyra , Rune
Starting Level: 26-27, 27-28, 29   , 27   , 27


```
 // DUNGEON #16 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\
```

|/  Weapons Plant          \_________________________________
   Enemies: Arthropod, LifeDeletr, Servant, Silvalt, Star Drone,
            Wiredine
  Treasure: BURSTROC (Skill), PLSMLAUNCH, ELST-GEAR, ELST-ARMOR,
            REPAIR-KIT (infinite supply)
As soon as you enter, Rika asks what the place is, to which Wren replies
that it is a weapons plant that Mother Brain built a thousand years ago. It
was soon realised to be an unnecessary facility and was shut down, but
within the last six months it has begun manufacturing automatic weapons due
to orders from Kuran. Chaz asks if they should shut it down, but Wren tells
him that Zelan stopped the production once it was back in control. He sees
no problem with leaving the weapons plant it as it is.

Ignoring Wren's advice, head up across the room and take the elevator at
the top. Go right a short way and descend in the next elevator nearby. Go
left along the corridor and then up at the corner, turning right at the
top. Keep going to the right and then use the elevator in the upper wall.

Head to the left along the walkway, ignoring both the paths above and
below you, and continue to the left until the end. Walk up until you reach
a junction. The conveyor belt above is rolling against you, so take the
one to the right. From the end, head upwards and use the computer terminal
at the top to reverse the belt direction. Go back down and then left across
the conveyor, then take the conveyor above. At the top, go all the way to
the right, ignoring the first elevator, and take the next elevator to the
floor above.

Walk left, down, right, down and then left, and head up at the corner to
open the chest at the end. As usual, Chaz doesn't have a clue what the
things are inside, but Wren informs him that it is the Burst Roc unit, a
long range semi-automatic weapon that fires heat energy bursts. He installs
it. (Notice how he is less bashful than Demi at install weapon units).

Wren acquires the BURSTROC Skill
Return all the way round to the elevator, then descend back to the level
below. Head back to the left, and take the elevator you ignored earlier. In
this next area, go right, down, left, down and then right to the corner.
Walk up and then a little right, and enter the elevator in the top wall.

Head to the right, then step on the platform to be taken down to a small
walkway. Step onto the next platform just to the right, and then get off at
the end. Go to the left and use the elevator. Walk a little down, then
follow the path left, up and then right, and obtain the PLSMLAUNCH from the
end. This is far more powerful than Wren's PULSEVULCN, but only hits one
target, so don't bother equipping it yet. Return back left, down and right
then take the elevator back up.

Go left and use the two sets of platforms to return to the top, then head
left along the walkway to another platform on the left. Take it down, then
walk a little to the left and take the next platform to the bottom. Go
left, then descend in the elevator nearby.

Walk a little down, then go right and up, ignoring the empty chest to your
left and instead turning right at the junction. In the small room that
follows, pick up the ELST-GEAR and the ELST-ARMOR, and equip them both to
Wren straight away. Finally, if you feel you need some more REPAIR-KITs,
examine the computer panel between the two chests. You will obtain a
REPAIR-KIT. Examine it again and you will get another REPAIR-KIT. You can
do this as many times as you want, up until you can't carry any more.

There is nothing else to do in the Weapons Plant, so use HINAS or an
ESCAPIPE, or make your way out of the place on foot. Also make sure to give
the SILVR-TUSK back to Rika once the party are out.

<a id="s6-4-3"></a>

### 6.4.3. Theft in the Temple

Starting Party: Wren , Chaz , Rika , Kyra , Rune
Starting Level: 27-28, 29-30, 30-32, 28-29, 28-29
Get out your Ice Digger and drive east through the ice wall, heading to the
north along the way. Continue east until you can see Jut again. This time,
however, go a little northeast of Jut and you will find a large building.
This is Gumbious Temple, your next port of call. Go inside.

There are three corridors here, and first you want to head right. Take the
staircase to the basement, then go a little left and up to the junction.
Two Dezolisian guards are blocking the right passage, so go left and up at
the corner to a small room. Pick up the TRIMATE, MOON-DEW, STAR-DEW and
SOL-DEW, then go back down and return to the staircase. Take it.

Walk back left along the passage, continuing past the entrance to the next
staircase. Ascend to the floor above, then head right to the end of the
corridor. Go up and speak to the priest-like Dezolisian standing on the
steps, below the Eclipse Torch. Chaz obviously asks him for the Torch, as
he blatantly refuses, saying that the holy flame cannot go beyond the gate.
He continues that he will not allow it, even if it is the wish of the
mighty Lutz. Chaz then gets a little annoyed, pointing out that the entire
future of Algo depends on it, but the priest won't hear of it.

At that moment, three purple-robed witches (not dissimilar to the one you
met in the Climate Control Centre) appear around the Eclipse Torch. The
middle one laughs, and tells them that he intends to take the Torch. Chaz
asks what the witch thinks he's doing, then the left witch laughs and tells
him that they are from the Air Castle. The one in the middle then addresses
Rune personally, saying that if he is Lutz he will remember. The left one
then adds that Rune will know how will be waiting for him at the Air
Castle. They then take the Eclipse Torch. The left one then tells them
the group that if they want the Torch back they will have to come and get
it, if they don't mind losing their life. The middle one then laughs one
more time (a common trait with these witches), and then they all vanish.

The Dezolisian is stricken, blaming himself for his narrow-mindedness. Chaz
and Rune try to cheer him up, and Chaz says that all they have to do is go
and retrieve it. The priest is very grateful, but Chaz adds that if they do
recover it then they must be allowed to borrow it. The Dezolisian priest
happily agrees, then Rika asks Rune about the Air Castle. He says that Lutz
does remember it, and that it was a castle that used to float in the sky
above Parma. Rika notes, however, that it would have been destroyed along
with the rest of Parma a thousand years ago, and Wren adds that an asteroid
belt is all that is left of where Parma used to be. Rune suggests that
perhaps, somehow, the Air Castle managed to survive. Wren is sceptical, but
says that he will check the sensors on the Landale. Chaz then asks Rune who
the person was that the witches were talking about, and Rune explains that
the first Lutz and his companions fought a man in the Air Castle, and that
his name was Lashiec. Chaz asks if that is the person they meant, but Rune
replies that Lashiec was defeated by Lutz, and doesn't know what they will
find until they get there.

<a id="s6-4-4"></a>

### 6.4.4. Castle in the Skies

Starting Party: Wren , Chaz , Rika , Kyra , Rune
Starting Level: 27-28, 29-30, 30-32, 28-29, 28-29
Leave Gumbious Temple, save your game, and prepare for some Level building.
The next dungeon you are going to face is the biggest in the game, and the
most difficult so far. You will need to get all the characters up to an
absolute minimum of Level 32 before you even think of going anywhere else.
One of the best places to go to gain Levels quickly is the Weapons Plant,
as the enemies there provide the most EXP at this stage of the game. Try to
allow Arthropods and Wiredines to use their COMBINE ability, as LifeDeletrs
are very lucrative indeed.

By the time you have finished, Chaz should be at least Level 33 or 34, Rika
should be about Level 35 or 36, Rune and Wren should be at Level 32, and
Kyra should be around Level 32 or 33.

Go and buy all the equipment you may not have been able to afford earlier,
and replace Rika's THUNDRCLAW with the LACO-CLAW that you have yet to
equip. Also, ensure everyone else is equipped properly for the trial ahead.


```
Recommended       |   Wren   |   Chaz   |   Rika   |   Kyra   |   Rune   |
Equipment   |¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|
            |Head |ELST-GEAR |SILV-HELM |SILV-CROWN|SILV-CROWN|SILVCIRCLT|
            |Right|PULSEVULCN|LACO-SWORD|SILVR-TUSK|LACOSLASHR|SILVSHIELD|
            |Left | /2-HAND  | /2-HAND  |LACO-CLAW |LACOSLASHR|SILVSHIELD|
            |Body |ELST-ARMOR|RFLC-MAIL |RFLC-MAIL |RFLC-ROBE |RFLC-ROBE |
```

Once you are ready, use RYUKA or a TELEPIPE to teleport to Tyler, or hop
in the Ice Digger and head to this area, then go into the Spaceport.

The party automatically get into the Landale, and Wren begins his search
for the Air Castle. A moment later, he reports that he has got something,
although it is very faint. Rika asks if Wren can get it on-screen, so Wren
says he will try. An image of a floating castle amidst some asteroids
appears on the screen. Chaz says that it's the Air Castle, and Rune backs
this up. Chaz notes that it has a spooky atmosphere, so Kyra teases him,
asking if he's getting scared. Chaz says her to stop being ridiculous, and
announces that they are going in.

The Algo map screen appears, with a new destination on the list: A.CASTL.
Before you select it, though, cancel from the map and go down through the
Spaceport. Use one of the Regen Platforms to get the party fully prepared,
then return up and into the Landale. Select A.CASTL from the list, and
watch as the Landale cruises through space and lands next to the castle.

Wren says that gravity is normal and that there is a breathable atmosphere,
and notes that it must be an artificial condition. Chaz suggests that
whoever is there must be expecting them.

The Air Castle is, by far, the largest dungeon in the game, mainly because
it is really two dungeons merged into one. As such, the entire excursion is
split into two chapters, each outlining one of the distinct dungeon areas
of the Air Castle.

<a id="s6-4-5"></a>

### 6.4.5. Terrible Triumvirate

Starting Party: Wren , Chaz , Rika , Kyra , Rune
Starting Level: 32   , 33-34, 35-36, 32-33, 32


```
 // DUNGEON #17 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\
```

|/  Air Castle             \_________________________________
   Enemies: Bladeright, DimensWorm, FrostSaber, Spector, StoneHeads
  Treasure: 1000 MST, TRIMATE, 2000 MST, TRIMATE, 4000 MST,
            SWIFT-HELM, GENOCYCLAW, ESCAPIPE, 8000 MST, SOL-DEW
 \
  \   Boss: Xe-A-Thoul x3
   \______________________________

Go up and through the main entrance to the castle. Continue up across the
next small room and then up all the way to three flickering images of the
witches you met in Gumbious Temple. Examine them, and Kyra will notice that
they are just illusions. Rune adds that are also forming an 'invisible'
barrier (it's amazing how visible these barriers are). Chaz then suggests
that they will have to find the real witches and destroy them.

Go a little down and then right, taking the door in the upper wall along
this small passage. Head up, right and then down, and go straight into the
small room below you to acquire 1000 MST. Walk back up out of the room,
then continue to the right, down a little, right a bit more, and then up
through the next doorway. Continue up until you reach the crack in the
floor, then head left and up through the door.

Back outside, walk straight up and through the door back into the castle.
Head up actoss the small room, then turn right as soon as you pass the
doorway. Turn down at the corner and pick up the TRIMATE from the bottom of
the corridor. Go back up and a little to the left, then continue upwards.
Turn right after the doorway, then go down through the next door and ascend
the staircase to the floor above.

Head up, left at the corner and then down, and continue through the door
out onto the castle roof. Head a little down, then right to the edge. Walk
all the way down the battlement and through the doorway at the bottom to
take you back into the castle. Head down, completely ignoring the staircase
(it leads to a dead end), then go down into the small room to collect 2000
MST. Return back up, walk left, and then go all the way down the thin
corridor, across the small room, and back outside the castle.

Walk down, left, down and then left, and go up through the doorway. Turn
left again, then up along the balcony and go right at the top. Take the
doorway on the right and then go up the corridor, turning left and then
down. Head left, a little up and then left until you are below another door
that leads out onto the roof. You will also see the witch illusions below
you. Ignore this door, as it leads to a dead end, and continue left along
the balcony, a little down, then left and up through the next doorway.
Obtain the TRIMATE from the centre of this room, then go down through the
door on the left, following the corridor and out of the door at the bottom.
Head right, down and left along the balcony, then go through the doorway at
the end to take you back out onto the castle roof.

Go left, turn up and then left, and take the door back into the castle on
the left. Head up across the small room and up the thin corridor, then turn
right at the top. Ignore the stairs for the moment, and enter the small
room below to procure 4000 MST. Go back up and descend the staircase.

Head down and through the door out of the room. Ignore the path to the
right as it leads to a dead end, and instead continue downwards and then to
the right at the bottom. Turn up at the corner, then right again and down
into the next room. Retrieve the SWIFT-HELM and equip it to Chaz, before
returning all the way back round to the stairs. Take them.

Step a bit to the right, then go out onto the roof through the door above.
Head up across the battlements, turning right as soon as possible. Continue
right and take the door back into the castle at the end. In this single
room, pick up the GENOCYCLAW and equip it to Rika alongside the SILVR-TUSK.

Leave the room, then head a little to the left and up across the roof to
the next doorway. Step through and then continue upwards, turning left at
the corner and then heading down. Descend the staircase back down to the
level below, then walk up, right and down until you reach another larger
area. Go over to the left wall and then down into the small room to collect
the ESCAPIPE, then return out of the room and back to the right. Head down
and back out of the castle.

Turn right, down and then continue right all the way until you see a door
in the top wall. Directly opposite this door on the wall below is another
door. Go through the lower door and find yourself in a small chamber. This
is the room that the invisible barrier was guarding, and inside it is a
Regen Platform. Use this if you need to, then head up and out of the room.

Return up to the top door, then go through and head up to find another set
of the witch illusions. Walk left and go up through the next doorway, then
head right until you reach a junction. The right path takes you nowhere, so
go up between the chasms until you reach another junction. Again, the right
passage leads to a dead end, so head left and then up across the steps.
Turn left and then up through the doorway to take you back onto the roof.

Go left and then down along the roof, and descend the stairs at the bottom
(ignore the route to the right as it leads nowhere). Head right and then
up along the passageway, ignoring the stairs to the right for the moment
and continuing up the thin corridor into a small room. Acquire the 8000 MST
that are here, then return back down to the staircase and take them to the
floor above.

Head down along the thin balcony and then head right at the bottom. When
you reach a junction, head north and descend the stairs. Ignore the passage
above as it leads to a dead end, and go down the corridor to obtain the
SOL-DEW at the bottom. Return back up the passage, then go left and take
the stairs again. Go back down to the junction and turn right, then go up
through the doorway at the end. Take the stairs.

In the similar room above, head down and out onto the castle roof again,
then go left until you see a gap in the wall above. The doorway at the top
here leads to the three witches, and you'll want to make sure that each of
your characters is at least Level 34 before entering. It is unlikely that
anyone but Rika is at this Level at the moment, so spend some time in the
Air Castle gaining EXP until the others have caught up. Return to the
Spaceport to heal up when necessary, and save the game as often as you can.
You could even pay a visit to Motavia and test your skill against the
Sand Worms around Monsen, as they provide a lot of EXP when defeated.

Once everyone has fulfilled the Level 34 requirement, restore the party at
the Spaceport, save your game, and then carefully make your way back
through the Air Castle (escape from battles that you feel you may take a
lot of damage from). Once you have returned to the elaborate doorway, heal
any damage that the party may have received and then walk inside.

Walk up and approach the three witches. The party will stop just below
them and the witches will address you. The middle one will laugh, noting
that the party have come. The left one will then laugh, and tell you that
they have no use for anyone but Lutz, and the middle one will add that they
only have one use for him before laughing again. Finally, the left one will
say that they will kill him with their own hands. Battle then begins.


```
 __________
```

| BOSS #12 \____________  ____________________


```
| Xe-A-Thoul x3         ||                    |
|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|| Recommended Level: | 
|  HP: 1520             ||                    |
| EXP: 7374   MST: 1000 || Wren: 34          /
|                       || Chaz: 36         /
| Weak: Energy*,Light   || Rika: 38-39     /
| Res:  -               || Kyra: 34-35    /
| Imm:  -               || Rune: 34      /
|                       ||              /
```

Unless you are prepared and use the strategy given below, this will be an
exceptionally tough battle, and definitely the most difficult you will have
faced so far. If you are prepared, however, you may find that the battle is
no harder than the others. Even on their own, Xe-A-Thouls are considerably
powerful, but together they can combine their power to inflict a severe
amount of damage on the entire party. The most important things to do first
in this battle are to set up a Barrier to reduce your characters' damage
and to drop the Xe-A-Thouls' number to two.

In the first round, have Chaz use RAYBLADE, Rika use DBLSLASH, Rune use
EFESS, Wren use BARRIER, and Kyra use NAFOI. Make sure all three of the
single-target attacks are aimed at the same Xe-A-Thoul. This should inflict
around 1300-1350 HP of damage on that Xe-A-Thoul. Hopefully, Wren will be
able to set up his BARRIER before the Xe-A-Thouls can unleash their
combination attack, THNDRBLAST. Otherwise, each member of your party will
suffer a great deal of damage. Also, one or two of the Xe-A-Thouls may use
GIWAT or GIZAN, or they may just attack.

In the following rounds, have Chaz use AIRSLASH, Rika use SAR (or GISAR if
the party are very hurt), Rune continue to use EFESS, Wren use BURSTROC (or
RECOVER if he is low on HP), and Kyra use HEWN (or an appropriate curative
Technique if necessary). After your party has unleashed their first attack
or two, the most damaged Xe-A-Thoul will fall. This prevents them using
THNDRBLAST again. From now on, the battle will be much easier.

Keep following the above pattern, ensuring each member of your party stays
above half of their maximum HP, and the witches will be finished in a mere
three or four rounds.
Nothing is said once the battle is over, which is an unusual event after a
major boss battle. The room that the Xe-A-Thouls were guarding above only
contains a Regen Platform, so don't bother going in there. Instead, use
HINAS or an ESCAPIPE to return to the Air Castle entrance, then take the
Landale to a Spaceport. Use a Regen Platform here and save the game.

<a id="s6-4-6"></a>

> 🥈 **Towering Anger** — Prove yourself in the Tower of Anger. _(RetroAchievements · 10 pts)_


### 6.4.6. Castle Catacombs

Starting Party: Wren , Chaz , Rika , Kyra , Rune
Starting Level: 34-35, 36-37, 38-39, 34-35, 34
Return to the Air Castle, and head up through the main entrance door as
before. Continue up through the first room, and then up the passage to the
door that the barrier was blocking earlier. Now that it is gone, head up
through the doorway and find yourself in the small chamber with the Regen
Platform. Head through the top door and cross the area outside to go back
into the castle. Continue upwards and through the top door that the second
group of witch illusions was guarding. In the tiny room that follows, take
the staircase to the basement.


```
  ______________
 // DUNGEON #18 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\
```

|/  Air Castle Basement    \_________________________________
   Enemies: Bladeright, ChaosSorcr, DimensWorm, FrostSaber, Spector,
            StoneHeads
  Treasure: MOON-DEW, STAR-DEW, ECLPSTORCH
 \
  \   Boss: Lashiec
   \______________________________

The route through the basement is a simple one. Head a little left and then
all the way down to the bottom of the passage, ignoring the junction to the
right along the way. Turn right and then up at the next junction, and take
the stairs at the top. Go a little up and then right, then take the upper
path at the junction. Turn left at the top corner and then go down at the
junction that follows. Descend the staircase.

Head down to the bottom of the corridor and turn left at the junction. Head
up around the corner and follow the passage all the way to the end to pick
up a MOON-DEW. Return down to the bottom and then go right, continuing
right at the junction. Head up the passage, turning left and then up again,
then take the next staircase to the floor below.

Walk down, then left, and then continue down to the bottom. Head right and
then go up at the junction. Go up a little way and take the stairs. Go up,
left, down and then right around the spiral, then go up at the next corner.
Head up through the small room and then into the next one. Collect the
STAR-DEW from the right of this room, then go up and out of it. Head left
all the way along the passage, then down at the end. At the bottom of this

corridor go left again, then up, right and then down. Ascend the staircase.

Go down to the junction and turn left, heading up at the corner that
follows. Keep going up, then turn right at the top and then up to use the
next staircase. Head down the passage to the junction, taking the right
path this time. Go up when you reach the corner, and follow the corridor
to the end, turning a little left and then up to take another staircase.

Head up a short way, then turn right at the junction. Go down at the next
corner, and continue down to another junction. Turn left here, then go
down and ascend the very last staircase. Follow the passage down and go
left at the junction. Head up when you reach the corner, and continue all
the way to the top, ignoring the path to your right en route. Go through
the door in this small room, then equip Wren with his PLSMLAUNCH.

Go a little up, then walk over to the right and stand in front of the next
doorway. Heal up all the characters, then head through the door. Walk up
across the thin bridge between the chasms, then take the ECLPSTORCH from
the box in the centre of the platform. Chaz realizes it is a fake, and you
are automatically flung into battle (you'll also discard the ECLPSTORCH).

Don't worry - it's only a Spector. Defeat it quickly and painlessly, then
your true adversary appears. This huge, dark figure will hobble towards
the party, and notice that Lutz has finally come. It appears to be Lashiec,
as Rune points out, and Lashiec continues by saying that he has waited for
this moment for so long. Rune asks why Lashiec is reincarnated, and Lashiec
replies that it is for revenge. He then vows that Lutz, and all who are
helping him, will suffer endless pain, and that he will kill them all. He
says that he will make them tortured souls like him, who can never leave
the castle. Chaz asks if that's why Lashiec lured them there, and Lashiec
replies that he has waited two thousand years to cut their throats. This
instigates the next boss battle.


```
 __________
```

| BOSS #13 \____________  ____________________


```
| Lashiec               ||                    |
|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|| Recommended Level: | 
|  HP: 6383             ||                    |
| EXP: 29999  MST: 1    || Wren: 34-35       /
|                       || Chaz: 36-37      /
| Weak: Fire,Engy,Light || Rika: 39-40     /
| Res:  Water           || Kyra: 34-35    /
| Imm:  -               || Rune: 34-35   /
|                       ||              /
```

Although he is on his own, Lashiec will be more of a threat than all three
of the Xe-A-Thouls. However, he is just one opponent and therefore very
susceptible to your party's best single-target attacks.

In the first round, get Chaz to use RAYBLADE, have Rika use SANER, let
Rune throw out an EFESS, have Wren set up a BARRIER, and get Kyra to use
WARLA. This should set up a decent defence and also start the offensive
against Lashiec.

Lashiec will use one of a few different Skills to begin with - either
THNDHALBRT or ANOTHRGATE (both of which are powerful hit-all Skills, the
latter being the most damaging), or POSSESSION (a single-target Skill that
inflicts Sleep on one character). In the following rounds, have Chaz keep
using RAYBLADE (or NATHU when this runs out), get Rika to use GISAR or
NARES (depending on who was damaged in the round before), get Rune to
continue using EFESS (or NAFOI when this runs out), let Wren just attack
(or use RECOVER if he needs HP), and keep Krya using NAFOI (or GIRES or
a curative item if you need a little extra healing).

Once Lashiec gets to 1/4 HP, he will use REINFORCE, which increases all of
his statistics. This makes him that extra bit tougher, but indicates that
he's almost down. Keep using the above strategy, putting a little more
emphasis on healing if you need it, or letting Rika use DBLSLASH if there
is no healing to be done.

If any of your characters go down, get a fast character to use REVER or a
MOON-DEW, and follow this up with a slower character using GIRES or a
DIMATE or TRIMATE. Alternatively, just use a SOL-DEW or a REPAIR-KIT.

Keep pummelling Lashiec and maintaining your party's HP levels, and this
ancient king will be dethroned in about six or seven rounds.
Lashiec curses Lutz, raising a bright blue sphere above his head, and adds
that although Lutz has defeated him he will never get the Eclipse Torch.
Quick as a flash, Rika dives over Lashiec and grabs the Torch from him.
Kyra announces that they've done it, and Lashiec begins to dissolve. As
he melts away, Lashiec shouts that even now he will not die, and will
continue to be reincarnated again and again. He adds that he must continue
to serve 'Him', then he turns to dust. Wren reports that the Air Castle is
crumbling, so Chaz gets them out of there and they fly off in the Landale.

<a id="s6-4-7"></a>

### 6.4.7. Slash and Burn

Starting Party: Wren , Chaz , Rika , Kyra , Rune
Starting Level: 35   , 37   , 39-40, 35-36, 34-35
The Air Castle explodes as the Landale heads into space, and Wren warns the
party of a shock wave. It passes unnoticed, then Rune expresses his opinion
of Lashiec. He thinks that Lashiec is pretty pathetic, being seduced by an
enormous power and ending up a mere puppet. Chaz asks Rune who the 'He' was
that Lashiec mentioned, and Rika proposes that it was Dark Force. The party
then return to Dezolis.

Back in Gumbious Temple, the Desolisian priest is very pleased that the
party have recovered the Eclipse Torch, and he has no qualms about lending
it to them. Chaz then announces that they are going to the forest of
carnivorous trees. The ECLPSTORCH will now be in your inventory.

First, remove the PLSMLAUNCH from Wren and reequip him with the PULSEVULCN.
You haven't had the opportunity to heal the party yet, so teleport to Meese
and spend the night at it's hostelry. Also, buy any required items that you
may be lacking from your trek through the Air Castle, such as TRIMATEs and
status-curing medicines. By now, your party should already be as powerful
as it really needs to be for the next area you will visit, so you won't
have to get any more EXP before you continue.

Leave Meese and jump into the Ice Digger. Head north and then east, going
through the gap in the mountains that leads to the carnivorous trees. Head
north and the party will get out of the vehicle just before the forest.

Chaz holds the Eclipse Torch aloft, and its intense light burns the trees
to ash. Rika cheers, and Kyra comments on the long mission you have
accomplished. Chaz suggests that the party now goes to the Garuberk Tower,
so head north and save just outside the tall tree-like structure. This is
the Garuberk Tower, so go inside.

<a id="s6-4-8"></a>

> 🥈 **Purified Planet** — Dispel the evil of Garuberk Tower. _(RetroAchievements · 10 pts)_
> 🥉 **Towering Silence** — Investigate the Tower of Silence. _(RetroAchievements · 3 pts)_


### 6.4.8. A Living Tower

Starting Party: Wren , Chaz , Rika , Kyra , Rune
Starting Level: 35   , 37   , 39-40, 35-36, 34-35


```
 // DUNGEON #19 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\
```

|/  Garuberk Tower         \_________________________________
   Enemies: DarkMaraud, D-Elm-Lars, Ghoul, Hakenleft, King Saber,
            Radhin
  Treasure: TRIMATE, POW-SHIELD, TRIMATE, MOONSLASHR, STAR-DEW,
            MOON-DEW, ESCAPIPE, STAR-DEW
 \
  \   Boss: Dark Force
   \______________________________

You will be inside a stangely organic chamber. In fact, the entire tower is
organic, with different styles on different floors. It can be a little
confusing at first, but it really isn't as bad as it seems to be.

Head up and left across the snowy chamber, continuing up and around to the
right. There is a light flesh-coloured column in the wall. This functions
as an elevator, so use it as such.

There is nothing of any value in the area below you (except clear slime),
so go right and then up and around to the left. Continue left until you see
an eye protruding from the ground. Examine this and the whole floor will
tremble and make an odd noise. Walk up a little bit and collect the TRIMATE
from the right of the small room (you may need to look closely as the
chests are a little harder to spot in this dungeon).

Go back down and then head right. You will notice that touching the eye has
caused an opening to appear in the right wall, so continue through to the
right and then downwards. Head down and right, ignoring the junction to the
left for the moment, then walk all the way down to the bottom to retrieve
the POW-SHIELD. Return up the corridor then take the left turn you just
passed. Enter the elevator in the top wall.

Make your way down, heading straight past the passage to your right, and
continue all the way to the bottom right of the chamber, weaving in and out
of the green tubes. Pick up another TRIMATE, then go back up to the path
leading to the right. Continue right from here, then up, right and down,
then go left at the following junction. Ignore the next elevator you come
to, and head down, right and then up to use the elevator here instead.

This room is a dead end, and filled with green tubes. Go down around the
tubes and pick up the concealed MOONSLASHR from the bottom left. Equip this
to Kyra alongside one of the LACOSLASHRs, then return to the elevator. Go
back down, left and then up, and ascend in the elevator you passed earlier.

Head right, then go up and right along the corridor until you reach a
junction. Turn upwards, then turn left at the following junction to pick up
a STAR-DEW from the left side of the small room that follows. Go out of
this room and continue leftwards along the passage, turning down at the
corner. Head all the way to the bottom of the passage, turning a little
left along the way, then go around to the left and up to another elevator.
Enter it to get to the floor above.

Go right again, heading up and right until you get to a crossroad. Go down
a little from here and pick up the MOON-DEW, then return to the crossroad
and continue upwards (the right path is a dead end). Continue upwards and
leftwards until you reach a goo-plastered chamber. Use the elevator in the
top wall to go up yet another floor.

Walk a little to the left, then follow the passageway all the way around
upwards, left, down and then right until you reach a junction. Turn up into
the small chamber and collect the ESCAPIPE from the top right corner. Go
back down to the junction and continue to the right, heading up and then
left. Pass the first elevator you meet on the wall above, then head around
and then up, and take the second elevator just to the right.

In this small room, go to the bottom left and use the eye switch. This will
open up a room in the floor above. Once you have done this, ascend in the
elevator again and go back round to the one below that you ignored just
now. Take it to the floor below, then head a little down and then left.
Follow the corridor leftwards and upwards, then turn right at the corner
and continue upwards to another elevator. Enter it.

You are now in a large chamber, although the left part of it would have
been sealed before you activated the second eye. Head left to the newly
available elevator, and take it up to the final floor. Head down and then
into the corridor on the left, and procure the STAR-DEW from the bottom
corner before returning to the main passage. The path below is a dead end,
so head up and follow the passage until you see a weird creature occupying
the top wall. Before approaching, heal the party (you may even wish to
teleport out of the Tower, rest and then save first). Once you are ready,
equip the PLSMLAUNCH to Wren and then walk up to the creature.

The party will stop just before the monster, and Rika will ask if it is
Dark Force. Rune will reply that it is, but Wren will report that it is
nothing like anything they found on Kuran. Rika supposes there were two
Dark Forces, and Chaz adds that Raja was right about this one creating
havoc on Dezolis. Rune tells him that it is not just Dezolis, but that Dark
Force is destroying the whole Algo system. Wren informs the party that Dark
Force senses their presence, and it then attacks.


```
 __________
```

| BOSS #14 \____________  ____________________


```
| Dark Force            ||                    |
|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|| Recommended Level: | 
|  HP: 7524             ||                    |
| EXP: 46383  MST: 1    || Wren: 36          /
|                       || Chaz: 38-39      /
| Weak: Energy,Light    || Rika: 40-41     /
| Res:  -               || Kyra: 36-37    /
| Imm:  -               || Rune: 35      /
|                       ||              /
```

This version of Dark Force is a lot more powerful than the one you met in
Kuran, but so are the characters. Regardless of this, however, the battle
will be more difficult than the first one.

In the first round, get Chaz to use his RAYBLADE, let Rika use SANER, have
Rune fire his new LEGEON, get Wren to set up a BARRIER, and have Kyra use
WARLA. This will set up the party for the following rounds, ensuring Dark
Force acts last, and also scratch the surface of Dark Force's HP total.

Dark Force has a different range of abilities this time, including a Skill
that sends a character to Sleep (EVIL EYE), a very damaging beam that hits
one character (SHDWBREATH), and a powerful hit-all attack (LIGHTSHOWR).

Hopefully, Wren will be able to set up his BARRIER before Dark Force uses
SHDWBREATH or LIGHTSHOWR, or you may find that you receive a crippling
amount of damage (including the possibility of immediate flat-lining).

In the following rounds, keep Chaz using RAYBLADE (or NATHU when he runs
out), let Rika use either SAR or GISAR following a LIGHTSHOWR (don't use
NASAR as it will not be necessary at this stage of the game), or GIRES or
NARES following SHDWBREATH, have Rune use EFESS (or NAWAT once the supply
is depleted), get Wren to attack or use RECOVER if needed, and let Kyra use
NAFOI or provide some additional healing. If the organic members of your
party do not need healing, have Rika add to the offence by using DBLSLASH.

If any of the party fall, follow the usual fast character revival and slow
character healing strategy, or use a SOL-DEW if you need to revive quickly.

Try not to let a character's HP stay below half their maximum total, as
there is the possibility that a single attack from Dark Force may knock
them down. Also, if any of the characters succumb to Dark Force's EVIL EYE,
let wake up naturally (don't use Rune's AROWS as this will waste his turn).

Stay offensive and heal quickly, and you'll find that the battle will be
over in around eight to ten rounds.

<a id="s6-4-9"></a>

### 6.4.9. End of the Blizzard

Starting Party: Wren , Chaz , Rika , Kyra , Rune
Starting Level: 36-37, 39   , 41-42, 36-37, 36
Following Dark Force's second annihilation, the Garuberk Tower shatters
before your very eyes. Rune tell's Chaz that they've done it, and Rika
announces that the storm is over. The sky clears and Rune notes that the
Black Energy Wave has stopped. He also guesses that the patients in Meese
will already be recovering. Kyra sighs that it's over, and thanks the party
for all their help, realizing it was presumptious of her to think she could
do it alone. She decides to return to Meese to help with the work that's
still to be done and bids farewell to Chaz, embarrassing him by saying that
he's like a baby brother. She then says goodbye to Lutz, commenting that he
wasn't as she expected but he lived up to his name. Kyra then leaves.

Chaz is still dwelling on being called Kyra's baby brother, and wonders if
he is still so undependable. Rune reassures him that he has improved, but
that Chaz is still a lot like him. The two of them joke around a little,
when suddenly there is a huge explosion beyond the mountains. Rika realizes
that it is Gumbious Temple. Chaz is confused, noting that they have beaten
Dark Force, and Rune suggests they find out what's going on.

> **Kyra leaves the party**


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

The snowstorm is no more, but a new problem has now arisen. Before finding
out what happened to Gumbious Temple, take the PLSMLAUNCH from Wren and
return the PULSEVULCN to him, then teleport or drive to Reshel. Now that
the blizzard is over, this village has been partially rebuilt. Go in.

________


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\
Reshel  |Armour Store   |LACO-HELM   13800 MST|  +22 ATK                  /
_______/|               |LACO-CROWN  15000 MST|  +19 ATK                  \
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|               |LACOCIRCLT   9600 MST|  +12 ATK   +4 MTL         \
        |               |LACO-MAIL   43800 MST|  +64 ATK                  /
        |               |LACOSHIELD  20400 MST|  +29 ATK                  \
        |_______________|_____________________|___________________________/
```

This will be your last, and definitely most expensive, equipment shopping
trip in the game. All of the remaining equipment that is available for the
characters will be acquired from treasure chests and dropped by enemies in
later dungeons. Purchase a LACO-HELM for Chaz, a LACO-CROWN for Rika, a
LACOCIRCLT for Rune, and two LACO-MAILs for Chaz and Rika. This will come
to the incredible total of 126000 Mesetas, which should be quite easily
affordable after traipsing through Air Castle and the Garuberk Tower.

Sell every possible piece of equipment that is left over, except for the
PLSMLAUNCH, then stay at the Inn to recover from your fight with Dark
Force. When you are prepared, leave Reshel.

It is also worth noting that the Meese Perfume Store is now open as well.
You will find it in the northeast corner of town:

________


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\
Meese   |Perfume Store  |MOON-DEW     5000 MST /
_______/|               |STAR-DEW    10000 MST /
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|               |SOL-DEW     20000 MST \
        |_______________|______________________/
```

Once you have finished shopping and have refreshed the party, use RYUKA or
a TELEPIPE to GUMBIOUS, or get in the Ice Digger and drive to Gumbious
Temple. You will not find a large church, but a large hole in the ground.
Drop into the hole.

<a id="s6-4-10"></a>

### 6.4.10. Return to Motavia

Starting Party: Wren , Chaz , Rika , Rune
Starting Level: 36-37, 39   , 41-42, 36
Walk north and through the door. You will find a secret, underground
worship site. Approach the very old Dezolisian sitting on the raised
platform, and he will speak to you. He will introduce himself as the bishop
of Gumbious Temple, which had stood for two thousand years. Rune asks him
what's going on, and Rika will add that the temple has disappeared without
a trace. Chaz tells the bishop that they've defeated Dark Force, and asks
if that isn't enough. The bishop replies that 'The Profound Darkness'
still exists, adding that it is the root of all evil, causing death and
destruction since long ago. Apparently, Dark Force is merely a tool in this
existence. This doesn't sound good. The bishop continues that Dark Force
had come to Dezolis to find the location of Rykros. Chaz asks what this is,
and the bishop tells him it is something that is beyond the party's
control, and that it is the reason why the Profound Darkness stirs. He
explains that if the Profound Darkness cannot get hold of Rykros, it will
not allow the party to get it.

Rune asks what Rykros is, and Chaz adds that he can't understand how
something could be so important that they must scramble to find it. The
bishop replies that Rykros is the place where all the secret answers lie,
but the party do not understand. He then confesses that he does not know
what or where Rykros is, but he does know that when Rykros returns, the
Aero-Prism will light the way. Rune has heard of this artifact, and tells
the party that the first-generation Lutz stored the Aero-Prism in a place
called Soldiers' Temple on Motavia. Chaz notes that this is in the lake
near Krup, and Wren adds that he will contact Demi to arrange a vehicle
capable of crossing water. Chaz thanks the bishop and tells him that they
will return the Eclipse Torch. The bishop then asks if they will go to
Rykros, and Chaz replies that they will. To this, the bishop adds that he
has done his part, and that it is now up to the party to shape history.

The party automatically board the Landale and fly to Motavia. They enter
the Spaceport, and Demi (calling from Nurvus) welcomes Wren. He asks about
the condition of Motavia, and Demi reports that it is still on hold. She
adds that everything Wren requested is on standby, and Wren compliments her
on her efficiency. Demi is very grateful for this praise, and unveils the
Hydrofoil, explaining that it has been taken from the Machine Centre and
completely overhauled. Wren tells them that they can now cross water, and
Rune proposes that they go straight to the Soldiers' Temple. Chaz asks if
Demi is ready to go, but she tells him that it will still be some time
before Motavia's systems are running normally again. Rika says that it's a
pity, but wishes Demi the best of luck.

You now have unlimited use of the Hydrofoil, and you can use it at any
point outside. It is much faster than both the Land Rover and the Ice
Ice Digger, but it is the least powerful of the three. In addition to this,
the Hydrofoil can cross water. Select HYDROFOIL to enter the vehicle.

Once you have been given the Hydrofoil, the remaining four Hunters' Guild
jobs become available. The first three of these can be carried out at your
leisure, but if you want to complete the last job (and acquire Wren's best
weapon, armour and Skill), you will need to do it before getting ELSYDEON.
See '7.1.5. Stain in Life', '7.1.6. Dying Boy', '7.1.7. Man with twist' and
'7.1.8. Silver Soldier' for more details.

It will probably be a good idea to get these jobs done now, as you really
should get all the characters up to at least Level 38 before attempting the
next section of the quest. You should be aiming to get Chaz up to Level 41
or 42, Rika should be around Level 43 or 44, Rune should be at Level 38,
and Wren should be around Level 38 or 39. If you don't want to do the jobs,
head over to Monsen and take out some Sand Worms to get the EXP you need.

Once you have got the Levels you need, teleport to Krup and jump into your
new Hydrofoil. Head east across the water and get out of the vehicle on the
small island. On top of the island is the Soldiers' Temple, but you've got
to get the party up there first.

<a id="s6-5"></a>

> 🥉 **Falz into Darkness** — Defeat a rare enemy at The Edge. _(RetroAchievements · 5 pts)_


## 6.5. Stare into Darkness

<a id="s6-5-1"></a>

> 🥈 **A Path to the Stars** — Recover the Aero-Prism and escape the Soldier's Temple. _(RetroAchievements · 10 pts)_


### 6.5.1. Trip to the Temple

Starting Party: Wren , Chaz , Rika , Rune
Starting Level: 38-39, 41-42, 43-44, 38
Try to enter the cave and a cut-scene will begin.

A man will be standing at the entrance to the cave, and will ask if the
party are there to inspect the ruins. Chaz will reply that they are (sort
of), and ask the man who he is. He apologises for not saying his name
earlier, and introduces himself as Seth, a travelling archaeologist. He
tells the party that he is looking for the ruins of an ancient temple, but
that monsters inhabit the cave that leads to it. Chaz tells Seth that the
temple is exactly where they're going, and Seth thinks this very fortunate.
Seth requests if he can accompany the party, pointing out that he has
confidence in his skills. Chaz wonders how an archaeologist can be of any
help, but Wren adds that there is strength in numbers. Chaz accepts, and
Seth is extremely grateful. Rika comments to Rune on how nice and polite
Seth is, but Rune's mind seems to be elsewhere.

> **Seth joins the party (Level 35)**


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

Feel free to use as many of any of Seth's Skills during this dungeon, as he
won't be needing them for the boss fight at the end. Also, don't bother
healing his damage or reviving him. In fact, you may choose to kill him off
as soon as possible, as any share of the EXP that he takes will be wasted.
However you play Seth, make sure to put him at the front of the party so
that he absorbs most of the damage.


```
Recommended       |   Seth   | * Wren * |   Chaz   |   Rika   |   Rune   |
Equipment   |¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|
            |Head |LACOCIRCLT|ELST-GEAR |LACO-HELM |LACO-CROWN|LACOCIRCLT|
            |Right|LACODAGGER|PULSEVULCN|LACO-SWORD|SILVR-TUSK|SILVSHIELD|
            |Left |RFLCSHIELD| /2-HAND  | /2-HAND  |LACO-CLAW |SILVSHIELD|
            |Body |CYBER-SUIT|ELST-ARMOR|LACO-MAIL |LACO-MAIL |RFLC-ROBE |
```

*If the Silver Soldier mission has been completed, Wren's
             equipment should be LACO-GEAR, PULSEVULCN and LACO-ARMOR.

Once you are prepared, save the game then enter the cave.


```
  ______________
 // DUNGEON #20 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\
```

|/  Island Cave            \_________________________________
   Enemies: Flame Newt, Fract Ooze, Jr.Ooze, Shrieker
  Treasure: ESCAPIPE, SOL-DEW, TRIMATE, MOON-DEW, STAR-DEW
Head right straight away, then turn up when you get to the small ledge at
the end. Pick up the ESCAPIPE, then go down towards the wall. Walk left,
all the way along the bottom path, until you reach the left wall. Continue
up and left, ignoring both junctions to the right, until you reach a set of
steps leading up to a staircase. Go up and ascend to the floor above.

Go right and up into the large chamber, and procure the SOL-DEW from just
below the top wall. Head down and then back left to the stairs. Take them,
then go down the steps. Head right, up, right and down around the water,
then continue right, ignoring the steps above for the moment. Head up
again, then turn right at the top. Keep going right, making your way around
the ledge jutting out from the top wall, and then go through the doorway at
the end. Cross the room and descend the stairs at the top. Head left along
this small ledge, and pick up the TRIMATE from the end, then return back
to the floor above.

Return down out of the room, then go back left, down, and then left to be
below the steps you ignored just now. Head up the steps, and continue to
top to ascend the stairs. Seth will express his amazement at the party's
strength, pointing out that they must have felled many monsters, and Chaz
gets a little embarrassed.

Head to the right, ignoring the path below you en route, and continue all
the way along the corridor to the end. Grab the MOON-DEW, then head back to
the corridor you passed earlier. Head down to the next junction, and turn
left. Go down at the corner and pick up the STAR-DEW at the bottom. Go back
up again, then walk back to the left. Go through the gap at the top of the
wall to the left, then take the first path down. There are a few passages
and a staircase around this area, but none of these contains anything.
Instead, turn left when you can, and then continue going left until you hit
the wall at the end. Go left and down, then continue down to the corner,
where you should go right. Take the stairs.

Seth marvels at the party's abilities again, wishing that he had that kind
of strength. Chaz explains that it is the result of many hours training,
and tells Seth that he could be that strong if he put the effort into it.
Seth thinks about this, and Rika asks when Chaz ever did any training.

Follow the passage to the right, then turn up at the junction. Cross the
large chamber that follows, and go through the door at the top. You are now
outside at the top of the cave. Seth announces that they are at the temple,
and gives all credit to the party. He says there may still be monsters, and
asks to accompany the party just a little further. Chaz complies.

Remove all the equipment from Seth, as he will have no further use of it,
then head a little left and then up across the plateau. Walk up to enter
the temple at the top, then go around either left or right and up towards
the top of the room. Head down the steps in the middle and stop just before
the chest. Heal the party completely (not Seth), then open the chest. You
will acquire the AERO-PRISM.

Chaz announces his discovery, but asks how it will show the way to Rykros.
Rune replies that he has no idea, and Chaz sarcastically comments that he
is a big help. Walk up the steps and then around to the bottom of the
temple. Equip Wren's best single-target weapon (PLSMLAUNCH or PHOTNERASR),
then walk on out to begin a cut-scene.

The Aero-Prism suddenly becomes intensely radiant. Chaz comments on this,
and Rune tells him to hold the Aero-Prism to the sky. Chaz does this, and
a brilliant beam of light points directly upwards through the clouds. Chaz
asks what's going on, and Rune tells him that Rykros is at the end of the
light. Wren begins to calculate its direction, and Seth suddenly screams in
pain, clutching his face. Rika asks what's wrong, but Seth doesn't seem in
a position to answer. He continues screaming as he seems to be ripped apart
from the inside. A moment later, where Seth stood is now occupied by a
horrifying yet familiar figure. Rika sees that it is Dark Force, and Rune
is shocked to realise that Dark Force had been masquerading as a human.
Wren wonders if Dark Force can also evolve, but there doesn't seem time to
answer this question before the final battle with Dark Force begins.

> **Seth leaves the party**

| BOSS #15 \____________  ____________________


```
| Dark Force            ||                    |
|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|| Recommended Level: | 
|  HP: 8240             ||                    |
| EXP: 49999  MST: 1    || Wren: 38-39       /
|                       || Chaz: 41-42      /
| Weak: Energy,Light    || Rika: 43-44     /
| Res:  -               || Rune: 38       /
| Imm:  -               ||               /
|                       ||              /
```

The final manifestation of Dark Force is far more humanoid than its
predecessors. It is also the most powerful of the three. Even using the
strategy below, you may find this battle considerably difficult, as you
only have four characters available.

In the first round, set up the standard defence by getting Chaz to use his
RAYBLADE, having Rika increase the party's Agility by using SANER, letting
Rune let loose an EFESS, and having Wren set up a BARRIER. Hopefully, Wren
will create the BARRIER before Dark Force uses a damaging Skill, else one
or all of the characters will take a severe beating.

Dark Force has exactly the same Skills that Seth had (except DTHSPELL),
including CORRSION (this hit-all Skill is far more powerful this time),
SHADOWBIND (reducing the Agility of all organic characters) and MINDBLST
(a hit-all Skill that may inflict Sleep on each character). It also has a
normal, fairly damaging, attack.

In the second round, get Chaz to use RAYBLADE again, have Rika use DEBAN,
get Rune to unleash another EFESS, and have Wren just attack normally. If
the party need healing in this round, get Wren to use a STAR-DEW instead of
attacking. If only one character is injured, let him use a TRIMATE or his
RECOVER Skill.

In the following rounds, keep Chaz using RAYBLADE (or NATHU when this runs
out), let Rika take over the healing by using SAR, GISAR or GIRES (or NASAR
or NARES if necessary), have Rune use EFESS (or LEGEON or NAWAT when you
run out), and get Wren to attack or use RECOVER on himself.

As usual, let Rika throw out a DBLSLASH if no healing needs to be done, and
do not use AROWS if any characters fall asleep. After all, it is likely
that any characters that don't wake up immediately will wake up in the next
round. Using AROWS would just be a waste of a chance to use one of Rune's
powerful offensive spells.

If Rika falls asleep and there is healing to be done, get Wren to cover for
her by using a STAR-DEW or a TRIMATE, or let Chaz use one of his curative
Techniques if you are low on items.

Try to keep every characters' HP above half their maximum value at all
times, and if one of your party members is flatlined, follow the standard
fast/slow revival strategy or use a SOL-DEW or a REPAIR-KIT.

A little more care may need to be taken in this battle, as Dark Force's
Sleep-inflicting Skill may take characters out of commission for a round or
two on a fairly regular basis. It may be necessary to postpone attacking
Dark Force for an entire round if healing needs to be done.

This battle will very likely take a lot longer than any of the previous
boss battles, and possibly use a few items in the process, but if you keep
the characters at a safe HP level, it should all be over in around ten to
thirteen rounds.
Dark Force explodes in his usual dramatic way, and you can rest assured
that you won't be meeting him again. Rune thinks the situation is becoming
a bit sticky, and suggests that they go to Rykros as quickly as possible.
Chaz doesn't understand the hurry, but Rune explains that the followers of
Darkness are probably already aware of the location of Rykros through Dark
Force. Wren points out that they only know the direction of Rykros, but he
admits that there must be something there that the Darkness doesn't want
them to have. Chaz says that they had best get it, and Rika adds that they
will have to hurry before they are beaten to it. Wren reports that he has
the direction of Rykros stored in memory, but the distance is undetermined.
Rune proposes that they just head towards it in the Landale, so Chaz
decides to return to the Spaceport.

<a id="s6-5-2"></a>

### 6.5.2. No Turning Back

Starting Party: Wren , Chaz , Rika , Rune
Starting Level: 39   , 41-42, 44-45, 38-39
At this point, the village of Reshel is fully repaired. You can now return
there at any point and make use of its additional facilities:

________


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\
Reshel  |Inn            |Per person    130 MST /
_______/|_______________|______________________/
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\
        |Tool Store     |TRIMATE       400 MST /
        |               |ANTIDOTE       10 MST \
        |               |CURE-PARAL    120 MST /
```
