```
        |               |TELEPIPE      130 MST \
        |               |ESCAPIPE       70 MST \
        |_______________|______________________/
```

Teleport to Kadary and head down to the Spaceport. Don't bother with the
Regen Platforms, and instead head up to the Landale. Select Rykros as the
destination (suitably unmarked on the map), and watch the launch. Shortly
after, a cut-scene begins.

Chaz asks if they are going in the right direction, and Wren confirms that
they are on the correct course. Chaz wonders if it is a structure like the
Air Castle or an artificial satellite, but Wren simply responds that if
they stay on their current heading they will soon leave the Algo system.
Rune insists that they have to keep going, and Chaz remains astounded. At
that moment, the Aero-Prism flashes, and a green planet appears in front of
the Landale. Wren announces this, and Rune notices that it is not apparent
on the radar. Wren informs them that the planet is neither Motavia, Dezolis
or Parma, and that the planet is not recorded in his database. It is Chaz
who realises that it must be Rykros, and so they land on this new planet.

Arriving inside a strange building, the party head out of the Landale and
into a crystal chamber. They walk up to a glowing symbol in the centre of
the floor, and the room disappears around them into a starry deep-space
backdrop. The image of a galaxy appears below their feet, and a hidden
voice welcomes them, calling them Protectors. Chaz wonders what is going
on, and the source of the voice introduces itself as Le Roof of Rykros. It
explains that it remains on the planet to pass on the story of the genesis
of Algo. Chaz notes that he was right about the planet being Rykros, and Le
Roof confirms that it is, stating that it is the fourth planet in the Algo
star system. Wren disagrees, reporting that there are only supposed to be
three planets in the system, but Le Roof says that Rykros is protected by
a powerful and invisible barrier that stops any normal being from seeing or
otherwise sensing it. It continues by informing the party that Rykros'
orbit is highly elliptical, only passing near Algo once every thousand
years. Rune recalls the message the Dezolisian bishop gave, that the Aero-
Prism shows the way when Rykros returns, and adds that he now understands
what it meant by 'returns'.

Chaz gets to the point and tells Le Roof that they have come to Rykros to
find out about The Profound Darkness. He asks what it is, why it is
causing the disasters on Algo, and where it is now, and demands that Le
Roof tells them everything. Le Roof thinks for a moment, then says that he
will tell all to the courageous Protectors who had discovered Rykros (the
party), but adds that they must first perform a task. He informs them that
there are two towers on Rykros called The Courage Tower and The Strength
Tower. He charges the party to go and meet the guardians of these towers,
and tells them that he will truly recognise them as 'Protectors' when they
return and will tell them everything they wish to know. Chaz asks if Le
Roof is testing them, and Le Roof replies that it is absolutely necessary.
Chaz realises that they have no choice, so he announces their departure.
Before the party leave, Le Roof finishes by saying that they must hurry,
as the hand of the Darkness is already closing in. He awaits their return.

After the normal surroundings are restored, you will discover that the
symbol the party was standing on is also a Regen Platform. The party is
automatically refreshed, and you have a new planet to explore.

<a id="s6-5-3"></a>

### 6.5.3. The Fourth Planet

Starting Party: Wren , Chaz , Rika , Rune
Starting Level: 39   , 41-42, 44-45, 38-39
You are in a building known as the Silence Temple. Head down from the Regen
Platform and out into the corridor. Continue a little further down until
you reach the junction. The exit from the Silence Temple is below you, but
there are a few items to collect first. Head left, up left and then up, and
pick up the GUARDSHILD in the small room that follows. Next, go up, right,
up and then right into another room, and collect the GUARDSWORD and a
TELEPIPE. Equip this brilliant new sword to Chaz immediately, then continue
right, down, right and then down. Procure a TRIMATE from this last room,
then follow the path down, left, down and then finally left back to the
exit of the temple. Go down and out of the Silence Temple.

Enemies on Rykros (in a vehicle or out): CrminHeads, Cula-Bellr, DeathBearr
The traversible area of Rykros is very small, and contains only four areas
that can be entered. You can go to the Strength Tower and the Courage Tower
in either order you wish, as they will both need to be completed. They are
very similar in nature, and each have exactly the same enemies inside. The
major difference between them is the fact that they have very different
guardians, and because I feel the guardian of the Strength Tower easier
than the guardian of the Courage Tower, I have put them in that order in
the walkthrough.

Before you visit either tower, however, it would be best to get a few EXP
to tip the odds in your favour. Spend a little time on the surface of
Rykros getting Chaz up to around Level 43, Rika up to at least Level 46,
Rune up to Level 40 and Wren up to around 40 or 41. Take note that you will
only receive half as many EXP for defeating an enemy in a vehicle than you
would for defeating the same enemy on foot. Return to the Silence Temple
when you are finished to regenerate the party. 
If you wish to follow the walkthrough exactly and tackle the Strength Tower
first, head directly northwest from the Silence Temple until you find a
secluded area containing red rocks. The largest and most central of these
rocks contains a door at the front. This is the Strength Tower. Save your
game outside, then go in. Follow '6.5.4. Proving Your Strength'.
If you wish to try things a little differently and tackle the Courage Tower
first, go directly east from the Silence Temple until you hit a wall. From
here, head due south and you should spot a large purple rock with a door at
the front, just a little to the east. This is the Courage Tower. Save your
game outside, then go in. Follow '6.5.5. Proving Your Courage'.

<a id="s6-5-4"></a>

> 🥈 **Towering Strength** — Prove yourself in the Tower of Strength. _(RetroAchievements · 10 pts)_


### 6.5.4. Proving Your Strength

Starting Party: Wren , Chaz , Rika , Rune
Starting Level: 40-42, 43-44, 46-48, 40-41


```
 // DUNGEON #21 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\
```

|/  Strength Tower         \_________________________________
   Enemies: Bladeright, BloodSaber, CrminHeads, Dark Witch,
            Hakenleft, Illusionst, Le-Faw-Gan, Twinarms
  Treasure: MOON-DEW, GUARD-ROD, GUARD-CLAW, GUARD-CLAW, MOON-DEW,
            PALMA-RING, MOTA-RING, DEZO-RING
 \
  \   Boss: De-Vars
   \______________________________

Head straight up, ignoring the paths to the left and right, and stop just
before the staircase. Go along the small passage to the left, just above
the stairs, and pick up a MOON-DEW. Return to the right and ascend the
staircase to the next floor. Go left and take another staircase, then head
down to the bottom of the corridor. Ascend the staircase to the right.

Go right along the corridor, then turn up and then right and acquire the
GUARD-ROD. Equip this to Rune if you want, but I would advise keeping the
shields. Go back left and down, then head left. Walk past the staircase and
go up, left and then up again, and turn right at the top corner. Head up
and then right again, and follow the thin passage at the top to the right
to obtain a GUARD-CLAW. Replace Rika's LACO-CLAW with this final model,
then head back left and down, and return down the stairs.

Head back up and take the next staircase to the floor below. Take the path
down between the staircases, and turn right at the bottom. Go up at the
corner, then take the thin passage to your left to get another GUARD-CLAW.
Don't equip this to Rika, as her SILVR-TUSK is far more useful. Instead,
go back to the right then up through the gap in the wall, and ascend the
stairs to your right.

Walk left to the wall, then go up and left and collect the MOON-DEW from
the alcove, then head back right and then down all the way to the bottom.
Continue left and then up, and take the next staircase on the left. Go
right and down, then climb the final stairs to the top floor.

When you arrive, you will see two Gi-Le-Farg witches attacking a large
fiery being. The witches are dispatched quite easily, and control returns
to you. Heal the characters, then equip Wren's best single-target weapon
(PLSMLAUNCH or PHOTNERASR). Speak to the fiery being, and it will inform
the party that they must pass his test. This begins a boss battle.


```
 __________
```

| BOSS #16 \____________  ____________________


```
| De-Vars               ||                    |
|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|| Recommended Level: | 
|  HP: 5499             ||                    |
| EXP: 35000  MST: 1    || Wren: 40-43       /
|                       || Chaz: 43-46      /
| Weak: -               || Rika: 46-49     /
| Res:  -               || Rune: 40-42    /
| Imm:  Fir,Frc,Grv,Lgt ||               /
|                       ||              /
```

The guardian of the Strength Tower, De-Vars is a master of physical combat.
In the first round, have Chaz use RAYBLADE, get Rika to set up DEBAN, let
Rune use LEGEON, and get Wren to just attack normally (a BARRIER would be a
waste of time, as De-Vars doesn't use magical attacks). De-Vars will either
perform a standard attack or unleash a hit-all Skill called DISRUPTARM.

In the following rounds, let Chaz continue using his RAYBLADE (or NATHU if
this is exhausted), get Rika to use GIRES or GISAR (you won't need more
powerful healing than this), get Rune to use LEGEON (or NAWAT if this runs
out), and keep Wren attacking (or use RECOVER if he is low on HP).

As usual, have Rika perform DBLSLASH if there is no organic healing to be
done, and revive fallen characters with the fast-slow method, a SOL-DEW or
a REPAIR-KIT (for Wren).

Follow the strategy above, and De-Vars will concede in around seven or
eight rounds.
De-Vars will admit that the party is better than he thought, and find this
fact comforting. He will allow you to take some objects, stating that they
are the proof that the party needs. Three chests then appear below.

Collect the PALMA-RING, MOTA-RING and DEZO-RING, and equip these to Wren,
Rika and Rune, respectively. Also, replace Wren's PLSMLAUNCH or PHOTNERASR
with the PULSEVULCN again. Now, use HINAS or an ESCAPIPE, or make your way
out of the Strength Tower on foot. Head back to Silence Temple and into the
main chamber. If you have already completed the Courage Tower, follow the
walkthrough from '6.5.6. Genesis of Algo'. Otherwise, head up and use the
Regen Platform to restore the party, then leave the Silence Temple.

Next, go directly east from the Silence Temple until you hit a wall. From
here, head due south and you should spot a large purple rock with a door at
the front, just a little to the east. This is the Courage Tower. Save your
game outside, then go in. Follow '6.5.5. Proving Your Courage'.

<a id="s6-5-5"></a>

> 🥈 **Towering Courage** — Prove yourself in the Tower of Courage. _(RetroAchievements · 10 pts)_


### 6.5.5. Proving Your Courage

Starting Party: Wren , Chaz , Rika , Rune
Starting Level: 40-42, 43-44, 46-48, 40-41


```
 // DUNGEON #22 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\
```

|/  Courage Tower          \_________________________________
   Enemies: Bladeright, BloodSaber, CrminHeads, Dark Witch,
            Hakenleft, Illusionst, Le-Faw-Gan, Twinarms
  Treasure: STAR-DEW, STAR-DEW, GUARD-MAIL, GUARDARMOR,
            GUARD-ROBE, ALGO-RING, RYKR-RING
 \

\   Boss: Sa-Lews
   \______________________________

Go up and then left, and procure a STAR-DEW from the alcove to the left.
Return to the centre of the chamber and continue upwards until you hit the
top wall. From here, head right and then down to ascend the stairs to the
floor above.

Head up, left and then down the passage, ignoring the path on the left near
the top wall. Keep going down until you see a small path to the right. Go
in and pick up another STAR-DEW, then go left, down and left again, then up
to a junction. Ignore the stairs to the left for a moment, and walk up,
right and down, then take the stairs in this small room.

Go up and left, and climb another set of stairs. Head right and then down,
then pick up the GUARD-MAIL from the alcove to the right and the GUARDARMOR
from the area below you. Equip the GUARD-MAIL to Rika (she needs it more
than Chaz), and equip the GUARDARMOR to Wren. Return back up and left to
the stairs, and take them.

Return right and down and take the next staircase, then go back up, left
and down to the junction you were at earlier. Take the left path this time,
and climb the stairs to the next level. Go right, down, right and up, and
acquire the GUARD-ROBE from next to the top wall. Replace Rune's RFLC-ROBE
with this new protection, then go back down, left, up and left, passing the
stairs as you head up the corridor. Turn right at the top, then continue to
the far wall and take the stairs below.

Head left, up, left, and then down at the corner. When you reach the corner
at the bottom, turn right and climb the final staircase.

When you arrive, you will see two BlindHeads attacking a large being made
blue fire. The StoneHeads are dispatched quite easily, and control returns
to you. Heal the characters, then equip Wren's best single-target weapon
(PLSMLAUNCH or PHOTNERASR). Speak to the fiery being, and it will inform
the party that they must pass his test. This begins a boss battle.


```
 __________
```

| BOSS #17 \____________  ____________________


```
| Sa-Lews               ||                    |
|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|| Recommended Level: | 
|  HP: 5499             ||                    |
| EXP: 35000  MST: 1    || Wren: 40-43       /
|                       || Chaz: 43-46      /
| Weak: -               || Rika: 46-49     /
| Res:  -               || Rune: 40-42    /
| Imm:  Fir,Frc,Grv,Lgt ||               /
|                       ||              /
```

The guardian of the Courage Tower, Sa-Lews is a master of magical combat.
In the first round, have Chaz use CROSSCUT, get Rika to use SANER, let Rune
use LEGEON, and get Wren to set up his BARRIER.

Sa-Lews will use a number of Rune's Skills, including FLAELI, HEWN, TANDLE
and LEGEON. As three of these are hit-all Skills, you may be in for a tough
time in this battle.

In the following rounds, let Chaz continue using his CROSSCUT, get Rika to
use GIRES or GISAR (you may need to use NASAR following some of Sa-Lews
attacks), get Rune to use LEGEON (or NAWAT if this runs out), and keep Wren
attacking (or use RECOVER if he is low on HP).

As usual, have Rika perform DBLSLASH if there is no organic healing to be
done, and revive fallen characters with the fast-slow method, a SOL-DEW or
a REPAIR-KIT (for Wren).

Follow the strategy above, and Sa-Lews will concede in around seven or
eight rounds.
Sa-Lews will admit that the party has done well, and ask that they take
some objects as proof that they have met and passed Sa-Lews. Two chests
then appear below.

Collect the ALGO-RING and the RYKR-RING, and equip the former to Chaz.
Also, replace Wren's PLSMLAUNCH or PHOTNERASR with the PULSEVULCN again.
Now, use HINAS or an ESCAPIPE, or make your way out of the Courage Tower on
foot. Head back to Silence Temple and into the main chamber. If you have
already completed the Strength Tower, follow the walkthrough from '6.5.6.
Genesis of Algo'. Otherwise, head up and use the Regen Platform to fully
restore the party, then leave the Silence Temple.

Next, head directly northwest from the Silence Temple until you find a
secluded area containing red rocks. The largest and most central of these
rocks contains a door at the front. This is the Strength Tower. Save your
game outside, then go in. Follow '6.5.4. Proving Your Strength'.

<a id="s6-5-6"></a>

### 6.5.6. Genesis of Algo

Starting Party: Wren , Chaz , Rika , Rune
Starting Level: 42-43, 45-46, 48-49, 41-42
The party will automatically walk up onto the Regen Platform as before. The
temple will fade into the starry background again, and Le Roof will appear. 
He will congratulate the Protectors on having completed the missions well,
and adds that he can now enlighten them with the secret of Algo's genesis.

It begins billions of years ago, when a spiritual life form split into two
lesser beings, who eventually began to fight. After a long and terrible
battle, there emerged a victor. The winner banished the enemy spritual
life form to another dimension. Le Roof adds that they call the victorious
side The Great Light, and the defeated one The Profound Darkness. However,
The Great Light feared The Profound Darkness' return, and placed a seal
over the dimensional portal, consisting of three planets orbitting a fixed
star. This seal has become known as the Algo solar system.

Le Roof continues that The Great Light distributed Protectors between the
three tribes of Algo - the Parmanians, the Motavians and the Dezolisians.
Unfortunately, there were fluctuations in the strength of the seal, meaning
that it would be at its weakest once every thousand years. As a warning of
this phenomenon, The Great Light created Rykros, which would return every
thousand years, and himself, Le Roof. Chaz asks, rightly, how an invisible
planet can be any kind of warning, and Le Roof continues that the mission
would be forgotten by the generations of Protectors over a thousand years.
He then adds that Rykros was meant to break its silence when the seal's
final moment came, to remind the Protectors of the mission they were born
to do. Rika asks what Le Roof means by 'final moment', so Le Roof explains
that, throughout time, The Profound Darkness has seethed with animosity and
the need for revenge. He adds that, once every thousand years when the seal
is at its weakest, the most intense part of The Profound Darkness' spirit
is able to break through the portal and come to Algo in physical form. Rune
understands that this is Dark Force, and Le Roof continues. He tells the
party that every time Dark Force appeared, a courageous person would defeat
it, and bring about a brief period of peace. However, The Profound Darkness
is patient, and it eventually managed to destroy the planet Parma, removing
part of the seal.

Now, a thousand years later, The Profound Darkness is trying to free itself
completely. Chaz asks if that is what is happening now, but Le Roof just
replies that it may be. Rika questions this response, and Le Roof clarifies
it by saying that either The Profound Darkness will free itself completely,
or someone will conquer the Darkness and render the seal meaningless. Chaz
knows that someone means them. Le Roof then tells the Protectors that, if
The Profound Darkness escapes, the entirety of Algo will certainly be
destroyed. The only way to prevent this is to go to the Darkness' dimension
and destroy it. He explains that, as long as the party has the Rings of the
Stars, they will be able to withstand the strongest part of the Darkness.
He tells the party that the time has come, and to obey the will of The
Great Light by destroying The Profound Darkness, pointing out that it is
the very mission that they, as Protectors, were born to do. Chaz disagrees.

Chaz asks Le Roof who he thinks they are, insisting that he's not going to
fight for any mission. He also asks where The Great Light is now, and why
it isn't doing anything. Le Roof replies that it is no longer in their
galaxy, but somewhere far away. Chaz gets even madder, stating that The
Great Light just hands down missions and then disappears. He adds that he
doesn't care about Protectors or missions, and that he won't fight for
someone like The Great Light, but live by his own will. Chaz begins to walk
off, and Rika calls out to him. Rune tells him that there is no one single
truth, and Le Roof tells Chaz that now he has set foot on Rykros he must
hurry. He must choose his path.

Back at the Landale, Rika asks Chaz what they are going to do. Chaz doesn't
answer, instead telling Rune that he doesn't know what's going on. He adds
that, when Alys died, Rune explained things to him and Rika tried to lift
his spirits, but he still didn't understand. Chaz adds that all he knew was
that the person who had looked after him and taught him everything had
died. He continues that he would have gladly sacrificed his life for the
peaceful repose of Alys' soul, but gradually he learned that people
depended on him to fight. Rune asks if that isn't fine, but Chaz replies
that he can't have the fate of all Algo rest on his shoulders. He also adds
that the mission is handed down from The Great Light, and if they dance to
its tune they are no different from Zio. Rune understands why Chaz might
think that, and informs him that there is someone he wants Chaz to meet.
He proposes they go to the Esper Mansion.

You will now be at the Algo map screen. Select Dezolis as the destination,
then await your return to this cold planet.

<a id="s6-5-7"></a>

> 🥉 **A Hero's Sword** — Find Elsydeon. _(RetroAchievements · 3 pts)_


### 6.5.7. Sword of the Espers

Starting Party: Wren , Chaz , Rika , Rune
Starting Level: 42-43, 45-46, 48-49, 41-42
If you wish to complete the Silver Soldier job at the Hunter's Guild,
assuming you haven't done so already, then you must do so before continuing
the walkthrough. If you do not, the job will be withdrawn.

Back at the Spaceport, use a Regen Platform then teleport to Esper Mansion.
Save your game, then enter the building. Speak to the guards to get by,
then make your way all around the mansion and into the inner sanctuary.
Descend the stairs into Lutz's room, and the party will automatically head
to the top wall behind the Telepathy Ball. Rune opens a secret door in the
wall, then a cut-scene begins.

Rune informs Chaz that the sacred sword Elsydeon awaits him. Chaz asks what
it is, and Rune tells him that it's probably the only weapon that has the
power to destroy The Profound Darkness. Rune charges Chaz to go, alone, and
meet with Elsydeon, to which Chaz asks if Rune means 'meet'. Rune confirms
this, adding that Chaz should find the answers he is looking for.

> **Rika leaves the party**


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

> **Rune leaves the party**


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

> **Wren leaves the party**


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

You now control Chaz alone. You can speak to Rune to heal Chaz, but you
cannot leave or save your game. Go up through the secret door.


```
  ______________
 // DUNGEON #23 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\
```

|/  Sacred Sword Cave      \_________________________________
   Enemies: Phantom
  Treasure: ELSYDEON
Head up to the top of the passage, then turn to the right. Go down the set
of steps that follows, and keep next to the left wall as you continue down
the corridor. Head a little right at the bottom and take the staircase. Go
up the passageway and up the steps to the statue on top of the raised
platform. Examine it to begin a cut-scene.

The statue is holding what Chaz supposes to be the sacred sword Elsydeon.
Chaz then hears a voice in his head which welcomes him, calling him by
name. The voice continues that Chaz is in the place where the spirits of
those who fought to protect Algo return to, and that Elsydeon is the sword
sheltered by those spirits. The voice tells Chaz to take Elsydeon is his
hands, at which point Chaz has a vision.

He sees a woman fighting what appears to be Dark Force, followed by images
of other people involved in the battles against the Darkness, and the Algo
star system. The vision ends, and the voice confirms that Chaz is the one
that Rune had selected, and that he now understands. An apparition of a
girl appears, and tells Chaz that they entrust Elsydeon to his care, adding
that all their thoughts are in the sword. The voice finishes by saying that
they will be with Chaz, always. Chaz tells them not to worry, and that they
can leave it to him.

<a id="s6-5-8"></a>

### 6.5.8. Holey Disaster

Starting Party: Wren , Chaz , Rika , Rune
Starting Level: 42-43, 45-46, 48-49, 41-42
The next thing you see is Chaz emerging from the cave with Elsydeon. The
rest of the party are still there, and Rune says that Elsydeon promised it
would give Chaz its power and that there was no mistake in his judgment.
Rune then tells Chaz that they should go and save Algo, and Chaz agrees
unhesitatingly, adding that they will protect all life on Algo and free the
world of terror once and for all. Suddenly, Wren reports that there is an
emergency, saying that Demi has informed him that a disaster has just
erupted on Motavia. Chaz proposes that they hurry to Motavia.

> **Rika rejoins the party**


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

> **Rune rejoins the party**


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

> **Wren rejoins the party**


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

You are in Lutz's room at Esper Mansion. Leave the room and then teleport
back to Tyler or make your own way back to the village.

Head into the Spaceport. The party will automatically head up, and find
that Raja and Kyra are there to meet them. Chaz asks if Raja is ok now, and
also acknowledges Krya. Raja jokes that a minor sickness like that couldn't
keep him in bed, and asks to go with them. Krya also informs the party of
her wish to accompany them, to which Chaz thanks both of them. The group
then head off to Motavia in the Landale.

Upon arrival, the group are welcomed by Hahn, Gryz and Demi, who were
waiting for them at the Spaceport. Chaz acknowledges them all, and Hahn
notes that Chaz seems to have become stronger since they last met. Gryz
says that he was scolded by Pana, but he came anyway, and Demi reports that
the system is finally stabilized, so she can go with them. Chaz thanks
everybody, and Wren asks Demi what the disaster is. Demi informs the party
that a large hole suddenly appeared north of Piata, and that life around
the area has started dying. She adds that there are no gas or radiation
emissions coming from the hole, but Rune knows it to be a very powerful
Black Energy Wave. He surmises that it must be coming from The Profound
Darkness itself, and that it must have finally opened the door from the
other dimension.

Hahn tells Chaz that they should go to fight the last battle, and Kyra adds
that she would like to go with them too, pointing out that they need taking
care of by their big sister. Chaz announces that, since they are all there,
he would like all of them to go, but there is a problem. Rune adds that
there are only five 'Rings of Stars' to protect them from the power of the
Darkness, and Chaz tells them that they will only be able to choose one
person to take.

Control passes back to you, and before you decide on your final companion
it is worth noting that you will now be able to acquire for Chaz the most
powerful Technique in the game - Megid. If you wish to obtain it, see '7.2.
Megid - The Anger Technique' for more details. This will also allow you to
obtain the final item of equipment for the party.

<a id="s6-5-9"></a>

### 6.5.9. Final Preparations

Starting Party: Wren , Chaz , Rika , Rune
Starting Level: 42-43, 45-46, 48-49, 41-42
Hahn and Gryz are on the left side of the Spaceport, and Rika, Kyra and
Demi are on the right. Select one of the characters to join the party by
speaking to them and accepting their offer of help. Each of the characters
has their own strengths and weaknesses, and they will also be equipped with
some of the best equipment they can have.

The following lists show the starting equipment for each of the characters.


```
Rejoining         |   Hahn   |   Gryz   |   Demi   |   Raja   |   Kyra   |
Equipment   |¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|
            |Head |MAHLAYRING|LACO-HELM |LACO-GEAR |LACOCIRCLT|LACO-CROWN|
            |Right|MAHLAYDGGR|LACO-AXE  |SONICBUSTR|LACO-ROD  |LACOSLASHR|
            |Left |MAHLAYSHLD| /2-HAND  | /2-HAND  | /2-HAND  |MOONSLASHR|
            |Body |MAHLAYMAIL|LACO-MAIL |LACO-ARMOR|RFLC-ROBE |RFLC-ROBE |
```

Hahn has a wide range of offensive Techniques and a high Mental score to
use them, so select him if you want more psionic power in your group.
If you select Hahn as the fifth party member, replace his MAHLAYDGGR with
the GUARDSHILD, as he will be using Techniques rather than attacking.
Gryz is a strong character with powerful physical attacks, but has no real
skill elsewhere, so select him if you want some more muscle in the party.
If you select Gryz as the fifth party member, none of his equipment should
be changed unless you acquire a DEFEAT-AXE to replace his LACO-AXE.
Demi is fairly strong, yet also has a few useful Skills to protect and cure
the characters, so select her if you want some back-up offence and defence.
Also note that Demi is an android, so she is immune to status effects.
If you select Demi as the fifth party member, swap her LACO-ARMOR with
Wren's GUARDARMOR, as Demi will benefit more from a higher defence.
Raja is the ultimate physician, with a plentiful supply of TP to keep the
party alive, so select him if you want a healer and reviver for the party.
If you select Raja as the fifth party member, replace his LACO-ROD with two
SILVSHIELDs, as he will be mainly healing rather than attacking.
Kyra has a mix of curative and offensive Techniques, miscellaneous Skills
and magic spells, so select her if you want an all-rounder for the party.
If you select Kyra as the fifth party member, none of her equipment should
be changed unless you get another MOONSLASHR to replace her LACOSLASHR.
Once you have made your decision, you will need to place your party in the
most effective marching order. The following five lists give these:

Fifty party member:    Hahn     Gryz     Demi     Raja     Kyra
Marching order:    1   Wren     Wren     Wren     Wren     Wren
                   2   Chaz     Gryz     Demi     Chaz     Chaz
                   3   Rika     Chaz     Chaz     Rika     Rika
                   4   Hahn     Rika     Rika     Rune     Kyra
                   5   Rune     Rune     Rune     Raja     Rune

Once you've set the marching order, you will need to boost the party's EXP
one last time. Before facing the final challenge you will want every member
of the party to be at least Level 45. This should mean that Chaz will be at
about Level 49, Rika will be at about Level 52, Rune will be at least Level
45, and Wren will be at about Level 46. The other party member will be of
a suitable Level as well. A good place to do this would be one of the
towers on Rykros, or Vahal Fort (if you have completed Silver Soldier).

It would also be a good time to sell off all your old items (excluding
REPAIR-KITs) and buy as many TRIMATEs, STAR-DEWs and SOL-DEWs as you can
afford and carry. Leave space for at least two or three items, as you may
acquire some useful things from enemies in the final dungeon.

Once you are done, fully restore your party, then make your way to the
village of Mile (by teleporting, driving or walking). Ignore the village
(it is dead) and head south to a large grey area. In the middle of the grey
patch is a massive hole, and this is your destination. Check your party are
fully prepared, save your game, hold your breath, then head on down.

<a id="s6-5-10"></a>

### 6.5.10. Destiny

Starting Party: Wren , Chaz , Rika , Rune , Fifth
Starting Level: 46+  , 49+  , 52+  , 45+  . 45+


```
Recommended       |   Wren   | * Chaz * |   Rika   |   Rune   |  Fifth   |
Equipment   |¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯��¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|
            |Head |PALMA-RING|ALGO-RING |MOTA-RING |DEZO-RING |          |
            |Right|PULSEVULCN|ELSYDEON  |SILVR-TUSK|SILVSHIELD| See List |
            |Left | /2-HAND  | /2-HAND  |GUARD-CLAW|SILVSHIELD|  Above   |
            |Body |GUARDARMOR|LACO-MAIL |GUARD-MAIL|GUARD-ROBE|          |
```

*If MEGID has been acquired, Chaz should have GUARD-MAIL


```
  ______________
 // DUNGEON #24 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\
```

|/  The Edge               \_________________________________
   Enemies: BlindHeads, ChaosBrngr, Dark Rider, Gi-Le-Farg,
            Imagiomage, Outerbeast, Prophallus, Soldrfiend
 \
  \   Boss: Profound Darkness
   \______________________________

This is it. Welcome to the final dungeon of the game, and what an unusual
dungeon it is. It may be a little difficult to make out the path from time
to time, but the light streaks across it should help point it out.

First, head up, right, up, left, up, right and up, then enter the teleport
area to take you to the next area. Go right until you reach a junction,
and take the upper path, turning right at the top. Continue to the right
and step into the next teleport. Walk down all the way to the bottom, then
go left and down to another teleport area.

Go left, down, then left to the junction. Ignore the path leading up, and
keep heading left to use the next teleport. Head up to the junction and
turn left, then go up to the next junction and turn left again. Go upwards
at the corner and enter the teleport area to go to the next section. Head
left, down, left again, then up to yet another teleport. Head all the way
up to the next teleport, then head all the way up again. Stop before the
last teleport area and completely heal the party. Also, equip Wren with his
PLSMLAUNCH or PHOTNERASR. This is, after all, the last battle of the game,
so you'd best be prepared. Step onto the teleport.

The party will emerge in front of a huge, black, sprawling mass. Chaz asks
if this is the shape The Profound Darkness has taken, and Rune confirms it
is an emanation of it. He adds that he feels its anger and hatred of all
life, and its great need to destroy. Rune says that they must defeat it,
and that The Profound Darkness must not be allowed to get to Algo. Rika
notes that the portal is not yet completely open, and that they must take
advantage of this opportunity, so Chaz announces that they must do it now.
Wren and the other other party member concur, so Chaz finishes by saying
that this is the time they determine Algo's future - their future. The
final battle with Darkness then begins.


```
 __________
```

| BOSS #18 \____________  ____________________


```
| Profound Darkness     ||                    |
|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|| Recommended Level: | 
|  HP: 4120/4620/12999  ||                    |
| EXP: -      MST: -    || Wren: 46+         /
|                       || Chaz: 49+        /
| Weak: Energy,Light    || Rika: 52+       /
| Res:  -               || Rune: 45+      /
| Imm:  -               || 5th:  45+     /
|                       ||              /
```

The Profound Darkness is the spirit of pure evil, a seething consciousness
filled with anger, hate and hostility. And now you have to fight it.
The final boss battle of the game consists of three stages, each involving
combat with one of the incarnations of The Profound Darkness. They all
differ in their strength and abilities, so this strategy guide will explain
each incarnation separately. Also, the fifth character you have chosen will
determine the best method of fighting The Profound Darkness, so there are
five different strategies representing each possible choice. Good luck!

Stage 1 - The first incarnation is fairly unsettling it its appearance, but
          it is the weakest of the three. It will use only single-target
          attacks, including RAY-BREATH, FIREBREATH and SHDWBREATH. They
          are fairly similar in their strength, but certain characters will
          be weaker or more resistant to certain attacks. You will only
          need to use single-target healing to overcome these Skills.

Hahn - In the first round, have Chaz use RAYBLADE, Rika use SANER to
          speed up the party, Rune use NAWAT, Wren throw up a BARRIER, and
          Hahn use his VISION Skill.

In the second round, get Chaz to use RAYBLADE again, let Rika use
          DEBAN, have Rune use NAWAT, have Wren just attack or use RECOVER,
          and let Hahn use GIRES or NARES (or NAWAT if Wren uses RECOVER).

In the following rounds, keep Chaz using RAYBLADE, have Rika take
          over the healing (or use DBLSLASH if no healing is required), let
          Rune continue using NAWAT, get Wren to attack or use RECOVER, and
          have Hahn use NAWAT as well.

Keep using this strategy until the incarnation dissipates and the
          second form appears, which should take no more than six rounds.

Gryz - In the first round, have Chaz use RAYBLADE, Rika use SANER to
          speed up the party, Rune use NAWAT, Wren throw up a BARRIER, and
          Gryz perform a WAR CRY.

In the second round, get Chaz to use GIRES or NARES (or RAYBLADE
          if Wren uses RECOVER), let Rika use DEBAN, have Rune use NAWAT,
          have Wren just attack or use RECOVER, and let Gryz just attack.

In the following rounds, get Chaz to use RAYBLADE, have Rika take
          over the healing (or use DBLSLASH if no healing is required), let
          Rune continue using NAWAT, get Wren to attack or use RECOVER, and
          have Gryz attack as well.

Keep using this strategy until the incarnation dissipates and the
          second form appears, which should take no more than six rounds.

Demi - In the first round, have Chaz use RAYBLADE, Rika use SANER to
          speed up the party, Rune use NAWAT, Wren attack normally, and
          Demi set up a BARRIER.

In the second round, get Chaz to use GIRES or NARES (or RAYBLADE
          if Wren uses RECOVER), let Rika use DEBAN, have Rune use NAWAT,
          have Wren just attack or use RECOVER, and let Demi just attack or
          use RECOVER too.

In the following rounds, get Chaz to use RAYBLADE, have Rika take
          over the healing (or use DBLSLASH if no healing is required), let
          Rune continue using NAWAT, get Wren to attack or use RECOVER, and
          have Demi attack or use RECOVER as well.

Keep using this strategy until the incarnation dissipates and the
          second form appears, which should take no more than six rounds.

Raja - In the first round, have Chaz use RAYBLADE, Rika use SANER to
          speed up the party, Rune use NAWAT, Wren throw up a BARRIER, and
          Raja use BLESSING.

In the second round, get Chaz to use RAYBLADE, let Rika perform a
          DBLSLASH, have Rune use NAWAT, have Wren attack or use RECOVER,
          and let Raja use RES or GIRES (or defend if Wren uses RECOVER).

In the following rounds, get Chaz to use RAYBLADE, have Rika keep
          using DBLSLASH, let Rune continue using NAWAT, get Wren to attack
          or use RECOVER, and have Raja continue the healing.

Keep using this strategy until the incarnation dissipates and the
          second form appears, which should take no more than six rounds.

Kyra - In the first round, have Chaz use RAYBLADE, Rika use SANER to
          speed up the party, Rune use NAWAT, Wren throw up a BARRIER, and
          Kyra use her WARLA Skill.

In the second round, get Chaz to use RAYBLADE, let Rika use GIRES
          or NARES (or DBLSLASH if no healing is required), have Rune use
          NAWAT, have Wren attack or use RECOVER, and let Kyra use NAFOI.

In the following rounds, get Chaz to use RAYBLADE, have Rika keep
          up the healing or using DBLSLASH, let Rune continue using NAWAT,
          get Wren to attack or use RECOVER, and have Kyra use NAFOI.

Keep using this strategy until the incarnation dissipates and the
          second form appears, which should take no more than six rounds.

Stage 2 - The second incarnation has only slightly more HP than the first,
          but has far more powerful Skills. Apart from a lightning-style
          normal attack, the second form has use of DISTORTION, LIGHTSHOWR
          and ANOTHRGATE. These three Skills deal a considerable amount of
          damage to all members of the party, so target-all healing will be
          the order of the day this time. As there is no initial setup to
          be done, the second stage shouldn't last as long as the first.

Hahn - From the beginning, keep Chaz using RAYBLADE (or CROSSCUT when
          this runs out), have Rika use GIRES or GISAR (or use DBLSLASH if
          no healing is required), let Rune continue using NAWAT, get Wren
          to attack or use RECOVER, and have Hahn use NAWAT as well.

Keep using this strategy until the incarnation dissipates and the
          final form appears, which should take no more than five rounds.

Gryz - From the beginning, keep Chaz using RAYBLADE (or CROSSCUT when
          this runs out), have Rika use GIRES or GISAR (or use DBLSLASH if
          no healing is required), let Rune continue using NAWAT, get Wren
          to attack or use RECOVER, and have Gryz just attack as well.

Keep using this strategy until the incarnation dissipates and the
          final form appears, which should take no more than five rounds.

Demi - From the beginning, keep Chaz using RAYBLADE (or CROSSCUT when
          this runs out), have Rika use GIRES or GISAR (or use DBLSLASH if
          no healing is required), let Rune continue using NAWAT, have Wren
          attack or use RECOVER, and get Demi to use PHONOMEZER or RECOVER.

Keep using this strategy until the incarnation dissipates and the
          final form appears, which should take no more than five rounds.

Raja - From the beginning, keep Chaz using RAYBLADE (or CROSSCUT when
          this runs out), have Rika use DBLSLASH, let Rune continue using
          NAWAT, get Wren to attack or use RECOVER, and have Raja keep up
          his expert healing by using a RES or a SAR (or else just defend).

Keep using this strategy until the incarnation dissipates and the
          final form appears, which should take no more than five rounds.

Kyra - From the beginning, keep Chaz using RAYBLADE (or CROSSCUT when
          this runs out), have Rika use GIRES or GISAR (or use DBLSLASH if
          no healing is required), let Rune continue using NAWAT, get Wren
          to attack or use RECOVER, and have Kyra keep using NAFOI.

Keep using this strategy until the incarnation dissipates and the
          final form appears, which should take no more than five rounds.

Stage 3 - The third and final incarnation of The Profound Darkness is the
          toughest of them all, and with about three times as many HP it
          will definitely take the longest. It has a standard attack which
          is fairly damaging, and a few other abilities as well. These
          consist of POSSESSION (that may inflict Sleep on a character),
          CANCELING (extremely annoying, as it removes all assistance
          effects from the party such as BARRIER, DEBAN, SANER, etc.), and
          the powerful MEGID Technique. Don't hold back. This is it.

Hahn - From the beginning, have Chaz use MEGID (or CROSSCUT if you can't
          use this Technique), get Rika to take care of the healing (or use
          DBLSLASH if healing isn't required), let Rune throw out a LEGEON
          (or EFESS when this runs out), get Wren to use POSIBOLT if he has
          it (else attack, using RECOVER when needed), and have Hahn use
          his ASTRAL Skill (or NAWAT when the stock is depleted).

After CANCELING, have Rika use DEBAN instead of healing, let Wren
          use BARRIER instead of attacking or healing, and get Hahn to
          cover the curative responsibility by using NARES or an item.

If Rika runs out of TP from healing, have Hahn take over by using
          Techs, or by dipping into your (hopefully extensive) item supply.

Keep using this strategy until The Profound Darkness is finally
          destroyed, which should between nine to twelve rounds.

Gryz - From the beginning, have Chaz use MEGID (or CROSSCUT if you can't
          use this Technique), get Rika take care of the healing (or use
          DBLSLASH if healing isn't required), let Rune throw out a LEGEON
          (or EFESS when this runs out), get Wren to use POSIBOLT if he has
          it (else attack, using RECOVER when needed), and have Grzy keep
          attacking (this is his forte).

After CANCELING, have Rika use DEBAN instead of healing, let Wren
          use BARRIER instead of attacking or healing, and get Gryz to
          cover the curative responsibility by using appropriate items.

If Rika runs out of TP from healing, have Gryz take over the job
          by dipping into your (hopefully extensive) item supply.

Keep using this strategy until The Profound Darkness is finally
          destroyed, which should between nine to twelve rounds.

Demi - From the beginning, have Chaz use MEGID (or CROSSCUT if you can't
          use this Technique), get Rika take care of the healing (or use
          DBLSLASH if healing isn't required), let Rune throw out a LEGEON
          (or EFESS when this runs out), get Wren to use POSIBOLT if he has
          it (else attack, using RECOVER when needed), and have Demi use
          PHONOMEZER if she can (else attack, using RECOVER when needed).

After CANCELING, have Rika use DEBAN instead of healing, let Wren
          use BARRIER instead of attacking or healing, and get Demi to
          cover the curative responsibility by using MEDIC PW or an item.

If Rika runs out of TP from healing, have Demi take over with her
          MEDIC PW or by utilizing your (hopefully extensive) item supply.

Keep using this strategy until The Profound Darkness is finally
          destroyed, which should between nine to twelve rounds.

Raja - From the beginning, have Chaz use MEGID (or CROSSCUT if you can't
          use this Technique), get Rika to keep using DBLSLASH (or attack
          when the stock is exhausted), let Rune throw out a LEGEON (or
          EFESS when this runs out), get Wren to use POSIBOLT if he has
          it (else attack, using RECOVER when needed), and have Raja keep
          using curative Techs (or ST. FIRE if no healing is required).

After CANCELING, have Rika use DEBAN instead of attacking, and
          let Wren use BARRIER instead of attacking or healing.

If Raja runs out of TP from healing, have Rika take over for a
          round while Raja uses ATARAXIA on himself to regain some TP.

Keep using this strategy until The Profound Darkness is finally
          destroyed, which should between nine to twelve rounds.

Kyra - From the beginning, have Chaz use MEGID (or CROSSCUT if you can't
          use this Technique), get Rika take care of the healing (or use
          DBLSLASH if healing isn't required), let Rune throw out a LEGEON
          (or EFESS when this runs out), get Wren to use POSIBOLT if he has
          it (else attack, using RECOVER when needed), and have Kyra use
          TANDLE (or NAFOI if this runs out).

After CANCELING, have Kyra use WARLA instead of attacking, and
          let Wren use BARRIER instead of attacking or healing.

If Rika runs out of TP from healing, have Kyra take over with her
          Techs or by dipping into your (hopefully extensive) item supply.

Keep using this strategy until The Profound Darkness is finally
          destroyed, which should between nine to twelve rounds.
Eventually, The Profound Darkness will be defeated.

<a id="s6-5-11"></a>

### 6.5.11. The Cycle is Broken

The Profound Darkness is no more, but the party now have a new problem to
deal with. Rune points out that the force holding the dimensional door open
is gone, and Wren reports sensing a time warp. Rika asks what they are
supposed to do, when Elsydeon begins to shine. Rune realises that it is
protecting them, and Chaz thanks the spirits within.

A short while later, everyone is back on the surface of Motavia, watching
the sun rise. Rune announces that it is over, and Chaz agrees. Rika adds
that they were able to keep Algo safe. Wren reports that the departure
preparations are complete for the Landale, and Raja and Kyra decide to go
back to Dezolis. Raja says it was quite a journey, the likes of which he
hasn't had in a long time. Kyra suggests that the others should visit
Dezolis once in a while, but Raja points out they don't have a spaceship,
and that flapping their arms won't get them too far. Kyra and Raja say
goodbye. Demi reports that she will go back to Zelan to assist Wren, and
bids Chaz farewell too. She says that eventually the time will come when
both she and Wren will become unnecessary to Algo, but until that time she
will work to complete her duties. Wren adds that, after he has taken the
others to Dezolis, he will go back to Zelan. He guesses that they will
still need the support of the system a little while longer.

Chaz suddenly notices that Rika is missing, and Wren tells him that she is
already waiting by the Landale, adding that parting must be difficult for
her. Chaz doesn't seem too happy. Wren finally says goodbye to Chaz, and
assures him that they will meet again. He, Demi, Raja and Kyra head to the
Landale, and Wren tells Rika that they are leaving. They all get on board,
and fly off into the distance. Gryz says that they are gone. On board,
Rika tries to speak to Wren, but Wren knows what she is thinking. He tells
her that the road she chooses will probably be painful and difficult, but
says that she is their hope. Wren tells Rika that she must be strong and
live with pride. Rika understands, and thanks him.

Back on the surface, Gryz tells the others that he's got to go back to
Tonoe. He thanks Chaz, adding that he has learnt a lot from the trip. Hahn
decides to return to the academy. He says that he has become disgusted with
the sort of people there, but that he must learn to transform his feelings
into inner strength. He says goodbye to Chaz, and tells him that he will
always be proud to have fought beside him. Gryz and Hahn leave, and Rune
turns to Chaz and tells him that he guesses it is finally goodbye. He
continues that, although the battle against the ultimate fiend is over, his
mission as Lutz must continue. Rune explains that he must watch over all
Algo, and that he is still lacking in training and experience. He adds that
he must continue to improve himself, and eventually pass it on to the next
Lutz. Chaz asks if they will ever meet again, but Rune replies that it is
unlikely. Chaz begins to cry, bur Rune tells him that Chaz can live now
without anyone else's help.

At that moment, the Landale appears above them, and Rika is standing at the
doorway. Chaz and Rika call to each other, then Rika takes one last look at
Wren. With tears in her eyes, she leaps from the Landale and into the arms
of Chaz. Rune bids farewell to them both, and walks into the distance.
Under his breath, Chaz says his last goodbye to Rune, and thanks him. The
Landale soars off into space.

'The long battle is over.
 We were able to free ourselves
 from the terrible curse of yore.
 To the souls of those who
 sacrificed their lives for Algo
 sleep in peace.
 From person to person...
 From age to age...
 As long as memories last...
 We will not forget the
 sacrifices that have been made.'

Hahn goes back to teach at the academy, and Gryz and Pana live peacefully
back in Tonoe. Raja continues living leisurely, spending a lot of his time
at Gyuna's bar, and Kyra maintains her studies and prayer at the Esper
Mansion. Demi and Wren work together aboard Zelan, keeping Algo under
control, and Rune watches from afar as he wanders in the wilderness. Chaz
and Rika make a life together, and each finally find true happiness.
The epic story concludes.

'The eons-old struggle between
 Light and Dark has ended,
 and now the curtain
 rises on a new age...'

The credits roll.

Fin.

<a id="s6-6"></a>

## 6.6. Walkthrough Summary

In case you didn't want the exact guidelines to get through a particular
area of the game, I have compiled this summary to outline the different
stages of the game. This isn't entirely free of spoilers, but it doesn't
give any actual details either. It is also accompanied by the sections
that cover each specific area of the game.

Chaz and Alys go to Piata.                            1.1.

Find Alys, then speak to the principal.               1.1.

> **Go down to the basement and Hahn joins the party.     1.1.**

Go through the basement and fight the Igglanova.      1.2.

Go back to the principal.                             1.3.

Leave Piata and head north then east to Zema.         1.3.

Go through Birth Valley to find the Professor.        1.4.

Leave Zema and go south to Molcum.                    1.5.

> **Rune joins the party.                                 1.5.**

Head east then north to Valley Maze.                  1.6.

Go through then enter Tonoe.                          1.7.

Speak to Grandfather Dorin.                           1.8.

> **Rune leaves and Gryz joins the party.                 1.8.**

Go through the basement and get the Alshline.         1.9.

Return to Zema and use the Alshline.                  1.10.

Fight the Igglanova, then go into Bio-Plant.          1.10.

Head through Bio-Plant to find the Professor.         1.11.

> **Rika joins the party.                                 1.11.**

Go north then west to Aiedo.                          2.1.

Head east then north and go through Wreckage.         2.2.

Head through Passageway north of Aiedo.               2.3.

Go east then south and into Zio's Fort.               2.3.

Go through Zio's Fort and fight Juza.                 2.4.

Fight Zio, then Alys and Hahn leave the party.        2.4.

> **Demi joins the party and you get the Land Rover.      2.5.**

Go northeast and into Monsen.                         2.6.

Head northeast and go through the Plate System.       2.7.

Go south then southeast to Termi.                     2.8.

Head southwest and go into Ladea Tower.               2.8.

> **Go up Ladea Tower and Rune joins the party.           2.9.**

Go to the top and fight Gy-Laguiah.                   2.9.

Get the Psyco-Wand, then Alys dies.                   2.10.

Return to Zio's Fort and enter Nurvus.                2.10.

Head through Nurvus, and fight Zio again.             2.11.

Gryz and Demi leave the party.                        2.11.

Go into the Spaceport and head to Zelan.              2.12.

> **Go through Zelan and Wren joins the party.            2.13.**

> **Crash on Dezolis, and Raja joins the party.           3.1.**

Go north to Ryuon and speak to Gyuna.                 3.2.

Head northwest to Tyler and enter the Hanger.         3.2.

Go through the Hanger and raise the Spaceport.        3.3.

Get into the Landale and fly to Kuran.                3.3.

Go through Kuran and fight Dark Force.                3.4.

Get the Ice Digger, then go north.                    3.5.

Go through Mysterious Valley and get the Silvr-Tusk.  3.5.

Head south then northeast to Zosa.                    3.6.

Head northeast and go to the Climate Control Centre.  3.6.

Fight Gy-Laguiah, then through to fight D-Elm-Lars.   3.7.

Leave, then head southeast to Meese.                  3.8.

> **Raja leaves the party.                                3.8.**

Go northeast to the Carnivorous Trees.                3.9.

> **Retreat, then Kyra joins the party.                   3.9.**

Go southwest then southeast to Esper Mansion.         3.10.

Meet Lutz, then leave Esper Mansion.                  3.10.

Go southwest to Jut, then west to Weapons Plant.      4.1.

Go through, then go back to Gumbious Temple.          4.2.

Witness the theft of the EclpsTorch.                  4.3.

Go back to the Spaceport, then fly to Air Castle.     4.4.

Head through Air Castle and fight Xe-A-Thouls.        4.5.

Leave, then go back into Air Castle.                  4.6.

Go through Air Castle Basement and fight Lashiec.     4.6.

Get the EclpsTorch, then return to Dezolis.           4.7.

Destroy the Carnivorous Trees.                        4.7.

Head north and go into Garuberk Tower.                4.7.

Go through Garuberk Tower and fight Dark Force.       4.8.

> **Kyra leaves the party, and Gumbious Temple explodes.  4.9.**

Head back to Gumbious Temple and enter the hole.      4.9.

Speak to the Dezolisian bishop.                       4.9.

Go to the Spaceport and fly back to Motavia.          4.10.

Get the Hydrofoil then head to Krup.                  4.10.

> **Go east onto the island, and Seth joins the party.    5.1.**

Head through Island Cave to the top.                  5.1.

Go into Soldiers' Temple and get the Aero-Prism.      5.1.

> **Seth leaves the party, then fight Dark Force.         5.1.**

Return to the Spaceport and go to Rykros.             5.2.

Speak to Le Roof, then go to the Strength Tower.      5.3.

Go through the Strength Tower and fight De-Vars.      5.4.

Get the Rings, then go to the Courage Tower.          5.4.

Go through the Courage Tower and fight Sa-Lews.       5.5.

Get the Rings, then return to Silence Temple.         5.5.

Speak to Le Roof and learn the Algo genesis.          5.6.

Head back to Dezolis and into Esper Mansion.          5.7.

Go to Lutz's room and enter Sacred Sword Cave.        5.7.

Get Elsydeon, then return to Motavia.                 5.7.

Select the fifth party member.                        5.8.

Go to Mile, then head south and into The Edge.        5.9.

Go through The Edge, then fight Profound Darkness.    5.10.

The game is complete.                                 5.11.
7. Side Quests                                                        CSDQS

<a id="s7"></a>

# 7. Side Quests

<a id="s7-1"></a>

## 7.1. The Hunters' Guild

<a id="s7-1-1"></a>

> 🥉 **HG: The Ranch Owner** — Complete 'The Ranch Owner' in the Hunter's Guild. (Missed upon finding Elsydeon.) _(RetroAchievements · 5 pts)_
> 🥈 **Limit: Mile Sand Worm** — Defeat the Sand Worm in 'The Ranch Owner' before finding Demi. Combined level limit: 35, party of 5. _(RetroAchievements · 10 pts)_


### 7.1.1. The Ranch Owner

Recommended Level:  12+
When Available:     Immediately
Commission Awarded: 5000 MST
This is a request from a ranch owner at the village of Mile.

"The sand worms at my ranch have become so big that I'm at my wit's end.
 Please help me..."

That is the message.

After accepting this job, teleport to Mile and speak to the man directly
opposite the entrance to the village. The ranch owner will tell you that he
can no longer look after the dangerous Sand Worms, so he asks you to deal
with the problem by whatever means necessary. Make sure you are fully
healed and the game is saved, then walk through the small gate and wander
around the ranch until a battle starts. You will now fight a Sand Worm.

Use your best skills and techniques available, as you will only need to
defeat one of these beasts. This Sand Worm will only attack individual
members of your party, so just heal whenever a character gets low on HP and
keep hacking away. After a short while it should go down.

Return to the rancher and he will lament the loss of his dream, but also
realise that it had to be done. He sends the commission to the guild, so
return to Aiedo and pick up your hard-earned cash.

<a id="s7-1-2"></a>

> 🥉 **HG: Tinkerbell's Dog** — Complete 'Tinkerbell's Dog' in the Hunter's Guild. _(RetroAchievements · 5 pts)_


### 7.1.2. Tinkerbell's Dog

Recommended Level:  N/A
When Available:     After obtaining the Land Rover
Commission Awarded: 2000 MST (-280 MST costs = 1720 MST profit)
This is a request from the house where Tinkerbell lives.

"Our household pet 'Rocky' has disappeared.
 Please find him..."

That is the message.

After accepting this job, head to the east side of Aiedo. There are two
houses near the south wall next to the river. Tinkerbell's house is the one
on the left, so enter.

Speak to Tinkerbell's father on the left and he will explain the situation,
hinting that the dog is likely to be found outside of Aiedo, then speak to
Tinkerbell's mother near the door and she will inform you that Rocky is
very fat and that he likes sweet things. You can speak to Tinkerbell if you
wish, but you won't get any important information.

Leave the house, and go to the south gate. Step just outside and head left
along the wall. Turn north at the end, hugging the wall all the way, until
you reach a building at the corner. When you go in, you will see that the
room is deserted, so head down the stairs and you find yourself in Naura
cake shop. Speak to the man behind the counter and buy one SHORTCAKE for
280 MST, then leave Aiedo.

Rocky will either be in Krup, Monsen or Termi. In Krup and Monsen, you will
find Rocky to the southeast of the Tool Store. In Termi, he will be to the
southeast of the statue of Alis. Address Rocky when you find him, and the
dog will bark. Chaz will surmise that he is Rocky. Address the dog again
and you will give him the SHORTCAKE. You then take Rocky back to Aiedo.

A second later and your back in Tinkerbell's house. Her father will thank
you, and inform you that your commission will be sent to the guild. Return
to the Hunters' Guild and collect your 2000 MST.

<a id="s7-1-3"></a>

> 🥉 **HG: The Missing Student** — Complete 'The Missing Student' in the Hunter's Guild. _(RetroAchievements · 5 pts)_


### 7.1.3. Missing Student

Recommended Level:  N/A
When Available:     After shutting down Nurvus
Commission Awarded: 3000 MST (-40 MST costs = 2960 MST profit)
We have a request from the caretaker of the student dorms in Piata.

"One of the students entrusted to our care has disappeared.
 Please find her..."

That is the message.

After accepting this job, teleport to Piata and head to the building in the
northwest corner of town. Walk in and speak to the man nearby. He will ask
for your help, explaining that one of the female students living in the
dorm has gone missing. She had apparently become a devotee of some sort of
religious cult, and he had hoped that the infatuation would pass and that
she would come back. Obviously, she hasn't. He goes on to point out that
something like this could tarnish the reputation of the entire Academy, and
begs for the party's help.

The only religious cult that we've come across so far is the one that was
worshipping Zio in Kadary. Before going there, however, teleport to Termi
and go to the Bayamare Gift Store. Purchase a PEROLYMATE for 40 MST.

Now, teleport to Kadary and go to the large church in the northwest of the
village. Head to the northwest corner of the church and speak to the blonde
girl that's there. She will cry, saying that she wants to go back to Piata.
This must be her. Chaz says that they will take her back, but then the girl
feels faint, says that she is hungry, and collapses.

They take her to the Inn in Kadary. The girl is resting in bed, and the old
man nearby explains that she was eating irregularly. She needs to eat
something nutritious. He will then notice that you have the PEROLYMATE, and
inform you of it's high nutritional value. You then give it to the girl.

Speak to the student, and she will be a little dazed. You will then all
appear back in the dorm in Piata. The caretaker will thank you, and tell
you that he will send the fee to the guild. He also asks if the party could
keep the matter to themselves. All done, teleport back to Aiedo and collect
your earnings from the guild.

<a id="s7-1-4"></a>

> 🥈 **HG: Fissure of Fear** — Complete 'Fissure of Fear' in the Hunter's Guild. _(RetroAchievements · 10 pts)_


### 7.1.4. Fissure of Fear

Recommended Level:  19+
When Available:     After shutting down Nurvus
Commission Awarded: 5000 MST
This is a request from Eddie who lives in Monsen.

"My son has fallen into a crack in the earth!
 Please help my son!"

That is the message.

After accepting this job, teleport to Monsen and visit the house directly
north of the crack in the ground. Speak to the woman inside, and she will
inform you that her son, Tallas, was playing outside when he fell through
the crack. She wants to go and rescue him, but tells the party that creepy
groaning sounds have been coming from the crack in the ground. She finishes
by asking the party to rescue Tallas.

Go outside and you will see that the sign has been removed from the fence.
Rest at the Inn if you need to, then save your game and drop down the hole.


```
  ______________
 // DUNGEON #25 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\
```

|/  The Hole               \_________________________________
   Enemies: Jr.Ooze, Meta Slug, Zol Slug
 \
  \   Boss: Fract Ooze
   \______________________________

Chaz will be surprised that there is a vast cave underneath Monsen, an Rika
will notice that Tallas is nowhere in sight. The path to the left leads to
a staircase that takes you to the surface outside Monsen, so head right.
Turn up at the corner, then continue right and down. Examine the shoes on
the floor, and Rika will wonder if they are Tallas' shoes. Continue to the
right until you reach a junction. The lower path leads nowhere, so head up
and follow the passage up and a little to the right until you see a large
orange slug. Examine it, and Rika will become concerned about the fate of
Tallas. Chaz will mention that it is bad luck to even think such a thing,
and then the creature will attack.


```
 __________
```

| BOSS #19 \____________  ____________________


```
| Fract Ooze            ||                    |
|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|| Recommended Level: | 
|  HP: 1999             ||                    |
| EXP: 42236  MST: 855  || Party: 19+        /
|                       ||                  /
| Weak: Fire,Water,Elec ||                 /
| Res:  Force.Gravity   ||                /
| Imm:  Light           ||               /
|                       ||              /
```

You could argue that this isn't really a boss battle, as the music is just
normal battle music. However, the battle is necessary to the completion of
the mission, so I thought it should be categorized as a boss battle.
Use your best Skills and Techniques to get the battle over as quickly as
possible, avoiding light Skills as the Fract Ooze is resistant to these.
Apart from its standard attack, the Fract Ooze only uses one Skill called
CELL SPLIT, a hit-all attack that does a small amount of damage. If you
stay on the offensive, it is unlikely you will need to heal at all, and the
battle should be over in no more than two or three rounds.
Once the fight is over, Tallas will be standing where the Fract Ooze was.
He asks if they are on the other side of the planet, and Chaz asks Tallas
if he was really eaten. Rika is glad Tallas is safe, pointing out that he
would have been digested had they not come along in time. Tallas agrees,
then thanks Chaz before running off down the passage.

Use HINAS or an ESCAPIPE, or follow Tallas, heading all the way to the left
to the staircase that you ignored earlier. Go back into Monsen and return
to Eddie's house (see that the sign has been replaced). Speak to Tallas'
mother and she will thank you, saying that she had lost all hope. She tells
you that she will send the commission to the guild, so teleport back to
Aiedo and pick up your reward.

<a id="s7-1-5"></a>

> 🥉 **HG: The Stain in Life** — Complete 'The Stain in Life' in the Hunter's Guild. _(RetroAchievements · 5 pts)_


### 7.1.5. Stain in Life

Recommended Level:  N/A
When Available:     After obtaining the Hydrofoil
Commission Awarded: 50000 MST (-50000 MST costs = 0 MST profit)
This is a request from the village chief of Uzo via letter transmission.

"My two daughters have left the village and have not returned since.
 Please find out where they are..."

That is the message.

Before you accept this job, take note that you will need 50000 MST in order
to complete it. Although you will get this money back, you will not get
anything else.

After accepting this job, teleport to Piata and get into the Hydrofoil.
Head north and then to the west end of the land, then go due south. You
will come to an island, and on this island is the village of Uzo. Drive in.


```
Uzo          Inn             |    80 MST per person|
                             |                     |
             Tool Store      |TRIMATE   |   400 MST|
                             |ANTIDOTE  |    10 MST|
                             |CURE-PARAL|   120 MST|
                             |TELEPIPE  |   130 MST|
                             |ESCAPIPE  |    70 MST|
```

Go to the house in the southwest corner of the village, and speak to the
woman at the back of the house. She informs you that their two daughters
made a raft and went to the mainland to do some shopping at the market.
However, that was a month ago, and there has been no sign of them. She is
not even sure whether they made it to the mainland or not. The woman then
explains that her husband makes out that he is stubborn and obstinate, but
he is really more worried than she is. She begs the party to find their
daughters.

There are only two places that have anything like a market on Motavia -
Tonoe and Aiedo. Of course, Tonoe is hidden within a mountain range and
protected by a monster-filled cave, so Aiedo seems like the most likely
location for the girls to be found. Teleport back there.

Head up to the market complex, but don't go in. Instead, head right and
then up around the building. Continue up the path to the river, then go a
little to the left and cross the bridge. Head up through the gate and into
the building. This is Aiedo prison.

In the left-most cell you will see two girls. Speak to the one on the left,
and she will tell you that they came to Aiedo from far away to do some
shopping. Unfortunately, they got a little carried away, were unable to pay
for their rooms, and were subsequently caught. She then finds out that the
party are there at the girls' parents' request, but points out the watchman
that is nearby.

Speak to the watchman on the left, and he will inform you that the girls
have a ten-year sentence. The seem to ask if the watchman can let them out,
but he tells them that he can only do that if they post the girls' bail.
However, the bail is 50000 Mesetas. Speak to the man again and he will ask
if you want to pay the bail. Agree, and the man is amazed by the party's
magnanimity, then he unlocks the girls' cell.

Speak to the girl on the left again, and she will also be amazed. Chaz then
suggests that they all go back to Uzo, so that's what they do. The girls'
father thanks the party, and tells them that he will send the commission to
the Hunters' Guild as promised. He will then express his gratitude once
more. Teleport back to Aiedo, and reclaim your expenses from the guild.

<a id="s7-1-6"></a>

> 🥉 **HG: The Dying Boy** — Complete 'The Dying Boy' in the Hunter's Guild. _(RetroAchievements · 5 pts)_


### 7.1.6. Dying Boy

Recommended Level:  N/A
When Available:     After obtaining the Hydrofoil
Commission Awarded: 10000 MST (-500 MST costs = 9500 MST profit)
This is a request from Mr. Culvers of Torinco via letter transmission.

"My son has fallen ill. I would like to dicuss a certain plan I have to
 deal with this matter. I will go into more detail after we meet."

That is the message.

After accepting this job, teleport to Termi and go to the Bayamare Gift
Shop to buy an ALIS-SWORD. Leave the village, then get into the Hydrofoil
and head southwest to the west coast near the Ladea Tower. From here, go
due south onto a large island. The village of Torinco should be within
sight to the west, so drive in.


```
Torinco      Inn             |    90 MST per person|
                             |                     |
             Tool Store      |TRIMATE   |   400 MST|
                             |ANTIDOTE  |    10 MST|
                             |CURE-PARAL|   120 MST|
                             |TELEPIPE  |   130 MST|
                             |ESCAPIPE  |    70 MST|
```

Go north up the first few steps, then continue up and cross the next steps.
Head east and then north up another flight of steps, then go back west and
ascend the last steps to find a house just to the right. Go in.

Speak to the man standing next to the bed on the left side of the house. He
introduces himself as Culvers, and informs you that his son has become ill.
The doctors said that he had been cured, but Culvers says that the boy is
still convinced that he is going to die and that he can't be cured.
Apparently, it is one of those psychological illnesses. Culvers adds that,
back in the days when there were fewer monsters, they used to take family
trips to Termi. He wishes that they were able to go there now, but says
that it is not possible. However, Culvers thinks that if they were able to
take their son something connected with Termi, that it might restore his
strength. He asks the party if they can buy something from the gift shop
in Termi.

Fortunately, you have already bought something from the shop, so approach
the boy in bed and speak to him. The boy sees the Alis-Sword, and remembers
the heroine that he saw in Termi. The party step away from the bed, and
Chaz stands in the middle of the floor before the boy. Chaz tells the boy
to watch, then performs a few stylish sword moves. The boy is impressed,
and Chaz explains that the sword is filled with the strength and courage of
the heroine Alis. He gives the sword to the boy and tells him to get
better. The boy thanks Chaz, and tells him he is feeling better already.

Speak to Culvers once more, and Culvers will say that it is a miracle. He
thanks the party greatly, and says that he thinks Chaz is the second hero.
After that, he will tell the party they can collect their fee from the
guild. Return to Aiedo, and do what the man said.

<a id="s7-1-7"></a>

> 🥈 **HG: Man with a Twist** — Complete 'Man with a Twist' in the Hunter's Guild. _(RetroAchievements · 10 pts)_
> 🥈 **Limit: King Rappy** — Defeat King Rappy in 'Man with a Twist' with no 5th party member. Combined level limit: 110, party of 4. _(RetroAchievements · 10 pts)_


### 7.1.7. Man with twist

Recommended Level:  36+
When Available:     After obtaining the Hydrofoil
Commission Awarded: Nothing
This is a request from Mr.Sekreas of Torinco.

"We are at our wits' end due to a flock of birds who are eating up our
 terraced fields. Please exterminate them..."

That is the message.

Before you accept this job, take note that although you are offered 20000
Mesetas to complete the task, you won't actually receive any money at all.

After accepting this job, teleport to Termi and get into the Hydrofoil.
Now, head southwest to the west coast near the Ladea Tower. From here, go
due south onto a large island. The village of Torinco should be within
sight to the west, so drive in.

Go north up the first few steps, then continue up and cross the next steps.
Head east and enter the house at the end. Speak to the man in here, and he
will introduce himself as Sekreas. He will tell you that a strange flock of
birds has been eating up the fields, and that he knows where the head
honcho bird can be found. He asks the party to exterminate the head honcho
bird, and explains it can be found in a cave to the northeast of Torinco.

Rest at the Inn if you need to, then head out of the village. Go a little
to the north, then east below the mountain range. Save your game just
outside the cave entrance, then go on in.


```
  ______________
 // DUNGEON #26 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\
```

|/  Rappy Cave             \_________________________________
   Enemies: Blue Rappy, Rappy
 \
  \   Boss: King Rappy
   \______________________________

Head up the passage until you reach a junction. Go right and then continue
upwards, crossing the set of steps when you come to them. Follow the path
up and then around to the left, continuing up until you reach another set
of steps. Ignore the corridor to the right, and head up the thin passage
above. Walk all the way to the top, then stop when you reach a larger
chamber. Heal up all the characters, and equip Wren's best single-target
weapon (PLSMLAUNCH or PHOTNERASR). Now, address the large yellow bird
sitting on the platform above. It won't speak, but it will attack.


```
 __________
```

| BOSS #20 \____________  ____________________


```
| King Rappy            ||                    |
|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|| Recommended Level: | 
|  HP: 2911             ||                    |
| EXP: 39852  MST: 555  || Party: 36+        /
|                       ||                  /
| Weak: Fire            ||                 /
| Res:  -               ||                /
| Imm:  Light           ||               /
|                       ||              /
```

The master bird is not too difficult, and won't really require any serious
careful strategy to defeat.

In the first round, have Chaz use RAYBLADE, let Rika use DEBAN, have Rune
use LEGEON, and get Wren to use BARRIER. If there is another character in
your party, let them perform their best attack (avoiding light Skills).

King Rappy will either use a normal attack or its EARTHQUAKE Skill (which
damages all characters). With the defences set up, neither of these attacks
should pose too much of a threat.

In the rounds that follow, let Chaz continue using RAYBLADE, have Rika use
DBLSLASH, get Rune to use NAWAT, let Wren just attack, and have your other
character (if there is one) use their best abilities.

Obviously, have Wren use RECOVER if he needs to (unlikely), and get Rika to
heal any other characters that drop to low HP levels (also unlikely).

If you keep the pressure on, King Rappy should fly the nest in about four
or five rounds.
After the battle, the boss bird will fly around the characters and down the
corridor. Chaz will tell it to stop, and start to run after it. At that
moment, Sekreas runs into the room and tells the party to stop. Sekreas
tells the party to let the bird go, but Chaz asks why, considering Sekreas
was the one who asked for it to be exterminated. Sekreas agrees, then asks
for the party's forgiveness. Rika demands to know what's going on, so
Sekreas explains. He starts by telling the group that he has always been an
animal lover, and that recently he discovered a new breed of bird. He goes
on to say that he used the cave to rear the birds, but eventually they
began looking for food. The birds went to Torinco and started to eat up the
fields, so the villagers decided to set about exterminating them. He asks
the party if they agree with him that this was a cruel thing to do, but
Chaz asks why, if that was the case, Sekreas commissioned the Hunters'
Guild to exterminate the boss bird. Sekreas replies that he knew a head
honcho bird had started to emerge in the flock, and that it was very
powerful. He (foolishly) thought that even a hunter wouldn't be able to
defeat it, and hoped that this would disuade the villagers from trying to
destroy the birds. Chaz realises that Sekreas had been using them, and
