Sekreas admits that he had grossly underestimated their strength. Sekreas
says he is sorry, and consents to the party locking him up in prison or
whatever they want. Chaz can't be bothered with him, and tells Sekreas to
get out of his sight. Sekreas complies, running off down the passage.

Chaz tells the party that he can sort of understand why Sekreas did what he
did, and adds that the boss bird has flown away somewhere, and that it
won't eat up Torinco's fields any more. Rune points out that it could just
go and start on some other fields, but Chaz just says that they'll deal
with that when they come to it.

Don't bother returning to Torinco as Sekreas will only apologise for what
he has done. Instead, report to the Hunters' Guild and report what has
happened. The receptionist will say that no word has been received from
Torinco, and that action will be carried out to both reclaim Sekreas' debt
and to save face for the guild. Chaz insists not to bother, so the matter
is forgotten.

<a id="s7-1-8"></a>

> 🥈 **HG: Silver Soldier** — Complete 'Silver Soldier' in the Hunter's Guild. (Missed upon finding Elsydeon.) _(RetroAchievements · 10 pts)_
> 🥉 **Initiate: Positron Bolt** — Recover the Positron Bolt parts in Vahal Fort. (Missed upon finding Elsydeon.) _(RetroAchievements · 5 pts)_


### 7.1.8. Silver Soldier

Recommended Level:  36+
When Available:     After obtaining the Hydrofoil
                    Before obtaining Elsydeon
Commission Awarded: 80000 MST
This is a request from an old man in Zema.

"We are having problems with some strange machines that have begun to roam
 the outskirts of the village. We have not yet been attacked, but we
 villagers are afraid and would like something to be done about it."

That is the message.

After accepting this job, ensure that the party are fully healed and then
teleport to Zema. Head inside and you will be accosted by three Servants.
Defeat these guardians, then head to the house in the northeast corner of
the village. Speak to the old man in the room on the right, and he will
explain that, in the last week, unidentified machines have been roaming the
village. It seems like they are trying to investigate Birth Valley. They
are not doing any harm to the villagers, but it is making everyone uneasy.
He requests that the party drive the machines away. Chaz finds it strange
that they were attacked upon entering the village, but Wren points out that
he seemed to be their only target.

You could speak to the villagers to learn more about the problem, but all
you really need to do is go to the source of the machines. Teleport to
Nalya, then get into the Hydrofoil and head due east. Continue onto an
island, and stop outside the metal structure. This is Vahal Fort. Enter it.


```
  ______________
 // DUNGEON #27 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\
```

|/  Vahal Fort             \_________________________________
   Enemies: Browren486, Jurafaduel, Goldine, LifeDeletr,
            VopalSphre, Dominator
  Treasure: REPAIR-KIT, PHOTNERASR, LACO-GEAR, LACO-ARMOR,
            POSIBOLT (Skill)
 \
  \   Boss: Dominator x3
   \______________________________

Wren will report that there is a transmission from Demi. She will inform
him that the Plate System has sustained an attack from a mysterious android
attack squad. She reports that she has kept the damage to a minimum, but
she judges from the sophistication of their attack that there must be a
sophisticated tactician behind it. Rika can't understand how someone could
still be sending spurious orders now that Kuran is silenced, and Wren
reports to Demi that they are investigating the matter as well. He advises
her to shift to Alert Mode 1. Demi agrees, then cuts out. Rika asks if the
attack squad could be anything like they met in Zema, and Wren replies that
it seems orders are being given for the destruction of all AI systems above
a certain level. Chaz then sees why Wren was attacked in Zema, and Rika
realises that the reason the machines were in Zema in the first place was
to destroy Seed. Rune asks if the person responsible for the attack didn't
know Seed had already self-destructed, and Wren theorizes that someone in
possession of old Parmanian data, and far removed from Zelan, must be
responsible, and Chaz suggests that they could be here.

Head up to the junction, then go right, up and then right, and pick up a
REPAIR-KIT. Return left, down, and then left past the entrance to the left
wall. Continue up, left and then up again, ignoring the alcove on the left,
and head up to the top wall. Go right and then up, right and down the
corridor until you reach a central elevator shaft. Go down around it to the
right, and take the passage to the right from here. Head up the corridor at
the end, then turn right and then down. Pick up the PHOTNERASR from the
bottom left of this chamber, then return up, left, down and left. Head down
and left to the elevator, and descend to the floor below.

Walk straight down the walkway, ignoring the paths to the left and right
for the moment. Continue to the bottom and pick up the LACO-GEAR. Unless
Wren already has the PALMA-RING, equip this new item to him. Return back up
and turn either left or right, and then up at the corner. Keep going up and
then back around to continue up the walkway to the top wall. There are two
ways to go here, but first you should go left. Head left, down, left and
down, and keep going down until you reach the bottom. Walk right, down and
right, then procure the LACO-ARMOR. As before, only equip this to Wren if
he hasn't already acquired the GUARDARMOR.

Return back left, up and then right to the junction, then continue right,
down, right and then down all the way to the bottom. Turn left, down and
left, then take the elevator in the wall above. Upon arrival, Rune will
comment that the place is awesome, and add that if everything here started
to move at once, Motavia would instantly fall under their control. Chaz
sarcastically asks Rune to remind him why they are here, and Wren tells
them that they have to hurry, as it is not a joking matter.

Walk a little down and then left, ignoring the platform above you, and use
the terminal on the left of the walkway. Head back to the right, and step
onto the conveyor belt at the end. On the other side, step onto the next
conveyor above you, then head right over the thin walkway and take the
elevator to the next floor.

Head straight down the corridor to the bottom and open the chest. Chaz asks
if they are more of Wren's spare parts. Wren looks in the chest and states
that he can't believe it, as he thinks it's a Positron Bolt unit. Wren
explains that it is a weapon developed for attacking space fortresses, and
that a 10-second burst could even destroy Zelan. Rune is amazed at the
power of the unit, yet notes how small it is. Wren adds that, under normal
circumstances, he would prefer to avoid using such a weapon, but admits
that in the current situation he has no choice. He installs it.

Wren acquires the POSIBOLT Skill
Go back up the passage and use the elevator. Head left across the walkway,
then use the conveyor belt above you. At the top, walk left all the way to
the end of the walkway, ignoring the platform below, then step onto the
belt at the end. Back on the walkway again, head left and take the elevator
to the bottom floor. Go down to the corner, then left until you emerge in a
larger chamber. Walk up to the panels above, then completely heal your
party. Examine one of the panels.

As Wren is wondering what the system is, it speaks. The computer welcomes
them, and introduces itself as Daughter, the protector of Algo, responsible
for administering law and ensuring order. Rune asks of what it is a
daughter, but Rika seems to know, saying that Seed told her the plan had
been abandoned. Wren confirms that his data says that as well, but admits
that he must have an error in his data. Chaz asks Daughter if it was the
one that sent androids to Zema and the Plate System, and Daughter replies
that he is correct. Chaz then asks why, if Daughter is the protector of
Algo, it would destroy the environmental control system. Daughter explains
that it is trying to purge the AIs not under its control, and that its
primary objective is peace and prosperity for all of Algo. It adds that any
AI that does not obey its orders is an enemy of Algo and must be destroyed.

Rika takes control of the conversation now, asking Daughter if it was aware
that its network is not connected to external systems, and that any order
it did send would not reach the other systems. Daughter disagrees, saying
it was designed to take control of all remaining systems of Mother Brain,
and that all AI systems in Algo are under its control. Wren informs
Daughter that there is a fundamental error in its self-awareness. He tells
it that, because the environmental deterioration caused by the system
crash was greater than initially expected, the effects of the destruction
of Parma were calculated prior to the completion of the Daughter Project.
He goes on to say that the project was then abandoned at the prototype
manufacturing stage, and that Daughter is but a test machine. Daughter
questions this, but Wren continues that, subsequently, a network was
constructed in Zelan whose sole object was to restart and stabilize Algo's
environmental control system. Wren introduces himself as the AI in charge
of managing the entire system, and Daughter replies that it understands.

Daughter and Wren say little for a moment, then Daughter continues by
saying that it understands that Wren is the one creating disorder in its
system. It adds that it will use all its power to exterminate anything that
interferes with its programs, and then a boss battle begins.


```
 __________
```

| BOSS #21 \____________  ____________________


```
| Dominator x3          ||                    |
|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|| Recommended Level: | 
|  HP: 999              ||                    |
| EXP: 14400  MST: 1500 || Party: 37+        /
|                       ||                  /
| Weak: Electric        ||                 /
| Res:  Fire,Watr,Force ||                /
| Imm:  Light           ||               /
|                       ||              /
```

Three Dominators are the sum total of Daughter's defences, and it shouldn't
be a great chore to defeat them. Use hit-all Techniques and Skills (try out
Wren's POSIBOLT), and the Dominators should only last a couple of rounds.
After the battle, Wren approaches the computer terminal and tells Daughter
that he is going to shut it down. Daughter asks why Wren is doing it,
telling him that Algo would never retain its former prosperity without it.
Daughter, in desperation, adds that there is even a possibility that all
will be ruined. Wren explains to Daughter that he was only given minimal
environmental control ability, yet humans have continued to live for over a
thousand years. Daughter begs Wren not to shut it down, but Wren continues
by telling it that civilization has indeed fallen into decay, but that this
is exactly why humans have retained their vitality. He tells it that humans
worked together to overcome all of the problems they have faced. Daughter
sounds weak now, and all you can make out is the word 'stop'. Finally, Wren
tells Daughter than there is no need for excessive interference. Daughter
is then shut down.

Wren turns to the party and explains that technicians at the time planned
to reopen the project after the environment was stabilized. He supposes
that they must have had an independent AI at Nurvus that was keeping things
under control at Vahal Fort. He notes that both he and Demi were negligent,
ignoring the ancient facility because it was unrelated to their official
tasks. Rune adds that all efforts were put into starting Zelan, so Daughter
was forgotten. Rika concludes that a signal must have been sent to wake
Daughter after they had shut down Nurvus.

After this long dialogue, teleport out of Vahal Fort (or walk if you wish),
then get back to the Hunters' Guild to collect your dues.

<a id="s7-2"></a>

> 🥉 **The Cursed Blade** — Equip Chaz with a rare sword from a Shadow Saber. _(RetroAchievements · 5 pts)_


## 7.2. Megid - The Anger Technique

You must have acquired ELSYDEON before you can complete this side mission.

Go to Rykros. Leave the Silence Temple, and head southeast to the Courage
Tower. From here, head due west through the thin passageway until you reach
an area filled with a few green rocks. The largest of these rocks has a
door at the front. Save your game, then enter.


```
  ______________
 // DUNGEON #28 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\
```

|/  Anger Tower            \_________________________________
   Enemies: Bladeright, BloodSaber, CrminHeads, Dark Witch,
            Hakenleft, Illusionst, Twinarms
  Treasure: GUARD-MAIL, SOL-DEW, MEGID (Technique)
 \
  \   Boss: Alys, (Re-Faze)
   \______________________________

Chaz will notice that Elsydeon is shining, and Rika states that a voice is
reverberating in her head. The voice tells them that the Anger Tower gladly
welcomes the Protectors of Algo.

Head up the corridor, then turn right when you reach the top. Head down at
the corner, then left a little, then continue down to take the stairs at
the bottom. Head up and right to acquire the GUARD-MAIL, which should be
equipped to Chaz immediately. Go back to the stairs, then descend to the
floor below. Return up and left to the junction, then continue left and
down, picking up the SOL-DEW in the middle of the floor. Go to the bottom
right corner and climb the staircase.

Go up to the top, then right to the far wall. Walk down and go left through
the small passage, then head down to the staircase. Take it to the top
floor. You emerge in a large room, in the middle of which is a person who
looks very familiar - Alys.

Chaz is also entirely alone, the rest of the party having been unable to
follow. You can return down the stairs to rejoin them if you wish, but it
would be best to approach the Alys-like figure. Address her, and Chaz will
ask why she is on Rykros. There is no response. Instead, Alys starts to
push Chaz, and a battle follows.


```
 __________
```

| BOSS #22 \____________  ____________________


```
| Alys                  ||                    |
|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|| Recommended Level: | 
|  HP: 420              ||                    |
| EXP: 1      MST: 1    || Chaz: 45-46       /
|                       ||                  /
| Weak: -               ||                 /
| Res:  Force,Radiation ||                /
| Imm:  Fire,Light      ||               /
|                       ||              /
```

This is not really a boss fight, although the music is different and
ironically appropriate. Just have Chaz use normal attacks, as Alys should
not be able to inflict enough damage to kill him before she falls.
After the battle, Chaz cries out for Alys, and an unseen laughter can be
heard. Chaz asks who it is, and the room disappears into blackness. A ball
of fire appears, and teases Chaz by saying he is a weakling for wailing and
lamenting for something he knows to be an illusion. Chaz is baffled, and
begins to get annoyed. The fire seems to take enjoyment from the anger and
hatred coming from Chaz, and comments that it is quite a show of Chaz's
force of character. It asks Chaz if he would like to be able to transform
those feelings into strength, but Chaz doesn't understand. The fire goes on
to explain that there is a technique to transform emotions of anger and
hatred into powers of destruction. It asks if Chaz wants to know about it.

Whatever you do, select 'No'. If you reply that Chaz does want to know, the
ball of fire will be disappointed with Chaz, and tell him that it finds it
ridiculous that a fellow like Chaz would consider himself worthy to wield
Elsydeon. It will then attack. Re-Faze (as this is its name) is immensely
powerful, and uses a technique called Megid. This inflicts severe damage on
Chaz, and will ultimately kill him. There is no way to win this fight.

After selecting 'No', Chaz will tell Re-Faze not to mess with him, and
Re-Faze will ask why. Chaz explains that winning with such a power would be
meaningless, and would only make them the same as the Darkness. Re-Faze
seems to be impressed, saying that Chaz has fought the illusion yet hasn't
lost sight of himself. It says it will trust Chaz with the forbidden
technique, Megid.

Re-Faze tells Chaz it is necessary to feel anger and hatred for humans to
be human, and he feels that there shouldn't be any danger that Chaz will be
corrupted by the power of Megid as long as he doesn't forget his true self.

Chaz acquires the MEGID Technique
Make your way back to the Silence Temple by teleporting or otherwise, then
head into the Landale and select your next destination.
8. Cast of Characters                                                 CCOCR

# 8. Cast of Characters

This section contains a description of each important character in the
game, listed in the order in which they are first encountered or brought
to attention. The playable characters are also represented by excellent
ASCII pictures, courtesy of the ASCII Generator.

<a id="s8-1"></a>

## 8.1. Playable Characters

Chaz is the core character of the game, and he is the only member of your
party that is kept from beginning to end. As an orphaned child, Chaz lived
in a far off country, where struggle to survive taught him how to take care
of himself in a fight. He did some pretty bad things during this time,
until he happened to chance upon a hunter named Alys, who realised his
potential and helped Chaz sort himself out. After training with Alys, Chaz
finally qualified as a fully-fledged hunter, and it is at this point that
the game begins.

He is a headstrong and confident young man, very outwardly emotional and
sensitive. He is honest in his opinions of others, especially of Rune in
the beginning, although over time both Chaz and Rune begin to respect each
other's talents, and end up very close friends. Throughout the game, Chaz's
strength seems to flow from his feelings, and early in the game his passion
is what manages to scrape him through.

His relationships with the other party characters are varied. He sees Alys
as an older sister, someone he looks up to and loves dearly. He suffers
greatly after her death, and starts to share Gryz's need for revenge. He
also forms a close bond with Rika, and they're affection for each other
later forms the romantic element in the game.

As he journeys and meets new and very different friends, he learns to
control his emotions and finds that he has a tremendous power inside of
him. Through focusing this power he is capable of fulfilling a great
destiny that he never knew he had.

Chaz's favoured weapons are swords and daggers, and he wears mainly helms
and heavy armours.

Chaz has a range of Techniques, including curative Techs, thunder, force
and travel Techs. He is also able to acquire the most powerful Technique in
the game, but only after he has mastered his emotions.

His Skills consist of special attacks, a sleep ability, and instant-death.

```
----------------------------------------------
```

Alys is in the party from the beginning, but she doesn't remain for very
long. She is the most famous hunter on Motavia, and has acquired the
nickname of the Eight Stroke Warrior because of her reputation as a skilled
fighter. Nothing is really known about Alys' past, nor even how old she is,
but she and Rune seem to know each other from a long time ago. Alys found
Chaz while he was living as a criminal, and helped him sort his life out.

She is an attractive and strong woman, and she always needs to be on top of
the situation. Alys is also very open-minded, accepting other people's
views but at the same time being very attentive to their intentions. She
knows her talents, and seems to have a very mercenary attitude to using
them for others, as Hahn initially finds out at his cost. However, we later
learn that her reason for fighting is not one based on money, but a deeper
and more noble cause.

There isn't a great opportunity to learn much about Alys, as she falls
victim to Zio quite early in the game. Her valiant sacrifice to protect
Chaz is a sure sign of her nobility.

Alys' favoured weapons are slashers, and she wears mainly crowns and heavy
armours.

Alys' Techniques are rather limited, having access to only fire and force,
and a couple of assistance Techs.

Her Skills include an attack, a sleep ability, and causing instant death.


```
----------------------------------------------
```

Hahn is with the party until Alys falls sick, but he will return again near
the end of the game. He is a regular Parmanian, and the son of a blacksmith
in Krup. He grew up in the village, and began to learn his fathers' trade,
but he soon realised that working as a blacksmith would be a waste of his
true talent. The thing was that Hahn was far more intelligent than most,
and his thirst for knowledge was the cause of his decision to go to Motavia
Academy and become a scholar. This made Hahn's father furious, and he
threatened to disown Hahn if he left. Alas, Hahn's heart was already set,
and he left for the Academy.

During the years that he spent at the Academy, Hahn fell in love with a
school teacher in Krup, a girl named Saya, and they became engaged. A short
while after this, the monster scare takes place, and Hahn's part in the
game begins.

Hahn is a highly intelligent man, capable of reasoning a situation instead
of becoming emotional. He also has a very inquisitive nature, wishing to
understand the world around him, but fortunately he does not take any risks
in this search. This is demonstrated when he first meets the hunters, as he
balances his drive to learn with realising the dangers it may pose. Even
with his great intellect, Hahn is sometimes a little naïve. He trusts
others quite readily, and Alys takes advantage of this fact.

Hahn's favoured weapons are dagger, and he wears mainly bands and light
armours.

Hahn has the widest selection of Techniques, including curative Techs,
water, force and death Techs, and hindrance Techs.

His Skills include divining, evasion, and causing instant death.

```
----------------------------------------------
```

Rune is a useful guide throughout the game, aiding the party for a short
while at the beginning before joining permanently not long afterwards. For
a long time, nothing is really known about Rune. He seems to know an awful
lot about quite few things, and is also an old friend of both Alys and
Grandfather Dorin. Even when it is discovered that Rune is, in fact, the
fifth-generation Lutz, his life story still remains a mystery.

Rune is a wise yet enigmatic man, known for his ability to use a strange
technique known as 'magic'. He is very helpful in the game, providing
information about a variety of subjects, although some of the things he
knows seem to create an air of suspicion around Rune, especially to Chaz
and Rika. He is also considerably powerful, having access to unique spells
and being the best offensive Technique user of all the characters.

His attitude towards Chaz is a confusing one at first, as he seems to enjoy
teasing Chaz for no reason at all. This is meant harmlessly, but Chaz
doesn't find Rune's remarks amusing. Only when they reach Esper Mansion
and Chaz discovers Rune's legacy and true opinion of Chaz, does Chaz really
understand what Rune was doing. It is from this point that Rune and Chaz
begin to become very close friends.

Rune is a mentor, an adviser and a guide. He seems to be quite insensitive
on occasion, but ultimately cares very deeply about everyone. He is also
able to detect the Black Energy Wave, seemingly due to a combination of his
magical prowess and the fact that he is Lutz. On a personal note, I think
that Rune is the best character in the game.

Rune's favoured weapons are rods, and he wears mainly bands and robes.

Rune has a large selection of offensive Techniques and a few others,
including fire, water and gravity, a couple of curative Techs, travel
Techs and a hindrance Tech.

His Skills include powerful offensive and instant-death spells.


```
----------------------------------------------
```

<a id="s8-1-5"></a>

### 8.1.5. Gryz


```
|Joins Party: In Tonoe               |Starting Level:  6 | Initial Stats |
|-------------------+----------------+-------------------|               |
| Initial Equipment |Initial Techniques: BROSE           | HP    -    66 |
|                   |                                    | TP    -    20 |
| Head   TITN-HELM  +------------------------------------| Str   -    18 |
```

Gryz is the muscle of the party, providing a useful offensive edge when
faced with enemies that are resilient to magical effects. It is fairly
obvious from the start that Gryz has no hidden agenda. He grew up in the
small Motavian village of Molcum, west of Krup, with his parents and Pana,
his younger sister.

Gryz's family lived peacefully in the village for many years, until one day
it was attacked by Zio. Trained as a warrior, Gryz fought valiantly to
protect his family and his village, but was unable to save his parents.
As the village burned, Gryz took Pana and escaped with some other survivors
to the north. It was there that they sealed themselves behind a huge rock
and attempted to start anew. This hidden settlement became Tonoe.

Gryz is a strong Motavian and skilled at combat, although he lacks speed
and mental power as a consequence. He is an honest person, and forthright
with his opinions. Gryz's primary concern at the beginning is to avenge his
parents' death, and once this has been achieved he leaves the party to
return to his sister. It is only at the end of the game that he returns to
fight with his old comrades, after realising that his strength can be used
for a far greater purpose than mere vengeance.

Gryz's favoured weapons are axes, and he wears helmets and heavy armour.

Gryz has only one Technique that is a poor instant-death attack.

His Skills consist of strength bolstering, an attack and instant death.


```
----------------------------------------------
```

Rika is an extremely weak character when she is first encountered at the
Bio-Plant, and she stays with the party until the end. Her poor performance
at the beginning is countered by her extremely fast growth rate, as she
increases in power very quickly. Rika is a unique character, as she is the
product of over a thousand years of genetic engineering advancement. She
was created by Seed using this knowledge, and was taught a great many
things by her 'father' and her tutor, Wren. Her adolescent appearance and
nature, coupled with the fact that she is only one year old, is proof of
her dramatically increased physical and mental growth.

Since her creation in the Bio-Plant, Rika had learned about the world
outside from images and text given to her by Seed and Wren. As she gained
more and more knowledge of the world her desire to experience these things
increased. After Seed asks the party to take Rika along with them, Rika is
upset to be leaving the only friends she had ever had, but her thirst for
seeing the outside world exceeds the pain of this loss. She has a respect
for the world around her that the other characters do not possess, as it is
a new place that Rika does not take for granted. This, combined with her
fear of being alone, is what drives her through their journey.

Rika is a beautiful, strong and intelligent young woman, and cares deeply
for her friends. This sensitivity is sometimes difficult for her to manage
effectively, as she has had no real experience of such things since her
creation. Rika is attracted to Chaz from the start, but her lack of
understanding causes her to translate these feelings into close friendship
for most of the game. She acts as Chaz's emotional anchor, helping him
through Alys' death and other occasions where he is afraid or confused. It
is only at the end, when she is about to part from Chaz, that Rika realises
what her feelings truly mean.

Rika is the soul of the party, often adding innocent, yet sometimes naïve,
insight that only a child could possess. For although she has the physical
appearance and intelligence of a teenager, she begins with only the
experience and emotions of a young child. Like Rune, Rika is able to sense
the Black Energy Wave. However, this seems to come from a type of sixth
sense that gives her the ability to detect emotions in an empathic way.
This helps her to understand other characters' feelings, but also acts
against her when faced with the malign emotions of the Darkness.

Rika's favoured weapons are claws, and she wears mainly crowns and heavy
armours.

Rika has no offensive Techniques, but possesses a considerable number of
curative and assistance Techs.

Her Skills include distraction, special attacks and causing instant death.


```
----------------------------------------------
```

Demi is the control android for the Motavian environmental systems, who
reports directly to Wren, the manager of the entire Algo system. After she
joins the party, she does not accompany them for very long before she is
required to restart Nurvus. Demi does return at the end of the game, once
her task has been completed.

She does not really have a background in the game, as she is merely an
android performing her duties as programmed. After Nurvus begins to run
out of control, Demi attempts to shut down the system but is captured by
Zio. The party then rescue Demi from Zio's Fort, and she accompanies the
party from this point until she is able to complete her mission and shut
down Nurvus.

For a three hundred-year-old android, Demi is quite child-like. She takes
great joy in working with machines, and helps the party understand what is
going on in terms of the environmental control systems in operation. For
the most part of the game, Demi is hooked into Nurvus in an attempt to
restore each system to its normal function. During this time, her role as
technological interpreter is taken by her master, Wren, whom she respects
very much.

Demi's favoured weapons are guns, and she wears special android armours.

Demi cannot use Techniques, as she is not human.

Her Skills include self-regeneration, protection and causing instant death,
and she can also acquire a powerful weapon upgrade as a Skill as well.


```
----------------------------------------------
```

Wren is the manager of Zelan, responsible for controlling the entire Algo
system network. He joins the party to help sort out the problems on Kuran,
and stays with them until the end of the game. His reason for staying with
the party is not an emotional one, as Wren does not possess emotions.
Instead, he seems to be driven by his programming, helping the party until
the Algo system is back to a stable state. As this is his primary function,
he does whatever is necessary to accomplish it.

Like Demi, Wren's past is not revealed in the game, as it involves mainly
routine maintenance and management of the Algo control system on Zelan. He
is an older model than Demi, and although far more advanced intellectually,
he does not possess feelings. To this end, Wren is a useful pillar of logic
and reason for the party, in addition to being an invaluable source of
information. He is also an expert in the use of firearms.

Wren is an enormous asset to the party, as he is capable of piloting the
Landale, driving the vehicles, interacting with other AI systems and other
tasks involving the advanced remnants of the past. He is also equipped with
sensors that allow him to provide information on their surroundings and
other beings they encounter.

Through spending time with the party, Wren tries to understand human
behaviour, and is helped in this endeavour by his pupil, Rika. Of special
interest to him are the disagreements between Chaz and Rune, and the
growing feelings between Chaz and Rika. The things he has learned from the
party are reflected in his conversation with Daughter in Vahal Fort, and
also in his understanding of Rika's decision at the end of the game.

Wren's favoured weapons are guns, and he wears special android armours.

Wren cannot use Techniques, as he is not human.

His Skills include self-regeneration, protection, a beam weapon and causing
instant death, and he can also install new weapons as Skills as well.


```
----------------------------------------------
```


Raja is the party's first contact on Dezolis, and decides to accompany the
party as compensation for the destruction of his temple. His sudden illness
causes him to leave rather abruptly, but after his recovery he returns to
aid the party at the end.

Raja's main strength lies in his tremendous healing powers that are derived
from his faith. These curative abilities make Raja a very useful supportive
character for the group, although he has few other uses beyond this. From
the moment he joins the party, Raja tries to explain to the rest of them
that the cause of the snowstorm on Dezolis is the Garuberk Tower, although
the party are more inclined to listed to Wren's theories at the beginning.
He remains adamant about this fact until he falls ill in Meese, after which
the party realise that he may be telling the truth.

He is an easy-going, jovial old man, who enjoys the company of others and
being the centre of attention. Before joining the party, he frequented
Gyuna's bar in Ryuon a lot, and his knowledge of the area helps the party
to acquire the Landale.

Raja is most notable for his attempts to crack jokes in all situations,
although these are mostly ignored by the rest of the party. His only real
audience is Rika, who thinks that he is funny, but sometimes she doesn't
even acknowledge his stabs at humour.

Raja's favoured weapons are rods, and he wears mainly bands and robes.

Raja has a full selection of curative Techniques, and also possesses a
couple of hindrance Techs.

His Skills include restoration, protection, a powerful divine spell and
causing instant death.


```
----------------------------------------------
```

<a id="s8-1-10"></a>

> 🥉 **Petrified People** — Save the people of Zema. _(RetroAchievements · 5 pts)_
> 🥉 **Kyra** — Recruit Kyra. _(RetroAchievements · 3 pts)_


### 8.1.10. Kyra Tierney



Kyra is the last proper character to join the group, her motivation being
one of compassion. She is an Esper, one of a group of magic-users who help
the needy and heal the sick. After joining late in the game, Kyra leaves
the party once the Garuberk Tower has been destroyed, but returns at the
end after her job in Meese has been done.

For her age, Kyra is remarkably mature, if a little impetuous. She is one
of the Espers that are looking after the people of Meese, but her rage at
the villagers' despair causes her to head to the source of the illness.
After the party rescue her from the carnivorous trees, she decides to
accompany them to achieve her goal.

Although not much older than Chaz, she assumes a position of leadership in
her own eyes, seeing herself as the big sister of the group, especially of
Chaz. It even seems that Kyra has a fondness for Chaz that goes beyond mere
friendship, but she does not pursue this course. She is an active girl, who
makes quick decisions and follows them up immediately.

Kyra is the first person to mention Lutz, and believes that he will have be
able to help the party with their problems. She has what seems to be a
schoolgirl crush on Lutz, making him out to be handsome, intelligent and
charming. This is all very imaginative of her, as she also claims only to
have seen him once, and that was from afar. When Kyra discovers that Rune
is Lutz, she is initially disappointed and upset by his insensitive nature,
but later realises that Rune is a great man and worthy of his title.

Kyra's favoured weapons are slashers, and she wears mainly crowns and
robes.

Kyra's Techniques include simple curative, fire and gravity Techs.

Her Skills comprise restoration and several offensive and hindrance spells.

```
----------------------------------------------
```

<a id="s8-1-11"></a>

> 🥉 **Seth** — Recruit Seth. _(RetroAchievements · 1 pts)_


### 8.1.11. Seth

Seth is not really one of the true party members of the game, but he is a
playable character, and therefore fits the sole criterion of this section.

Seth meets the party on the island east of Krup, introducing himself as an
archaeologist. The party are surprised to see him, but he behaves extremely
friendly and in a very polite manner, so they allow him to join the party.
Rune, however, is immediately suspicious of Seth, which is not a good sign.

Apart from the fact that Seth happened to be on the island in the first
place, he earns more suspicion from the dark abilities he possesses. He
also seems very powerful for an archaeologist. All of these suspicions are
confirmed when Seth becomes Dark Force outside the Soldiers' Temple, but
Seth's true nature remains a mystery. It is not entirely certain whether
Seth was a disguise used by Dark Force, or if Seth was really a normal
Parmanian that was possessed by Dark Force. The two schools of thought on
this subject are as follows:

If Seth was just Dark Force's guise, why does he scream in pain before
being ripped apart and revealing Dark Force. If he was merely a mask,
surely you would expect him to laugh evilly or something like that, then
simply morph into Dark Force. Also, he is noted to be 39 years of age.
Surely if he was but a manifestation of Dark Force, he would have no age.

If Seth was a normal archaeologist before Dark Force possessed him, you
would expect that he could be found in some town or village beforehand, or
at least be mentioned by someone somewhere. You'd think, being a scholar,
that he would be known at Motavia Academy. Also, how would Seth have got
to the island in the first place, having no mode of transportation?

Seth's favoured weapons are dagger, and he wears mainly bands and light
armours.

Seth cannot use any Techniques, which is unusual for a human.

His Skills include dark offensive and hindrance spells.

<a id="s8-2"></a>

## 8.2. Non-playable Characters

This section gives a brief description of each of the key characters that
do not join the party. They include allies, enemies and neutral beings,
both human and inhuman. Some of the characters are involved in the story
itself, some are encountered in the side quests, some are beings that have
a connection to an important character or event, and the others are only
notable references.

Academy Principal     - Met in Motavia Academy in Piata.
                        Type: Parmanian

Initially a suspicious man, he commissions the
                        Guild to rid the academy basement of monsters. He
                        is a rather cowardly man, falling back on his
                        authority when necessary, but folding when faced
                        with power beyond his. Aside from this, he is a
                        good principal, and the academy has run well under
                        his administration.

Doctor Lubetz         - Referred to by a statue in Motavia Academy.
                        Type: Statue

A respected scientist of two thousand years ago, he
                        is immortalized by a statue in the front lobby of
                        Motavia Academy.

Professor Holt        - Referred to by Hahn.
                        Met in Birth Valley and Bio-Plant.
                        Type: Parmanian

Professor Holt is one of Hahn's teachers at the
                        academy. A rather absent-minded man, he led the
                        expedition into Birth Valley that ultimately led to
                        his disappearance. He is a scientist through and
                        through, sometimes blinding himself to matters more
                        important than his work.

Zio                   - Referred to by Academy Principal.
                        Met in Zio's Fort and Nurvus.
                        Type: Evil Being / Unique

The initial villain of the game, he is known as the
                        Black Magician. Responsible for the destruction of
                        Molcum and the petrification of Zema, and revered
                        as a god by a number of the residents of Kadary,
                        Zio is a force to be reckoned with early in the
                        story. It is only after facing him that the party
                        realises he is just a pawn in a much bigger game.
                        Zio is a cold, ruthless and intelligent man, his
                        only desire being to wipe out all life on Algo. To
                        this end he wreaks havoc and instills confusion,
                        waiting in anticipation for his master's return.

Hahn's Father         - Met in the Armour Store in Krup.
                        Type: Parmanian

Hard-working and honest, Hahn's father is the local
                        blacksmith in Krup. Along with his wife, he owns
                        the armour store where Hahn grew up. Hahn's father
                        had always tried to teach his son the art of being
                        a blacksmith so that Hahn could take over the
                        family business, but Hahn was too interested in
                        books and studying to really pay attention. After
                        Hahn's decision to go to Motavia Academy, Hahn's
                        father disowned him. This was really more an act of
                        frightening Hahn into staying rather than actually
                        disowning him. However, Hahn didn't fall for it.

Hahn's Mother         - Met in the Armour Store in Krup.
                        Type: Parmanian

A little more understanding than Hahn's father,
                        Hahn's mother tries to keep the peace between the
                        two men in her life. She appreciates her husband's
                        wish for Hahn to learn his father's trade, but also
                        respects Hahn's decision to study at the Adademy,
                        realising that he should use whatever gifts he has.

Saya                  - Met in the school in Krup.
                        Type: Parmanian

Saya is the schoolteacher in Krup, and also happens
                        to be Hahn's fiancee. How the two first met is not
                        mentioned in the story, but it would be fair to
                        assume that Hahn and Saya have been engaged for a
                        few years. She is a kind, attractive and smart
                        woman, adored and idolized by the children she
                        teaches. She is also a reasonably talented healer,
                        and looks after Alys when Alys falls ill.

Grandfather Dorin     - Met in the northeast tent in Tonoe.
                        Type: Motavian

The chief of the Motavians, Grandfather Dorin is a
                        wise and knowledgable man. He calls himself the
                        information monger, and is generous with both his
                        knowledge and his possessions. He is an old friend
                        of Rune's, and the two help each other for their
                        mutual benefit and the good of the planet. Even
                        with his wisdom, however, Dorin can be a little
                        careless with his speech.

Pana                  - Met in the northeast tent in Tonoe.
                        Type: Motavian

Gryz's little sister, Pana was brought to Tonoe by
                        her brother after Zio destroyed Molcum. She doesn't
                        say too much, and doesn't really interact in the
                        story, but she is Gryz's only family and Gryz
                        leaves the party to look after her.

Seed                  - Met in Bio-Plant.
                        Type: AI

Seed is the control system of the Bio-Plant, and
                        Rika's 'father'. He is a vastly intelligent system
                        with extensive knowledge of genetic engineering. He
                        used the scientific knowledge of the ancients and
                        refined it over the last thousand years to create
                        Rika. After the Bio-Plant began creating monsters
                        due to abnormal signals, Seed realised that he must
                        shut himself down, but did not want Rika to die in
                        the process. Hence, once Rika has left with the
                        party, Seed's part in the story ends with his self-
                        destruction.

Guild Receptionist    - Met in the Hunters' Guild in Aiedo.
                        Type: Parmanian

This woman is the point of contact between the
                        hunters and the Guild. The party can speak to the
                        receptionist to be given information about current
                        available jobs, and can also take these jobs from
                        the Guild through her. Plus, she is the person to
                        see to claim the commission for completed jobs.

Sand Worm Ranch Owner - Referred to by Guild Receptionist.
                        Met in Mile.
                        Type: Parmanian

The owner of the sand worm ranch is initially a

man full of hopes for the future, but after his
                        prized pets become too big to handle, he realises
                        that he can no longer look after them. He posts a
                        request to the Hunters' Guild, and the party can
                        take this job afterwards. After the party take
                        care of the fully grown sand worm, the ranch owner
                        is understandably upset. Even though he lost his
                        dream, the ranch owner seemed to be the sort of
                        man who would prosper again. However, fate has
                        another cruel stab at the entrepreneur, as he is
                        later killed by the Black Energy Wave.

Juza                  - Met in Zio's Fort.
                        Type: Evil Being / Warlock

Seemingly Zio's right-hand man, Juza is a powerful
                        mage whose sole purpose is to protect his master.
                        He blocks the entrance to the upper level of Zio's
                        Fort, as the staircase that leads there is only
                        accessible after Juza's demise.

Tinkerbell            - Referred to by Guild Receptionist.
                        Met in the eastern house in Aiedo.
                        Type: Parmanian

This little girl loses her pet dog Rocky, and her
                        parents commission the Guild to find the dog for
                        her. After the party accepts this job from the
                        Guild, Tinkerbell does not need to be spoken to at
                        all, as she gives no valuable information.

Tinkerbell's Father   - Met in the eastern house in Aiedo.
                        Type: Parmanian

Tinkerbell's father is the man who sends the
                        request to the Guild to find his daughter's pet.
                        In this job, the party will need to speak to the
                        man to get more details about the commission and
                        a few clues about Rocky.

Tinkerbell's Mother   - Met in the eastern house in Aiedo.
                        Type: Parmanian

Like her husband, Tinkerbell's mother is a useful
                        person to speak to in the second Hunters' Guild
                        job, as she can give a few hints as to how to find
                        Rocky, her daughter's dog.

Rocky                 - Referred to by Guild Receptionist.
                        Met in either Krup, Monsen or Termi.
                        Type: Dog

This fat, white dog is Tinkerbell's pet. It can be
                        seen in either Krup, Monsen or Termi, even before
                        the second job is available from the Guild. Rocky
                        has a penchant for sweet things, and this knowledge
                        is useful when the party attempt to capture him.

Earthquake Man        - Met in Monsen.
                        Type: Parmanian

This man is found outside in the eastern part of
                        Monsen, just above the crack in the ground. When
                        the party speak to him, an earthquake follows, and
                        the party can learn of the problems that Monsen
                        have been having. This leads to a visit to the
                        Plate System in order to stop the earthquakes.

Alis Landale          - Referred to by a statue in Termi.
                        Type: Statue

This heroine of legend is revered by the residents
                        of Termi, as she once stayed in this village. The
                        statue in the centre of the village represents Alis
                        Landale, and tourists come from miles around to see
                        the sights that Termi has to offer because of her.
                        You may also have noticed that the spaceship found
                        under Tyler is named after her.

Gy-Laguiah            - Met in Ladea Tower and Climate Control Centre.
                        Type: Darkspawn / Demon

This agent of Zio is first encountered in Ladea
                        Tower, after Rune succeeds in breaking the barrier
                        around the Psycho-wand. It had been awaiting their
                        arrival, and attempts to take the Psycho-wand as
                        soon as it is released. The party fight this demon
                        to prevent this from happening. Another Gy-Laguiah
                        is found guarding the entrance to the Climate
                        Control Centre, but this one is not very talkative.

Dark Force            - Referred to by Zio.
                        Met in Kuran, Garuberk Tower and Soldiers' Temple.
                        Type: Dark Force

The physical manifestation of The Profound Darkness
                        in Algo, Dark Force is a being of pure evil. Every
                        thousand years, when the seal is at its weakest,
                        Dark Force appears to wreak havoc and attempt to
                        break open the dimensional door, but is always
                        defeated by a group of brave heroes. However, since
                        the planet Parma was destroyed, the seal has been
                        drastically weakened, and this has caused there to
                        be more than just one incarnation of this vile
                        creature. Each Dark Force is a difficult opponent.

Dorm Caretaker        - Referred to by Guild Receptionist.
                        Met in the Academy Dormitory in Piata.
                        Type: Parmanian

This man is responsible for looking after the
                        students at Motavia Academy who stay in the dorms
                        in the northwest corner of Piata. After one of the
                        female students disappears, he posts a request to
                        the Guild to help find her. The party must speak to
                        the Dorm Caretaker in the third Hunters' Guild job
                        to get details about the commission.

Student Cult Devotee  - Referred to by Dorm Caretaker.
                        Met in the church in Kadary.
                        Type: Parmanian

This girl is the missing student in the third Guild
                        job, and is initially a devotee of Zio's cult.
                        After Zio's demise, she is found wandering around
                        the church in Kadary, dazed. Due to malnutrition,
                        the girl falls ill, and is taken to the Inn.

Caring Old Man        - Met in the Inn in Kadary.
                        Type: Parmanian

In the third Hunters' Guild job, after the missing
                        student is found she collapses and is taken to the
                        Inn in Kadary. The old man who looks after her
                        tells the party that they must bring the girl some
                        food with high nutritional value. The old man has
                        no further involvement in the game.

Eddie                 - Referred to by Guild Receptionist.
                        Met in the eastern house in Monsen.
                        Type: Parmanian

This woman lives just outside the large crack in
                        Monsen, and has always been worried that her son
                        Tallas might accidentally fall down it. Alas, this
                        does happen a little later, and so Eddie requests
                        the aid of the Hunters' Guild. In the fourth Guild
                        job, the party must speak to Eddie to allow them
                        access to the crack in the ground. After rescuing
                        Tallas, the party can return to the woman and get
                        the commission sent to the Guild.

Tallas                - Referred to by Eddie.
                        Met in The Hole.
                        Type: Parmanian

The young boy Tallas is at the focus of the fourth
                        Hunters' Guild job. While playing outside, he
                        accidentally falls down the crack in Monsen. If the
                        party take the job, they must follow Tallas into
                        the cave beneath Monsen, and rescue him from the
                        Fract Ooze that had eaten him. Strangely, Tallas is
                        not too shaken by his close shave with digestion,
                        and thanks the party in a matter-of-fact way before
                        running back home (picking up his shoes en route).

Chaos Sorcerer        - Met on the shuttle after Zelan.
                        Type: Evil Being / Sorcerer

Nothing more than a sneaky saboteur, this Chaos
                        Sorcerer is the only one of its kind that engages
                        the party in conversation. After the party leave
                        Zelan on the shuttle, the Chaos Sorcerer is found
                        in the engine room, attempting to sabotage their
                        flight to Kuran. After he is defeated by the party,
                        it turns out that he had been successful, and the
                        group are forced to crash on Dezolis.

Gyuna                 - Met in the bar in Ryuon.
                        Type: Dezolisian

The proprietor of the bar in Ryuon, and a friend of
                        Raja's, Gyuna is Dezolis' answer to Grandfather
                        Dorin. The party must speak to this man in order to
                        learn the method of gaining access to the Landale.
                        He has other topics that he can discuss, but none
                        of them is important to the game.

Tyler                 - Referred to by the grave in Tyler.
                        Type: Grave

The founder of the town in which he is buried,
                        Tyler was the captain of a Parmanian spaceship that
                        crashed on Dezolis many centuries ago. To honour
                        his death, and to protect the secret of the ship's
                        location, the Parmanians erected a monument to
                        Tyler in the town to which his name was given. The
                        grave is, in fact, the entrance to the hangar where
                        the Landale is hidden.

Musk Cat Chief        - Met in Mysterious Valley.
                        Type: Musk cat

A completely optional area of the game is a strange
                        place called Mysterious Valley, home to the musk
                        cats. They are a race of small orange felines, each
                        capable of speech, and led by a much larger chief.
                        The musk cats have a fond remembrance of Chaz,
                        although this may be due to his inherited legacy as
                        a destined Protector of Algo. The musk cat chief
                        gives the party the Silver Tusk, entrusted to his
                        care a long time ago, as he feels that they are
                        worthy to take care of this secret treasure.

D-Elm-Lars            - Met in Climate Control Centre.
                        Type: Evil Being / Witch

This witch is found in the Climate Control Centre,
                        as a trap for the party should they think that the
                        Dezolis snowstorm is caused by a malfunction in
                        this system. His sole purpose is to kill the party,
                        but he is not any sort of challenge to them.

Off-Duty Esper        - Met in the clinic in Meese.
                        Type: Esper

In order for the party to continue the plot of the
                        game, they must speak to this Esper who is found in
                        the right-hand room on the top floor of the clinic
                        in Meese. Doing this will cause Raja to fall sick
                        from the Black Energy Wave, and promptly alert the
                        party to Kyra's courageous (if somewhat futile)
                        attempt to enter the Garuberk Tower.

Lutz                  - Referred to by Kyra.
                        Met in Esper Mansion (technically).
                        Type: Esper

You could say that this should be in the playable
                        character section, as Lutz is in fact in the form
                        of Rune. However, Lutz is a different person, from
                        two millenia ago, who was a great wizard. He, too,
                        defeated Dark Force with a group of allies, and
                        through his magic was able to transfer his spirit
                        into a Telepathy Ball. As leader of the Espers, he
                        chose a worthy subject to carry his will, and they
                        became Lutz. As each host grew older, they selected
                        a new Lutz, and passed their combined knowledge
                        onto their successor. Rune is the fifth-generation
                        Lutz, and possesses all the knowledge of his
                        predecessors.

Dezolisian Priest     - Met in Gumbious Temple.
                        Type: Dezolisian

This nameless cleric is the keeper of the Eclipse
                        Torch, a holy relic stored in Gumbious Temple. When
                        the party request to borrow the torch, he flatly
                        refuses, but his stubbornness is punished by the
                        Eclipse Torch's theft by a trio of Xe-A-Thouls. In
                        return for the party reclaiming the temple's sacred
                        flame, the Dezolisian priest agrees to lend them
                        the Eclipse Torch.

Xe-A-Thouls           - Met in Gumbious Temple and Air Castle.
                        Type: Evil Beings / Witches

These three witches are the servants of Lashiec,
                        and are first encountered by the party in Gumbious
                        Temple. The Xe-A-Thouls steal the Eclipse Torch,
                        and take it back with them to the Air Castle, an
                        ancient fortress that once floated above Parma.
                        The party must defeat the Xe-A-Thouls in the Air
                        Castle in order to pass the invisible barrier that
                        blocks entry to the castle's basement.

Lashiec               - Referred to by Rune.
                        Met in Air Castle Basement.
                        Type: Evil Being / Unique

Lashiec was the king of the Air Castle when it
                        flourished two thousand years ago, but he was slain
                        by the first Lutz and the castle was thought to be
                        destroyed. However, since the rise in the Darkness'
                        power, Lashiec and his stronghold have reappeared,
                        albeit in a more twisted form. Lashiec is behind
                        the theft of the Eclipse Torch, although it seems
                        certain that his only interest in Dezolis' sacred
                        relic is to use it as bait to lure Lutz and his
                        companions. His need for revenge, coupled with the
                        malign influence of the Darkness, has turned
                        Lashiec into a wretched creature, imprisoned in his
                        own castle. When the party find him, he expresses
                        his intent to trap them there with him, but with
                        his defeat, he and the Air Castle are destroyed.

Dezolisian Bishop     - Met under Gumbious Temple.
                        Type: Dezolisian

After the party defeat the second Dark Force, and
                        the Garuberk Tower is no more, Gumbious Temple
                        explodes. Under its ruins, the party find a secret
                        chamber, where the bishop of Gumbious Temple is
                        discovered. He speaks to the party of Dark Force,
                        and reveal the existence of its master, The
                        Profound Darkness. The Dezolisian bishop also tells
                        the party of Rykros, where the secrets of Algo are
                        supposed to be found.

The Profound Darkness - Referred to by Dezolisian Bishop.
                        Met in The Edge.
                        Type: Profound Darkness

The ultimate evil, The Profound Darkness is a being
                        filled with hate, anger and hostility. Many eons
                        ago, the Darkness was trapped by its 'brother', The
                        Great Light, in another dimension, following a
                        battle that stretched over many years. It, like The
                        Great Light, were once part of a divine spiritual
                        being that was split into two. The dimensional
                        portal that trapped the Darkness was closed by a
                        great seal, known today as the Algo star system.

Chief of Uzo          - Referred to by Guild Receptionist.
                        Met in southwest house in Uzo.
                        Type: Parmanian

The chief of Uzo has two daughters, both of whom
                        went shopping in Aiedo. After about a month, the
                        chief began to get concerned, and sent a request to
                        the Hunters' Guild for help in finding them. This
                        man, who lives in the southwest house of Uzo, is
                        the person to speak to after accepting the fifth
                        Hunters' Guild job.

Chief's Daughters     - Referred to by Chief of Uzo.
                        Met in prison in Aiedo.
                        Type: Parmanians

These two girls can initially be met in the Inn in
                        Aiedo, and if the party speak to the girls before
                        resting at the Inn, you can witness them attempting
                        to run out without paying. They get caught, as you
                        would expect, and are thrown into jail. This event
                        has no importance until the fifth Hunters' Guild
                        job, when their father requests that the party find
                        his daughters. They must pay the girls' bail in
                        order to complete this job.

Mr. Culvers           - Referred to by Guild Receptionist.
                        Met in northwest house in Torinco.
                        Type: Parmanian

The Culvers family used to take regular trips to
                        Termi, where they spent many a happy drinking in
                        the delights of that fair village. Alas, the young
                        boy of the family becomes ill, and his Mr. Culvers
                        thinks that perhaps something to remind his son of
                        their time in Termi may help him to get better.
                        Because he is unable to get to Termi himself, Mr.
                        Culvers posts a request to the Hunters' Guild for
                        help, and this becomes the sixth Guild job.

Mr. Culvers' Son      - Met in northwest house in Torinco.
                        Type: Parmanian

The young Culvers boy is ill when first encountered
                        by the party, although the doctors that have seen
                        him are convinced that there is nothing wrong with
                        him, and that his condition is psychological. In
                        the sixth Hunters' Guild job, Mr Culvers, the boy's
                        father, requests that the party bring something to
                        his son that will remind him of Termi. He hopes
                        that this might cause him to get better. When Chaz
                        wields the replica of Alis' sword in front of the
                        boy, Mr Culvers' son does begin to feel better, and
                        Chaz allows him to keep the sword.

Mr. Sekreas           - Referred to by Guild Receptionist.
                        Met in northeast house in Torinco.
                        Type: Parmanian

Mr. Sekreas is an avid animal lover, and when a new
                        breed of bird is discovered on his island, he helps
                        the species by helping them flourish in a nearby
                        cave. Unfortunately, the rappy birds soon outgrow
                        their rocky home, and begin to plunder the fields
                        around the village of Torinco, so the villagers
                        decide they must be destroyed. Mr. Sekreas posts a
                        request to the Hunters' Guild asking for help to
                        destroy the chief bird, but his intention is not to
                        have the bird killed at all. His hope is that the
                        hunters will be defeated by the bird so that the
                        villagers will be disuaded from their attempts to
                        exterminate it. The party must fight the bird in
                        the seventh Guild job, but when the party defeat
                        it, the bird escapes and Mr. Sekreas intervenes,
                        explaining his original plan. He had no intention
                        to pay the commission, but the party are kind
                        enough to let him off.

Old Man in Zema       - Referred to by Guild Receptionist.
                        Met in northeast house in Zema.
                        Type: Parmanian

As if Zema hadn't had enough trouble, near the end
                        of the game it becomes overrun with machines. The
                        machines are not hostile, but the villagers are
                        understandably afraid. To this end, an old man who
                        resides in Zema sends a request to the Hunters'
                        Guild, and this becomes the final Guild job. The
                        party must speak to this man, located in the
                        northeast corner of the village, in order to gain
                        access to Vahal Fort.

Daughter              - Met in Vahal Fort.
                        Type: AI

Before the Great Collapse, Mother Brain designed a
                        new control system to govern the Algo network, just
                        in case an emergency did occur. When Parma exploded
                        and the system collapsed, it was thought that the
                        plan had never been put into action, but this
                        supposition was false. Even though a new, less
                        intrusive, control system was now in place on the
                        artificial satellite Zelan, the Daughter project
                        had already reached the prototype stage on Motavia.
                        Nurvus had kept Daughter dormant while it managed
                        the planet's environment, but after the party shut
                        down Nurvus, Daughter is awakened. As its function
                        is to manage the systems of Algo, Daughter begins
                        to send signals to the rest of the control centres,
                        but is unaware of its network isolation. As there
                        is no response from the other systems, Daughter
                        decides to remove the rogue AIs, and sends machines
                        to regain its control. In the eighth Guild job, the
                        party trace the source of the machines to Vahal
                        Fort, and find the prototype Daughter there. They
                        try to reason with it, but eventually realise that
                        they have to shut it down.

Le Roof               - Met in Silence Temple.
                        Type: Guardian

This being is best described as the lord of Rykros,
                        responsible for guarding its existence and passing
                        on the secrets of Algo to those worthy enough to be
                        called Protectors. It isn't quite clear whether Le
                        Roof is a physical entity or simply a spirit, but
                        he is a wise and compassionate being. His role is
                        to remind the Protectors of Algo of their duty, but
                        he can only do this after they have proved their
                        identity by passing De-Vars and Sa-Lews.

De-Vars               - Met in Strength Tower.
                        Type: Guardian

The guardian of the Strength Tower is a large being
                        of red flame, whose sole purpose is to test the
                        party in combat. He is a master of physical power,
                        and holds three of the Rings of the Stars that he
                        gives to the party once they have passed his test.

Sa-Lews               - Met in Courage Tower.
                        Type: Guardian

The guardian of the Courage Tower is a large being
                        of blue flame, whose sole purpose is to test the
                        party in combat. He is a master of magical power,
                        and holds two of the Rings of the Stars that he
                        gives to the party once they have passed his test.

The Great Light       - Referred to by Le Roof.
                        Type: The Great Light

Not much is said about The Great Light in the game,
                        as he departed from Algo may eons ago. He, like The
                        Profound Darkness, was once part of a celestial
                        spirit. After the spirit split into two, the Light
                        and the Darkness waged a massive battle. After a
                        long fight, The Great Light emerged victorious, and
                        banished his 'brother' to another dimension,
                        placing the Algo star system as a seal to its
                        doorway. Before he left, he created Rykros as a
                        sign of the seal's weakening, and Protectors to
                        push back the Darkness should it attempt escape.

Elsydeon              - Referred to by Rune.
                        Met in Sacred Sword Cave.
                        Type: Sword

You may (rightly) question why I regard Elsydeon as
                        a character, and my response is that it is met by
                        Chaz, and speaks with him. You may disagree with my
                        classification, but I'm sure Rune doesn't. The
                        sword embodies all the spirits of the heroes that
                        fought the Darkness, and it chooses whom is worthy
                        to wield it. Since the Great Collapse, Elsydeon has
                        been stored in the lowest level of the Esper
                        Mansion, awaiting the arrival of the next Protector
                        of Algo. Rune, as Lutz, chose Chaz for this task,
                        and Elsydeon is satisfied with his decision.

Alys Illusion         - Met in Anger Tower.
                        Type: Illusion

This illusion is used by Re-Faze to instill anger
                        into Chaz, the purpose being to test his strength
                        of will and determine his worth.

Re-Faze               - Met in Anger Tower.
                        Type: Guardian

On the top of the Anger Tower resides another
                        guardian of Rykros, but he seems a little more
                        chaotic than his brethren. When the party attempt
                        to enter the Anger Tower, Re-Faze determines if
                        they are worthy of entrance. Only after Chaz has
                        acquired Elsydeon do the party pass his scrutiny,
                        but this is only the beginning of Re-Faze's trials.
                        Once Chaz defeats the illusion of Alys on the top
                        floor of the tower, Re-Faze appears. Chaz is
                        angered by the situation, and Re-Faze tells him
                        that there is a way for Chaz to turn his rage into
                        power. If Chaz declines Re-Faze's offer to learn of
                        this ability, Re-Faze grants him Megid.
9. Character Statistics                                               CCRST

<a id="s9"></a>

# 9. Character Statistics

The following lists detail the statistics and required EXP for each
character, based upon their current Level. For the moment, these lists only
show the statistics up to the last Level that requires less than a million
EXP, but I will add the remaining entries once I have obtained them all.

- Chaz - Initial Technique: RES
- Skill 1   Skill 2   Skill 3   Skill 4   Skill 5
- EARTH     CROSSCUT  AIRSLASH  RAYBLADE  EXPLODE

- FLAELI    HEWN      DIEM      TANDLE    EFESS     NEGATIS   LEGEON

10. Techniques                                                        CTCNQ

<a id="s10"></a>

# 10. Techniques

Techniques are special powers that characters and monsters may possess.
They work by emitting a form of psionic energy that can have a variety of
different effects, based on the Technique being used. This energy drains
the user of the Technique, and this is represented in the form of TP.

Most characters in the game have access to some Techniques, although some
more than others. Enemies may also have access to a few Techniques as
well, but this is not common.

All but one Techniques are learned by characters when they reach a certain
Level. The method of obtaining the remaining Technique, Megid, is described
in more detail in '7.2. Megid - The Anger Technique'.

The first part of this section lists the different Techniques available to
each character, split into the three types of Technique, along with the
Level at which they learn the Techniques.

The second part gives a description of each Technique, split into the three
different types, along with TP costs and information on who or what can use
the Techniques.


```
-------------------------------------
```

<a id="s10-2"></a>

## 10.2. Heal Techniques

There are four small groups of Heal Techniques. The first group heals an
individual character and the second group heals all characters. Status Cure
Techniques remove various status effects, and Revival Techniques restore a
character from a flatlined state.


```
| Target Cure \_________ | Group Cure \__________
|                       ||                       |
| Tech    Cost   Heals  || Tech    Cost   Heals  |
|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯||¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|
| RES     3 TP   20-120 || SAR    12 TP   10-100 |
| GIRES   6 TP   90-180 || GISAR  24 TP   80-170 |
| NARES   9 TP  270-340 || NASAR  36 TP  200-260 |
|_______________________||_______________________|
```

```

|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯||¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|
| ANTI    2 TP || REVER  12 TP |
| RIMPA   8 TP || REGEN  36 TP |
| AROWS   9 TP ||______________|
|______________|
```

        It restores HP based on the user's MTL score.
        Can be used anywhere. Only works on organic life.

        It restores HP based on the user's MTL score.
        Can be used anywhere. Only works on organic life.
