<a id="s10-3"></a>

## 10.3. Attack Techniques

There are six different types of attack Techniques, five of which are
represented by elemental properties. Fire, Water, Energy, Force and Gravity
Techniques inflict damage to enemies in the form of their element. As most
enemies have some weakness, resistance of immunity to different elements,
using the right Technique can be very important. Death Techniques are
fairly self-explanatory, as they attempt to inflict instant death upon
enemies. The instant-death Techniques only work on organic enemies.


```
| Fire \________________ | Water \_______________ | Energy \______________
|                       ||                       ||                       |
| Tech    Cost   Damage || Tech    Cost   Damage || Tech    Cost   Damage |
|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯||¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯||¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|
| FOI     3 TP   20-120 || WAT     4 TP   30-130 || TSU     6 TP   40-140 |
| GIFOI   6 TP   80-160 || GIWAT   7 TP  100-170 || GITHU  12 TP  110-190 |
| NAFOI   9 TP  160-230 || NAWAT  10 TP  180-240 || NATHU  16 TP  190-250 |
|_______________________||_______________________|| MEGID  30 TP  270-360 |
                                                  |_______________________|
| Force \_______________ | Gravity \_____________ | Death \______
|                       ||                       ||              | 
| Tech    Cost   Damage || Tech    Cost   Damage || Tech    Cost |
|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯||¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯||¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|
| ZAN     8 TP   20-110 || GRA    10 TP   50-120 || VOL     8 TP |
| GIZAN  12 TP   80-160 || GIGRA  15 TP  120-170 || SAVOL  16 TP |
| NAZAN  16 TP  150-220 || NAGRA  19 TP  190-240 || BROSE  16 TP |
|_______________________||_______________________||______________|
```

¯¯¯     Also usable by Juza, Tech User and TechMaster.
3 TP
        A weak fire-based Technique that causes a small flame to erupt on
        the enemy. Effective against most monsters in a cold climate.
        Can only be used in battle.

GIFOI - Usable by Alys, Rune and Kyra.
¯¯¯¯¯   Also usable by Dark Witch and Le-Faw-Gan.

        Can only be used in battle.

<a id="s10-4"></a>

## 10.4. Misc Techniques

The three types of Misc Techniques are Assist, Hinder and Travel. The first
two types are used in battle. Assist Techniques increase the statistics of
one or all members of the party, and Hinder Techniques create non-damaging
effects on all the enemies. Finally, Travel Techniques transport the party
instantaneously. They can only be used in the field.


```
| Assist \_____ | Hinder \_____ | Travel \_____
|              ||              ||              |
| Tech    Cost || Tech    Cost || Tech    Cost |
|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯||¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯||¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|
| DEBAN   5 TP || GELUN   3 TP || HINAS   4 TP |
| SHIFT   7 TP || DORAN   4 TP || RYUKA  10 TP |
| SANER   8 TP || SEALS   9 TP ||______________|
|______________|| RIMIT  12 TP |              
                |______________|
```

DEBAN - Usable by Rika.
¯¯¯¯¯   Also usable by BloodSaber, FrostSaber, Radhin, ShadowSabr.
5 TP
        A remarkably useful Technique, it slightly increases the Defence
        Power of all party members.
        Can only be used in battle.

SHIFT - Usable by Alys and Rika.
¯¯¯¯¯   Also usable by BloodSaber, ChaosBrngr, DarkMaraud, DeathBearr and
7 TP     Radhin.

Fairly poor for its cost, this Technique slightly increases the
        Attack Power of one character.
        Can only be used in battle.

SANER - Usable by Alys and Rika.
¯¯¯¯¯   Also usable by Radhin.
8 TP
        This Technique is exceptionally useful in longer battles, as it
        increases the Agility of all party members.
        Can only be used in battle.

GELUN - Usable by Hahn.
¯¯¯¯¯   Also usable by Greneris.
3 TP
        A mostly pointless Technique, this may slightly decrease enemies'
        Attack Power. It targets all enemies, but its success rate is low.
        Can only be used in battle.

DORAN - Usable by Hahn.
¯¯¯¯¯   Also usable by DarkMaraud and Greneris.
4 TP
        Like Gelun, this is not a very useful Technique. It targets all
        enemies and may lower their Agility. Its success rate is low.
        Can only be used in battle.

SEALS - Usable by Rune and Raja.
¯¯¯¯¯   Also usable by ChaosBrngr, DeathBearr and Radhin.
9 TP
        Very useful against enemies with Techniques, this may remove the
        ability to use them. It targets all enemies.
        Can only be used in battle.

RIMIT - Usable by Hahn and Raja.
¯¯¯¯¯   Also usable by Greneris and Tech-Plant.
12 TP
        A considerably overpriced Technique, it has a chance of inflicting
        Paralysis on each enemy. Its success rate is low.
        Can only be used in battle.

HINAS - Usable by Chaz and Rune.


```
¯¯¯¯¯
```

4 TP    One of the invaluable travel Techniques, this automatically takes
        the party outside or to the entrance of the dungeon.
        Can only be used in dungeons.

RYUKA - Usable by Chaz and Rune.


```
¯¯¯¯¯
```

10 TP   An extremely useful Technique, this teleports the party to any town
        or village they have already visited.
        Can only be used outside or in a town or village.
11. Skills                                                            CSKLS

<a id="s11"></a>

# 11. Skills

Skills are special abilities that characters and enemies may use. They are
usually specific to a certain character or type of enemy, but some Skills
may be usable by other entities for some reason or another. Skills are most
often a result of a characters' training and experience in their chosen
field, such as Chaz's unique attacks and Rune's magical spells. Unlike
Techniques, Skills do not have a cost to use. Instead, each Skill has a
stock, which depletes when the Skill is used. When a Skill has no stock
available, it cannot be used. Resting at an Inn or using a Regen Platform
will replenish all Skill stocks to their maximum value.

Most Skills are learned when a character reaches the required Level, and
begin with a stock of 1. Android Skills, however, which come in the form
of weapon upgrades, must be found and installed before they can be used.
A Skill's stock will increase at a certain rate as the character increases
in Level.

The first part of this section lists the different Skills available to each
character, split into the three types of Skill, along with the Level at
which they learn the Skills.

The second part gives a description of each Skill available to the
characters, split into the three different types, along with information on
who or what can use the Skill. As some enemies may use certain Skills that
characters may use, with slightly longer names, there may be an alternative
Skill name following the list of enemies.

The final part gives a description of each Skill that can only be used by
enemies, listed in alphabetical order, along with information on which
enemies can use the Skill.


```
----------------------------------------------
```

<a id="s11-1"></a>

## 11.1. By Character



<a id="s11-2"></a>

## 11.2. Heal Skills

There are only five Heal Skills, so there isn't much point splitting them
into groups. None of the Heal Skills has direct Technique counterparts, so
they are all extremely useful. They include android healing, healing of
all characters (including androids), HP-based healing, and TP restoration.

ATARAXIA - Usable by Raja.


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

A unique and invaluable Skill that restores a target's TP by 1/4
           of its maximum value.
           Only works on organic life. Can only be used in battle.

MEDIC PW - Usable by Demi.


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

A fairly useful Skill throughout the game, as it revives and
           heals all organic characters' HP by 1/4 of their maximum value.
           Only works on organic life.

MEDICE   - Usable by Kyra.


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

This Skill is quite helpful in the Eclipse Torch section of the
           game, as it heals around 170-230 HP to one character.
           Works on any character.

MIRACLE  - Usable by Raja.


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

Highly useful in the later stages of the game, this Skill heals
           all characters by about 130-180 HP.
           Works on all characters.

RECOVER  - Usable by Demi and Wren.


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

This unique Skill performs a self-regeneration process on the
           android, restoring between 270-340 HP to itself.
           Works on the android that uses it.

<a id="s11-3"></a>

## 11.3. Attack Skills

There are three types of attack Skill - physical attack Skills, magical
attack Skills and android attack Skills. The difference between these types
is that physical attack Skills require the use of a weapon (the Skill is
unavailable if no weapon is equipped), whereas the other attack Skills
don't. Also, unless otherwise stated, the damage inflicted by physical
attack Skills is based on the ATK PWR of the character, and the damage
inflicted by magical attack Skills is based on the character's MTL PWR.
Android attack Skills involve special hardware and vary in effect.


```
|       Physical       ||       Magical        ||       Android        |
|                      ||                      ||                      |
| Hit-one      Hit-all || Hit-one      Hit-all || Hit-one      Hit-all |
|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯||¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯||¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|
| CRASH       AIRSLASH || ASTRAL      CORRSION || FLARE       BURSTROC |
| CROSSCUT     DISRUPT || DIEM           EFESS || SPARK         PHONON |
| DBLSLASH    SWEEPING || DTHSPELL        HEWN ||             POSIBOLT |
| DEATH                || EXPLODE       LEGEON ||______________________|
| ELIMINAT             || FLAELI       NEGATIS |
| RAYBLADE             || HOLYWORD    ST. FIRE |
| VORTEX               ||               TANDLE |
|______________________||______________________|
```

CRASH    - Usable by Gryz.


```
¯¯¯¯¯
```

Gryz takes his axe and strikes a precise blow on one enemy,
           with the possibility of causing instant death.
           Can only be used in battle.

CROSSCUT - Usable by Chaz.


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

Chaz uses his sword or dagger to slash across an enemy, then
           immediately strike down it, causing increased attack damage.
           Can only be used in battle.

DBLSLASH - Usable by Rika.
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯   Also usable by Debugger, Dominator, HungryMole and Red Mole.
            (DBL SLASH)

Rika performs two successive attacks with each claw she has
           equipped, causing increased attack damage to one enemy.
           Can only be used in battle.

DEATH    - Usable by Alys.


```
¯¯¯¯¯
```

Alys throws a slasher at an enemy with such accuracy that it
           has a chance of instantly killing the enemy.
           Can only be used in battle.

ELIMINAT - Usable by Hahn and Rika.


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

The character phases in front of an enemy, holding out their
           weapon in an attempt to kill the enemy. May cause instant death.
           Can only be used in battle.

RAYBLADE - Usable by Chaz.


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

Chaz infuses his weapon with the elemental property of energy,
           striking at an enemy to inflict typical damage of 200-270 HP.
           Can only be used in battle.

VORTEX   - Usable by Alys.


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

Alys spins one slasher at an acute angle towards one enemy,
           forming a spiral effect causing greatly increased attack damage.
           Can only be used in battle.

AIRSLASH - Usable by Chaz.
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯   Also usable by BloodSaber, FrostSaber and ShadowSabr.

Chaz performs a wide arcing swing with his weapon, hitting all
           enemies and inflicting normal attack damage to each.
           Can only be used in battle.

DISRUPT  - Usable by Rika.


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

Rika temporary splits into a number of separate copies that
           simultaneously strike each enemy, causing normal attack damage.
           Can only be used in battle.

SWEEPING - Usable by Gryz.


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

Gryz swings his axe in a strong, singular sweep across the
           enemies, inflicting normal attack damage to each.
           Can only be used in battle.

ASTRAL   - Usable by Hahn.


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

Hahn creates an astral force that is fired into an enemy,
           causing radiation-based damage of about 220-270 HP damage.
           Can only be used in battle.

DIEM     - Usable by Rune.


```
¯¯¯¯
```

Rune creates a few small pockets of negative energy that pull
           the life from one enemy, causing instant death to organic life.
           Can only be used in battle.

DTHSPELL - Usable by Seth.
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯   Also usable by Illusionst, Imagiomage and Spector.

Similar to DIEM, this spell sucks all life from an enemy,
           reducing it to an empty carcass. Only works on organic enemies.
           Can only be used in battle.

EXPLODE  - Usable by Chaz.


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

Chaz transforms into pure energy and attempts to rematerialise
           inside an enemy, causing it to explode. May cause instant death.
           Can only be used in battle.

FLAELI   - Usable by Rune and Kyra.
¯¯¯¯¯¯     Also usable by ChaosSorcr, Gi-Le-Farg, Illusionst, Imagiomage
            and Sa-Lews.

Rune creates four small spheres of fire that simultaneously
           strike an enemy, causing between 80-140 HP damage.
           Can only be used in battle.

HOLYWORD - Usable by Raja.


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

With a single word, Raja summons the power of heaven to strip
           life from an enemy. Very effective against enemies of Darkness.
           Can only be used in battle.

CORRSION - Usable by Seth.
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯   Also usable by ChaosSorcr, Dark Force (3), Haunt, Illusionst,
            Imagiomage, Spector and Zio (2). (CORROSION)

A spell of Darkness, this wave of destruction pulls apart all
           enemies in its wake, causing between 200-240 HP damage.
           Can only be used in battle.

EFESS    - Usable by Rune.


```
¯¯¯¯¯
```

Rune calls energy from the heavens to create a beam of pure
           light onto each enemy. This causes about 210-250 HP damage.
           Can only be used in battle.

HEWN     - Usable by Rune and Kyra.
¯¯¯¯       Also usable by ChaosSorcr, Illusionst, Imagiomage, Phantom,
            Sa-Lews and Zio (2).

A powerful vortex is created on each enemy, rending them with
           razor-sharp lashes to cause between 90-160 HP damage.
           Can only be used in battle.

LEGEON   - Usable by Rune.
¯¯¯¯¯¯     Also usable by Imagiomage and Sa-Lews.

Rune's most powerful spell, it unleashes a barrage of radiation
           onto all enemies. This causes typical damage of 290-320 HP.
           Can only be used in battle.

NEGATIS  - Usable by Rune.


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

A hit-all version of DIEM, Rune creates pockets of negative
           energy that cause instant-death to all organic enemies.
           Can only be used in battle.

ST. FIRE - Usable by Raja.


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

Raja sends forth a wave of pure light that covers all enemies
           in holy fire, typically inflicting 180-240 HP damage.
           Can only be used in battle.

TANDLE   - Usable by Rune and Kyra.
¯¯¯¯¯¯     Also usable by ChaosSorcr, Gi-Le-Farg, Illusionst, Imagiomage,
            Le-Faw-Gan and Sa-Lews. (TANDIL)

The only electric-based Skill available, this causes multiple
           bolts of lightning that cause between 190-240 HP damage.
           Can only be used in battle.

FLARE    - Usable by Wren.


```
¯¯¯¯¯
```

Wren's built-in weapon projects a beam of high-intensity
           radiation onto one enemy, causing between 170-220 HP damage.
           Can only be used in battle.

SPARK    - Usable by Demi and Wren.
¯¯¯¯¯      Also usable by Browren486.

The android injects a powerful EMP into one enemy, possibly
           causing instant death to machines.
           Can only be used in battle.

BURSTROC - Usable by Wren.
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯   Also usable by Dark Force (1).

A series of missiles are fired into the air, striking down on
           all enemies in a blaze of fire, inflicting 180-220 HP damage.
           Can only be used in battle.

PHONON   - Usable by Demi.
¯¯¯¯¯¯     Also usable by Dark Force (1) and Dominator. (PHONONMASR)

This powerful weapon projects high-frequency and destructive
           sound waves at all enemies, causing about 190-270 HP damage.
           Can only be used in battle.

POSIBOLT - Usable by Wren.


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

Wren fires a super-intense beam of extreme radiation across all
           enemies, inflicting typical damage of around 280-330 HP.
           Can only be used in battle.

<a id="s11-4"></a>

## 11.4. Misc Skills

There are Assist and Hinder Skills here, most of which may come in handy

occasionally, and some very often. Two of the Hinder Skills require the use
of a weapon, namely EARTH and MOONSHAD, so make sure that the relevant
character is properly equipped if you are thinking of using one of these.


```
|  Assist  ||        Hinder        |
|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯||¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|
| BARRIER  || BINDWA      MOONSHAD |
| BLESSING || EARTH         SHADOW |
| VISION   || HIJAMMER    STASISBM |
| WAR CRY  || ILLUSION      TELELE |
| WARLA    || MINDBLST             |
|__________||______________________|
```

BARRIER  - Usable by Demi and Wren.
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯    Also usable by Siren386 and Browren486.

The android projects an energy field that covers the party,
           reducing magical damage to all characters.
           Can only be used in battle.

BLESSING - Usable by Raja.


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

Raja calls the power of the saints to protect the party,
           increasing all characters' DFS in a similar manner to DEBAN.
           Can only be used in battle.

VISION   - Usable by Hahn.


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

Hahn concentrates on the enemies, studying their actions to
           understand their strategy. This increases Dexterity.
           Can only be used in battle.

WAR CRY  - Usable by Gryz.


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

Gryz cries out loudly, fueling his strength with aggression
           and adrenaline. This increases Attack Power.
           Can only be used in battle.

WARLA    - Usable by Kyra.


```
¯¯¯¯¯
```

Similar to DEBAN, Kyra sets up a wall of force that increases
           each character's Defence Power.
           Can only be used in battle.

BINDWA   - Usable by Kyra.


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

Kyra creates a network of energy strings that bind the enemies,
           possibly inflicting a Sleep-like status on all enemies.
           Can only be used in battle.

EARTH    - Usable by Chaz.


```
¯¯¯¯¯
```

A mostly ineffective Skill, Chaz attempts to create a force that
           sticks the enemies to the ground, possibly inflicting Sleep.
           Can only be used in battle.

HIJAMMER - Usable by Wren.


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

Wren unleashes a targetted EMP that has a good chance of
           ceasing electrical functions and inflicting Sleep on machines.
           Can only be used in battle.

ILLUSION - Usable by Rika.


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

Rika projects a number of images of herself onto all enemies,
           possibly disorientating them and lowering their Agility.
           Can only be used in battle.

MINDBLST - Usable by Seth.
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯   Also usable by Dark Force (3), Illusionst and Imagiomage.

Seth attempts to shut down each enemy's mental processes. If
           successful, the enemy is inflicted with Sleep.
           Can only be used in battle.

MOONSHAD - Usable by Alys.


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

Alys throws her weapon at an enemy in an attempt to blanket it
           in a sheet of darkness. If successful, this causes Sleep.
           Can only be used in battle.

SHADOW   - Usable by Seth.
¯¯¯¯¯¯     Also usable by ChaosSorcr and Dark Force (3). (SHADOWBIND)

Seth creates shadowy images around each enemy in an effort to
           confuse them. There is a chance that this will lower Agility.
           Can only be used in battle.

STASISBM - Usable by Demi.


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

Demi emanates a beam of numbing energy onto one enemy. It has a
           chance of inflicting Paralysis, but only affects organic life.
           Can only be used in battle.

TELELE   - Usable by Kyra.


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

A unique spell that causes fatigue in all enemies, possibly
           reducing their Attack Power.
           Can only be used in battle.

12. Abilities - General                                               CABGN

<a id="s12"></a>

# 12. Abilities - General

<a id="s12-1"></a>

> 🥉 **Just As Planned!** — Execute a Combo in a Macro. _(RetroAchievements · 3 pts)_
> 🥈 **Combo Strategist** — Execute 3 different Combos in a single battle, and win. _(RetroAchievements · 10 pts)_


## 12.1. Combinations

There are fourteen combination attacks in the game, even though the game
manual says there are fifteen. I will not say that I have been unable to
find the fifteenth, as I have tried every possible combination of Techs
and Skills there is. Quite simply, there are only fourteen combinations.

I haven't combined Alys with any character after Rika, or combined Hahn,
Gryz or Demi with most of the later characters, or combined Raja, Kyra or
Seth with anyone except Chaz, Rika, Rune and Wren, but that is because the
game story prohibits this. Therefore, the only possibilities are that the
manual is simply erroneous and that there never were fifteen combos, the
fifteenth combo uses two characters that cannot be in the party at the same
time (such as the Alys/Seth scenario above), the fifteenth combo involves
some specific equipment arrangement or Level requirement (in which case
there is a fifteenth combo but I haven't found it yet), or there were
originally fifteen combinations but either a required Technique, Skill or
the whole combo was removed (without changing the manual).

Combinations are very powerful attacks that are created by two or more
characters using specific abilities together. You may have noticed that I
have used no combinations in the walkthrough, as they are not essential to
winning battles. If you wish to use combos instead of standard abilities,
feel free to do so. They are usually far more powerful than the sum of
their parts, but their unpredictable success rate makes them a risky choice
in battle. For a combination to work, all of the characters involved must
be set to act in succession. In other words, a combination attack will not
work if any other character or enemy acts between the characters involved
in the combination.

E.g. Your party consists of Chaz, Alys, Hahn and Rune, and they are
     fighting two Sand Newts and a MonsterFly. You set Alys to use FOI,
     Chaz to use TSU, Hahn to use WAT, and Rune to defend, in the hope of
     creating the Triblaster combination. The following examples below
     demonstrate the results of different orders of actions:
     (C=Chaz, A=Alys, H=Hahn, R=Rune, S=Sand Newt, M=MonsterFly)

1. R - def, M - att, A - FOI, S - att, S - att, C - TSU, H - WAT
     2. A - FOI, R - def, M - att, C - TSU, H - WAT, S - att, S - att
     3. R - def, M - att, C - FOI, A - TSU, S - att, H - WAT, S - att
     4. M - att, R - def, S - att, CAH - Triblaster, S - att

As you can see, some of the combinatios may be very difficult to get to
work under normal circumstances. However, setting up a Macro will increase
this chance. If, using the example above, you had set up a Macro like the
one below, Rune would still act first, then some of the enemies may attack,
and then it will get to Hahn. Now, as Hahn is normally slower than Chaz,
Chaz should follow him immediately. The same principal goes for Chaz and
Alys. Technically, this should create a Triblaster nearly every time.

Rune - def, Hahn - WAT, Chaz - TSU, Alys - FOI

Now that I've explained how to increase the chance of a combination attack,
I will explain each of the combinations in detail. The method of creating
each combination is given after the combination name, and uses different
symbols to indicate how to create it:

/ - Separates different Techs or Skills that can be used as substitutes
+ - Indicates that the Techs or Skills can be combined in any order
> - Indicates that the Techs or Skills must be combined in the given order

All Combinations affect all enemies on the screen, and it should be noted
that items cannot be used as substitutes for the Techniques and Skills
required (e.g. you could not use a FLAMESWORD in place of FLAELI to create
the Fire Storm combination).
Black Hole - GRA/GIGRA/NAGRA + NEGATIS
(Destroy)    Requires Rune and Kyra

By combining a powerful gravitational field with NEGATIS'
             life-sapping effect, a black hole is formed that sucks all
             enemies from the screen, causing instant death to all.
Blizzard   - WAT/GIWAT/NAWAT + ZAN/GIZAN/NAZAN/HEWN
(Water)      Requires Chaz/Alys/Hahn and Rune, or Chaz/Alys and Hahn

One character creates a series of ice shards, which are then
             flung around by multiple whirlwinds to form a tempest of cold
             razors. This Combo is useful early in the game.
CircuitBrk - HIJAMMER + TANDLE
(EMP)        Requires Rune/Kyra and Wren

This Combo involves Wren sending out an EMP, that is then
             boosted by TANDLE to utterly destroy electrical circuitry.
             Ultimately, it causes instant death to all machines.
CondctThnd - WAT/GIWAT/NAWAT > TANDLE
(Electric)   Requires Hahn then Rune, or Rune then Kyra

The enemies are covered in water, which is then used to
             conduct the lightning effect of TANDLE directly into each
             enemy. It will come in handy in the later hi-tech dungeons.
Destruct   - DEBAN > MEGID + LEGEON + POSIBOLT
             Requires Rika then Chaz and Rune and Wren

Rika throws up a shield to protect the party, as the other
             characters combine the power of their most powerful abilities
             to create a devastating explosion. This causes 999 HP damage.
Firestorm  - FOI/GIFOI/NAFOI/FLAELI + ZAN/GIZAN/NAZAN/HEWN
(Fire)       Requires Chaz/Alys/Hahn and Rune/Kyra, or Chaz/Hahn and Alys

A super-hot blaze is created, which is formed into massive
             tornados by the other character. These vortices of burning
             death are very helpful in the early stages of the game.
GrandCross - CROSSCUT + EFESS
(Light)      Requires Chaz and Rune

Chaz performs two consecutive strikes, as Rune channels his
             powerful spell through Chaz's blade to wash all enemies in a
             wave of light. This Combo is useful against the Darkness.
Holocaust  - SAVOL + DIEM
(Death)      Requires Hahn and Rune

Hahn uses his primary instant-death Technique, while Rune
             strengthens the effect of each energy field with DIEM. This
             is almost guaranteed to instantly kill all organic enemies.
Lethal Img - ILLUSION + DEATH
(Death)      Requires Alys and Rika

While Rika disorientates the enemies with ILLUSION, Alys can
             perform her instant-death Skill with the intention of hitting
             all enemies. This has a very good chance of instant-death.
ParadinBlw - RAYBLADE + ASTRAL
(Energy)     Requires Chaz and Hahn

Chaz's blade, already infused with energy from the RAYBLADE
             Skill, is further enhanced by Hahn's simultaneous astral
             energy. This is very useful against the legions of the Dark.
PurfyLight - HOLYWORD + EFESS
(Cleanse)    Requires Rune and Raja

As Rune calls for the heavenly light to strike all enemies,
             Raja uses the prayer of his HOLYWORD through the light to hit
             all enemies, instantly killing enemies weak against light.
ShootinStr - BURSTROC > FOI/GIFOI/NAFOI/FLAELI
(Fire)       Requires Wren then Alys/Rune/Kyra

Wren launches his blazing missiles on the enemies, while the
             other character enhances them with a fire-based ability. This
             burning rain is very useful against cold enemies.
SilentWave - AIRSLASH + PHONON
(Force)      Requires Chaz and Demi

As Chaz performs his wide sweep through the enemies, Demi
             channels her PHONON through his weapon to inflict more direct
             damage. This is a generically useful combination.
Triblaster - FOI + WAT + TSU (cannot use advanced versions of these Techs)
(Radiation)  Requires Chaz and (Alys/Kyra and Hahn/Rune, or Hahn and Rune)

The three characters pool their power to create a beam of
             combined elements that sweeps across all enemies. Useful early
             in the game, this Combo becomes less valuable towards the end.

<a id="s12-2"></a>

## 12.2. Elemental and Status Types

Each attack in the game are based on an element, and this modifies the
damage it inflicts on an enemy depending on the enemy's affinity to that
element (weakness, resistance or immunity). There are also different types
of status effect, some of which may affect certain enemies while others
will not. This section looks at each elemental and status type, and each
Technique, Skill and Weapon that is based on them.

<a id="s12-2-1"></a>

### 12.2.1. Fire

Fire abilities make use of intense heat and combustion to cause burning
damage to targets. They can be in the form of physical flames or highly
increased temperatures.

Techniques: FOI, GIFOI, NAFOI

Skills:     FLAELI

Combos:     Fire Storm, ShootinStr

Weapons:    FLAMESWORD, NAPALMSHOT (DYNAMITE is fire-based)

Special:    A CRMCSHIELD automatically makes its paired weapon fire-based
            while equipped, regardless of its original affinity

Effective Against:   Dezolisian Biomonsters (not Helex), Slimes, Rappys,
                     Undead, Winged Plants, Lizard-Men, Lashiec

Ineffective Against: Right Blades, Bits, Sentries, Rens, Ghosts, Servitors,
                     Armour Mechs, Knights, Rip Fiends, De-Vars, Sa-Lews

<a id="s12-2-2"></a>

### 12.2.2. Water

Water abilities make use of intense cold and freezing to cause chilling
damage to targets. They can be in the form of physical ice shards or highly
decreased temperatures.

Techniques: WAT, GIWAT, NAWAT

Skills:     -

Combos:     Blizzard

Weapons:    -

Effective Against:   Motavian Biomonsters, Slimes, Sandworms, Gy-Laguiah

Ineffective Against: Dezolisian Biomonsters, Bits, Rens, Ghosts, Flamers,
                     Armour Mechs, Knights, Patrollers, Rip Fiends, Zio

<a id="s12-2-3"></a>

### 12.2.3. Energy

Energy abilities make use of power in its raw form, projected in either a
beam or a blast. They are not affiliated with any particular element, and
so are impossible to resist.

Techniques: TSU, GITHU, NATHU

Skills:     RAYBLADE, MEGID

Combos:     ParadinBlw

Weapons:    -

Effective Against:   All Darkspawn and Evil Beings (not Spearmen or Mages),
                     Dark Force, Profound Darkness

Ineffective Against: -

<a id="s12-2-4"></a>

### 12.2.4. Force

Force abilities make use of air and general physical forces to pummel and
slice targets. They can be in the form of powerful winds or physical
strikes.

Techniques: ZAN, GIZAN, NAZAN

Skills:     HEWN, PHONON, BURSTROC, CORRSION

Combos:     SilentWave

Weapons:    All except those mentioned elsewhere

Effective Against:   -

Ineffective Against: Slimes, Ghosts, Scorpions, Sentries, Flamers, Undead,
                     Servitors, Armour Mechs, Rip Fiends, De-Vars, Sa-Lews

<a id="s12-2-5"></a>

### 12.2.5. Gravity

Gravity abilities make use of localised fields of gravitational force to
warp and twist targets. They are only in the form of pockets of such force.

Techniques: GRA, GIGRA, NAGRA

Skills:     -

Combos:     -

Weapons:    -

Effective Against:   Rip Fiends

Ineffective Against: Slimes, Ghosts, Undead, Prophallus, De-Vars, Sa-Lews

<a id="s12-2-6"></a>

### 12.2.6. Electric

Electric abilities make use of lightning and powerful electrical currents
to cause shocking damage to targets. They are in the form of bolts of high-
intensity electrical charge.

Techniques: -

Skills:     TANDLE

Combos:     CondctThnd

Weapons:    THUNDRCLAW

Effective Against:   All Machines, Slimes, Frogs, Lizard-Men

Ineffective Against: Scorpions, all Blades, Sabers, Ghosts, Rip Fiends

<a id="s12-2-7"></a>

### 12.2.7. Radiation

Radiation abilities make use of nuclear reactions and non-material energy
to cause internal damage throughout enemies. They are usually in the form
of rays, beams or blasts.

Techniques: -

Skills:     FLARE, ASTRAL, LEGEON, POSIBOLT

Combos:     Triblaster

Weapons:    All LASR, PLSM, LACO and GUARD weapons, PULSEVULCN, PHOTNERASR

Special:    A PLSM-FIELD automatically makes its paired weapon radiation-
            based while equipped, regardless of its original affinity

Effective Against:   -

Ineffective Against: Rip Fiends

<a id="s12-2-8"></a>

### 12.2.8. Light

Light abilities make use of celestial energies and the power of The Great
Light to cast down denizens of the Darkness. They are in the form of beams
or waves of pure holy light.

Techniques: -

Skills:     EFESS, ST. FIRE

Combos:     GrandCross

Weapons:    PSYCO-WAND, SILVR-TUSK, ELSYDEON

Effective Against:   All Darkspawn and Evil Beings (not Spearmen or Mages),
                     Dark Force, Profound Darkness

Ineffective Against: All enemies that are not Darkspawn or Evil Beings,
                     Spearmen, Mages

<a id="s12-2-9"></a>

> 🥉 **Sudden Death** — Execute any instant-death Combo. _(RetroAchievements · 5 pts)_


### 12.2.9. Death

Death abilities are used to stop the natural process of life, and so only
work against creatures that could be regarded as organic.

Techniques: VOL, SAVOL

Skills:     DIEM, ELIMINAT, DEATH, DTHSPELL

Combos:     Holocaust, Lethal Img

Weapons:    SHADWBLADE, GENOCYCLAW

Effective Against:   All Biomonsters, Darkspawn & Evil Beings (not Ghosts,
                     Undead, Rip Fiends, Sandworms, Prophallus or bosses)

Ineffective Against: Machines, Ghosts, Undead, Rip Fiends, Sandworms,
                     Prophallus, all bosses

<a id="s12-2-10"></a>

### 12.2.10. Destroy

Destroy abilities are used to utterly annihilate creatures, and can work
against all but non-material or very tough beings.

Techniques: BROSE

Skills:     CRASH, EXPLODE, NEGATIS

Combos:     Black Hole

Weapons:    -

Effective Against:   All but Ghosts, Sandworms, Prophallus or bosses

Ineffective Against: Ghosts, Sandworms, Prophallus, all bosses

<a id="s12-2-11"></a>

### 12.2.11. Cleanse

Cleanse abilities use the power of light to remove all traces of Darkness
from a target, and are therefore only useful in destroying weaker creatures
of the Darkness.

Techniques: -

Skills:     HOLYWORD

Combos:     PurfyLight

Weapons:    ELSYDEON

Effective Against:   All Darkspawn and Evil Beings (not bosses)

Ineffective Against: Biomonsters, Machines, all bosses

<a id="s12-2-12"></a>

### 12.2.12. EMP

EMP abilities use an electro-magnetic pulse (EMP) to disrupt or entirely
stop any electrical signals within the target, and are therefore only
useful for temporarily stopping or utterly destroying mechanical beings.

Techniques: -

Skills:     SPARK, HIJAMMER

Combos:     CircuitBrk

Weapons:    -

Effective Against:   All Machines

Ineffective Against: Biomonsters, Darkspawn, Evil Beings
13. Items                                                             CITMS

<a id="s13"></a>

# 13. Items

Items of all shapes, sizes and functions will be purchased, found and used
throughout the game. Some are essential to the games completion, most are
beneficial in a variety of ways, and a few have no real purpose at all.

Your party's inventory can carry a maximum of 40 unequipped items at any
one time, and choosing the items to fill this space can be very important
late in the game. The following sections list and describe each and every
item available in the game, split into six different categories.

If the price of an item is preceeded by the letter 'S', the item cannot be
bought and the sale value is given. If there is no price given, the item
cannot be bought, sold or discarded.

<a id="s13-1"></a>

## 13.1. Expendables

Most expendable items are available from common Tool Stores, although a few
are a little more difficult to come by. The majority of expendable items
are curative, the others having unique purposes. They can be used in the
field and/or in battle, and they are lost after use.

MONOMATE   - 'A weak medicine that restores HP.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

20 MST       Available at Piata, Mile, Zema, Krup, Tonoe, Nalya, Aiedo,
              Kadary, Monsen, Ryuon and Tyler Tool Stores.
             May be dropped by Ismounos.

A useful item early in the game, as it allows you to heal
             characters without using TP. It heals about 45 HP.
             Can be used anywhere. Only works on organic life.

DIMATE     - 'A medicine that restores HP.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

160 MST      Available at Aiedo, Kadary, Monsen, Ryuon, Tyler, Zosa and
              Meese Tool Stores.
             May be dropped by Zios Guard.

A more potent medicine that is valuable a little later in the
             game when enemies deal greater damage. It heals about 90 HP.
             Can be used anywhere. Only works on organic life.

TRIMATE    - 'A strong medicine that restores HP.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

400 MST      Available at Reshel, Jut, Uzo and Torinco Tool Stores.
             May be dropped by BloodSaber, FrostSaber and Radhin.

The best medicine, this item proves very important late in the
             game when facing very tough enemies. It heals about 300 HP.
             Can be used anywhere. Only works on organic life.

ANTIDOTE   - 'A medicine that cures poison.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

10 MST       Available at Mile, Zema, Krup, Tonoe, Nalya, Aiedo, Kadary,
              Monsen, Ryuon, Tyler, Zosa, Reshel, Meese, Jut, Uzo and
              Torinco Tool Stores.
             May be dropped by FlattrPlnt, Gicefalgue, Guilgenova and
              MonsterFly.

A very useful item throughout the game, but especially at the
             beginning before learning the ANTI Technique. It cures Poison.
             Can be used anywhere.

CURE-PARAL - 'A medicine that cures paralysis.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

120 MST      Available at Zema, Tonoe, Aiedo, Kadary, Monsen, Ryuon, Tyler,
              Zosa, Reshel, Meese, Jut, Uzo and Torinco Tool Stores.
             May also be dropped by Toadstool and Shrieker.

Like ANTIDOTE, this item has a specific function, and is most
             useful before RIMPA is learned. It cures Paralysis.
             Can be used anywhere.

TELEPIPE   - 'A magic item that can use 'RYUKA' power.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

130 MST      Available at Zema, Krup, Tonoe, Aiedo, Kadary, Monsen, Ryuon,
              Tyler, Zosa, Reshel, Meese, Jut, Uzo and Torinco Tool Stores.

A great time-saving item, it teleports the party to any town
             or village on the same planet that they have visited before.
             Can only be used in the field, but not in a dungeon.

ESCAPIPE   - 'A magic item that can use HINAS power.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

70 MST       Available at Zema, Krup, Tonoe, Aiedo, Kadary, Monsen, Ryuon,
              Tyler, Zosa, Reshel, Meese, Jut, Uzo and Torinco Tool Stores.

This item teleports the party out of a dungeon, saving them if
             they are deep in hostile territory with low HP and TP.
             Can only be used in a dungeon.

SHORTCAKE  - 'A cake that is sold in an Aiedo bakery.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

280 MST      Available at Naura Cake Shop in Aiedo.

It seems highly expensive for a poor curative item, but it is
             essential for a Hunters' Guild job. It heals about 10 HP.
             Can be used anywhere. Only works on organic life.

REPAIR-KIT - 'A simple repair kit for androids.'

5 MST
             Rare and very important, it is the only item that can cure

             Can be used anywhere. Only works on androids.

The most common of the perfumes, this item will be invaluable

             This item can be sold, but cannot be discarded.


This highly unusual item is a very expensive ANTIDOTE. Using
             it on a Poisoned character will remove the Poison but the
             text will say HP has been increased (although it hasn't). This
             function of the PENGU-FEED can only be used inside Zosa Tool
             Store, as when the party try to leave, a Penguin runs across
             the front of the shop and steals the PENGU-FEED. This is
             unavoidable. Only buy this item if you want to witness this
             unique but ultimately pointless event.
             Can only be used in Zosa Tool Store.
             (Note: Teleporting doesn't work in the store)

<a id="s13-2"></a>

## 13.2. Weapons

Most of the harm that is inflicted upon your foes in the game will come in
the form of a melee or missile attack, by a character wielding a weapon of
some kind. Each character has their own preference over which type of
weapon they use, and there are a number of different weapons for each
character available throughout the game. They all have the same basic
purpose, but they vary in price and power. Some are better suited to a
particular type of enemy, and some are imbued with special properties.

Weapons that can be used as a specific Technique or Skill can only be used
in battle. In addition, some Skills require the use of a weapon.

This section gives a list of all the weapons in the game, followed by a
description of each weapon in order of ATK bonus, split into the seven
different types available.

Ch:Chaz, Al:Alys, Ha:Hahn, Ru:Rune, Gr:Gryz, Ri:Rika,
De:Demi, Wr:Wren, Ra:Raja, Ky:Kyra, Se:Seth

Enemy resistance and weakness applies to the affinity of the weapon. Unless
otherwise noted, all weapons are force-based.


```
-----------------------------------------------
```

<a id="s13-2-1"></a>

### 13.2.1. List

<a id="s13-2-2"></a>

> 🥉 **Initiate: Phononmezer** — Recover the Phononmezer parts in Plate System. _(RetroAchievements · 5 pts)_


### 13.2.2. Daggers

Daggers are made up of short, sharp blades attached to a hilt, perfect for
quick strikes. They are one-handed weapons, and so one can be equipped with
a shield, or two can be equipped at the same time. In the latter case, the
daggers' attack bonuses are cumulative.

Chaz, Hahn and Seth can use daggers.

DAGGER     - 'A knife with a small blade.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

40 MST       Hahn begins with this weapon.
             Also available at Mile and Aiedo Weapon Stores.

A poor weapon and the weakest dagger in the game. Exchange it
             for a HUNT-KNIFE as soon as possible.

HUNT-KNIFE - 'A large multi-purpose knife.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

120 MST      Chaz begins with this weapon.
             Also available at Mile, Zema, Tonoe and Aiedo Weapon Stores.

Although a weak dagger, Hahn will find two of these more
             preferable to the DAGGER at the beginning of the game.

TITNDAGGER - 'A dagger made of a titanium alloy.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

240 MST      Available at Tonoe and Aiedo Weapon Stores.

A durable dagger, it serves Hahn better than the HUNT-KNIFE in
             the early stages of the adventure.

CRMC-KNIFE - 'A knife made of ceramic.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

1600 MST     Available at Aiedo Hunters' Guild and Tyler Weapon Stores.
             May also be dropped by Speard.

> **Hahn's best weapon before he leaves the party on Motavia, this**

is a useful dagger to use before rescuing Demi.

LASR-KNIFE - 'A knife with a small built-in laser device.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

S            Found in Plate System.
1600 MST
             This radiation-based weapon can only be equipped on Chaz. As
             Chaz has better weapons at the time, sell this dagger.

PLSMDAGGER - 'A dagger with a small built-in plasma unit.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

S            May be dropped by Siren386.
1800 MST
             Like the LASR-KNIFE, only Chaz can equip this radiation-based
             weapon when it is found. It may as well be sold.

TORNDDAGGR - 'A dagger that has the power of HEWN magic.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

8300 MST     Available at Zosa and Meese Weapon Stores.

Although not useful as a weapon, like the two daggers above,
             this dagger can be used as a single-target HEWN spell.

LACODAGGER - 'A dagger made of high grade Laconia.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

9400 MST     Seth begins with this weapon.
             Also available at Jut Weapon Store.

Only useful if you choose Hahn at the end of the game, this
             radiation-based weapon is best paired with Hahn's MAHLAYDAGR.

MAHLAYDGGR - 'Dagger that Hahn created with his father.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

S            Hahn returns with this weapon. (Only usable by Hahn)
7900 MST
             The best dagger in the game. As well as having a good ATK, it
             can also be used in battle as the NAFOI Technique.

<a id="s13-2-3"></a>

### 13.2.3. Swords

Swords are made up of long, heavy blades attached to a hefty hilt, and are
used for slicing enemies in one stroke. Swords are also useful for parrying
enemy attacks. They are two-handed weapons, hence only one may be equipped
at a time and no shield may be equipped with it.

Only Chaz can use swords.

ALIS-SWORD - 'A legendary sword used by a heroine of yore.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

500 MST      Available at Termi's Bayamare Gift Store.

By far the weakest sword in the game, this item's only real
             use is in one of the Hunters' Guild jobs.

STEL-SWORD - 'A sword made of steel.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

280 MST      Available at Mile, Zema, Tonoe and Aiedo Weapon Stores.

The first sword available, purchase and equip this to Chaz
             as soon as possible. It is much better than two HUNT-KNIFEs.

TITN-SWORD - 'A sword made of a titanium alloy.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

560 MST      Available at Tonoe and Aiedo Weapon Stores.

More than twice as powerful as the STEL-SWORD, you should
             find this weapon very useful early in the game.

CRMC-SWORD - 'A sword made of ceramic.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

3600 MST     Available at Aiedo Hunters' Guild and Tyler Weapon Stores.

A very effective sword when it becomes available, it should
             be exchanged for a LASR-SWORD when one is found.

SHADWBLADE - 'Nothing is known about this weapon.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

S            May be dropped by ShadowSabr.
1 MST
             Although more powerful than CRMC-SWORD, it seriously reduces
             DFS, MTL and DEX. It can sometimes add DIEM to attacks.

LASR-SWORD - 'A sword with a powerful laser emitting device.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

S            Found in Zio's Fort.
2700 MST
             Only one of its type in the game, it should be given to Chaz
             as soon as it's found. It is radiation-based.

PLSM-SWORD - 'A sword with a large built-in plasma unit.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

S            Found in Zelan.
4350 MST
             This radiation-based sword should be equipped to Chaz as soon
             as it has been found, as it's much stronger than LASR-SWORD.

FLAMESWORD - 'A sword that has the power of FLAELI magic.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

12900 MST    Available at Zosa and Meese Weapon Stores.

This fire-based sword is effective against Dezolisian monsters
             but not Motavian monsters. It can also be used to cast Flaeli.

LACO-SWORD - 'A sword made of high grade Laconia.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

20400 MST    Available at Jut Weapon Store.

A very strong radiation-based sword, this should be bought and
             equipped to Chaz until you go to Rykros.

GUARDSWORD - 'Nothing is known about this weapon.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

S            Found in Silence Temple.
12550 MST
             A highly powerful radiation-based weapon, equip this to Chaz
             as soon as you can, only removing it when ELSYDEON is found.

ELSYDEON   - 'Nothing is known about this weapon.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

---------    Awarded to Chaz in Sacred Sword Cave.

The ultimate sword and strongest weapon in the game. It is
             a light-based weapon that can add HOLYWORD to attacks.

<a id="s13-2-4"></a>

### 13.2.4. Slashers

Slashers are curved weapons with a sharp outer edge. They are thrown at
enemies before returning to the wielder. They are one-handed weapons, and
so one can be equipped with a shield, or two can be equipped at the same
time. In the latter case, the slashers' attack bonuses are cumulative.
Slashers hit all enemies on the screen in one attack.

Both Alys and Kyra can use slashers.

BOOMERANG  - 'A thrown weapon.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

80 MST       Alys begins with this weapon.
             Also available at Mile and Aiedo Weapon Stores.

Although very useful at the beginning of the game for its hit-
             all ability, this weapon is the weakest slasher in the game.

SLASHER    - 'A blade weapon that is thrown.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

160 MST      Available at Mile, Zema, Tonoe and Aiedo Weapon Stores.

More powerful than the BOOMERANG, Alys should be equipped with
             two of these as soon as you can buy them.

TITNSLASHR - 'A slasher made of a titanium alloy.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

360 MST      Available at Tonoe and Aiedo Weapon Stores.

A good, strong slasher, this weapon will be Alys' weapon of
             choice until you acquire the LASRSLASHR.

LASRSLASHR - 'A slasher with a built-in laser emitting device.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

S            Found in Kadary.
1050 MST
             Alys' most powerful weapon, When found it should replace one
             of her TITNSLASHRs. This is a radiation-based slasher.

LACOSLASHR - 'A slicer made of high grade Laconia.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

21600 MST    Kyra begins with this weapon.
             Available at Jut Weapon Store.

A very powerful radiation-based weapon, try to get two of
             these for Kyra, replacing them only with MOONSLASHRs.

MOONSLASHR - 'A slicer that contains light from the moon.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

S            May be dropped by Dark Rider.
8400 MST
             The strongest slasher in the game should be equipped to Kyra
             when found. It can be used in battle as the MOONSHADE Skill.

<a id="s13-2-5"></a>

### 13.2.5. Rods

Rods are long poles crafted of a hard material, and are designed solely to
pummel enemies. Some are also noted to grant increased mental prowess or
even contain magical spells. They are two-handed weapons, hence only one
may be equipped at a time and no shield may be equipped with it.

Both Rune and Raja can use rods.

WOOD-CANE  - 'A cane made from the wood of a Laerumatree.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

S            Rune begins with this weapon.
70 MST       May also be dropped by Tech User.

The weakest of rods, it is not effective as an attacking
             weapon. It can be used in battle as the RES Technique.

PSYCO-WAND - 'A weapon that can nullify various magical-dfs.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

---------    Obtained at the top of the Ladea Tower.

Although not powerful, this light-based weapon is very useful
             against the Darkness. It can be used as the CANCELING Skill.

SILV-ROD   - 'A rod made of low purity Laconia.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

2700 MST     Available at Ryuon and Tyler Weapon Stores.

Stronger than the PSYCO-WAND in ATK terms, but nowhere near
             as useful and effective. Keep the PSYCO-WAND.

DREAM-ROD  - 'A rod that has the power of BINDWA magic.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

5400 MST     Available at Zosa and Meese Weapon Stores.

The only rod to give a DFS bonus. It may add BINDWA to an
             attack, and it can be used in battle as the BINDWA Skill.

FORCE-CANE - 'A cane that has been strengthened by magic.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

2500 MST     Available at Ryuon Weapon Store.
             May also be dropped by TechMaster.

Like SILV-ROD, the higher ATK power of this weapon is not
             enough to merit equipping it. The PSYCO-WAND is more useful.

LACO-ROD   - 'Rod made of hi-Laconia. Has a power of'EFESS'.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

S            Raja returns with this weapon.
6800 MST     May be dropped by Dark Witch.

Equip this radiation-based weapon if you acquire it, only
             replacing it with the GUARD-ROD. It can be used as EFESS.

GUARD-ROD  - 'Nothing is known about this item.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

S            Found in Strength Tower.
7250 MST
             The strongest of all rods, this radiation-based weapon should
             be replaced by PSYCO-WAND at the end. It can be used as SAR.

<a id="s13-2-6"></a>

### 13.2.6. Axes

Axes are made up of wide, sharp head attached to a long shaft. They can
inflict heavy blows upon enemies, and are effective at using defensively.
They are two-handed weapons, hence only one may be equipped at a time and
no shield may be equipped with it.

Only Gryz can use axes.

TITN-AXE   - 'An axe made of a titanium alloy.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

640 MST      Gryz begins with this weapon.
             Available at Aiedo Weapon Store.

The weakest axe, but generally a strong weapon. Replace this
             with BROAD-AXE as soon as you can.

BROAD-AXE  - 'A large axe made of a titanium alloy.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

1000 MST     Available at Zema and Aiedo Weapon Stores.

A more powerful axe than the TITN-AXE. Buy it and equip it,
             but you won't be using this weapon for very long.

STRUGGL-AX - 'A large and heavy axe made for use in battles.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

4600 MST     Available at Aiedo Hunters' Guild Weapon Store.

A strong weapon that will come in handy until you acquire the
             Land Rover. Keep it equipped until you acquire the LASR-AXE.

LASR-AXE   - 'An axe with an internal laser emitting device.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

S            Found in Plate System.

3200 MST

Equip this when you find it, as it is the best weapon for Gryz

> **until he leaves the party. It is a radiation-based axe.**

LACO-AXE   - 'An axe made of high grade Laconia.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

S            Gryz returns with this weapon.
13000 MST
             Far more powerful than the LASR-AXE, this radiation-based
             weapon will be very useful in the later part of the game.

DEFEAT-AXE - 'Nothing is known about this weapon.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

S            May be dropped by ChaosBrngr.
3 MST
             The best axe in the game. If you find one, equip it to Gryz
             immediately and keep it there. It can add BINDWA to attacks.

<a id="s13-2-7"></a>

### 13.2.7. Claws

Claws are sets of long, sharp spikes, worn on the hands as gloves. They
allow swift and accurate attacks. They are one-handed weapons, and so one
can be equipped with a shield, or two can be equipped at the same time. In
the latter case, the claws' attack bonuses are cumulative.

Only Rika can use claws.

CLAW       - 'A set of hooked claws, made of a titanium alloy'


```
¯¯¯¯
```

1000 MST     Rika begins with this weapon.
             Also available at Aiedo Weapon Store.

The weakest of the claws. Replace them with SABER-CLAWs
             straight away.


<a id="s13-2-8"></a>

### 13.2.8. Guns

Remnants of an ancient culture, guns are powerful weapons that fire some
form of ammunition upon enemies. They are two-handed weapons, hence only
one may be equipped at a time. Some guns hit all enemies on the screen.

Both Demi and Wren can use guns.

IMPACTER   - 'A gun that shoots compact bursts of air.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

S            Demi begins with this weapon.
1500 MST
             The weakest of the guns. Keep it until you can lay your hands
             on the STUN-SHOT.

             Although weaker than the PLSM-RIFLE, this weapon should be
             given to Wren as it is radiation-based and hits all enemies.


S            Found in Plate System.

             it. It can sometimes add the BINDWA Skill to attacks.

             based gun to Wren when you acquire it. It can hit all enemies.

```

```

2000 MST

> **Demi's most powerful weapon until she leaves the party, you**

won't have this weapon equipped for long.

<a id="s13-3"></a>

## 13.3. Shields

As well as weapons, some characters may be able to carry certain types of
shield. A shield uses up one hand, and therefore cannot be equipped with a
two-handed weapon. They are useful for increasing the Defence Power of a
character, but come at the cost of Attack Power. Most of the time, the best
defence is a good offence, so carrying two weapons or a two-handed weapon
is usually more beneficial than one weapon and a shield or two shields.
There are occasions, however, especially with characters that rely on their
mental power rather than their physical strength, when equipping a shield
or two may be the better option.

This section gives a list of each shield in order of DFS bonus. The symbols
following the shield names indicate which characters can use the shield:

Ch:Chaz, Al:Alys, Ha:Hahn, Ru:Rune, Gr:Gryz,
Ri:Rika, Ra:Raja, Ky:Kyra, Se:Seth

As you can see, androids may not use shields.


```
-------------------------------------------------------------------
|Shield    |Usable by                  |DFS |MTL |STR |   Price   |
|----------+---------------------------+----+----+----+-----------|
|LTHRSHIELD|Ch,Al,Ha,Ru,Gr,Ri,Ra,Ky,Se |  +2|    |    |    140 MST|
|CRBNSHIELD|Ch,Al,Ha,Ru,Gr,Ri,Ra,Ky,Se |  +5|    |    |    220 MST|
|TITNSHIELD|Ch,Al,Gr,Ri                |  +7|    |    |    600 MST|
|GRPTSHIELD|Ch,Al,Ha,Ru,Gr,Ri,Ra,Ky,Se | +11|    |    |    900 MST|
|CRMCSHIELD|Ch,Al,Gr,Ri                | +15|    |    |   2300 MST|
|LASRBARRIR|Ch,Al,Ha,Ru,Gr,Ri,Ra,Ky,Se | +18|    |    |S  1350 MST|
|PSY-SHIELD|Ch,Ha,Ru,Gr,Ri,Ra,Ky,Se    | +21|  +1|    |   4600 MST|
|PLSM-FIELD|Ch,Ha,Gr,Ri,Ky,Se          | +22|    |    |S  2750 MST|
|RFLCSHIELD|Ch,Ha,Gr,Ri,Ky,Se          | +23|    |    |  15600 MST|
|POW-SHIELD|Ch,Gr,Ri                   | +24|    | +10|S  6000 MST|
|SILVSHIELD|Ch,Ha,Ru,Gr,Ri,Ra,Ky,Se    | +25|    |    |   7200 MST|
|MAHLAYSHLD|Ha                         | +28|    |    |S 12000 MST|
|LACOSHIELD|Ch,Gr,Ri                   | +29|    |    |  20400 MST|
|GUARDSHILD|Ch,Gr,Ri                   | +30|    |    |S 14400 MST|

```

```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

14400 MST
             The strongest shield in the game, it should only be equipped
             to a character if you intend to rely more on their Techniques.

<a id="s13-4"></a>

## 13.4. Head Protection

Head protection serves to increase the Defence Power of a character. It is
not as strong as body protection, but it can make a noticeable difference
in the amount of damage a character receives. There are different types of
head protection, each suitable for different types of character.

This section gives a list of each item of head protection in order of DFS
bonus, split into the five different types. The symbols following the head
protection names indicate which characters can wear them:

Ch:Chaz, Al:Alys, Ha:Hahn, Ru:Rune, Gr:Gryz, Ri:Rika,
De:Demi, Wr:Wren, Ra:Raja, Ky:Kyra, Se:Seth


```
-----------------------------------------
```

<a id="s13-4-1"></a>

### 13.4.1. List



<a id="s13-4-2"></a>

### 13.4.2. Bands

Bands are made of small protective patches that cover the forehead, held in
place by a strip of material that wraps around the head. They are generally
the weakest of the different types of head protection, and are worn by
characters who rely most upon their mental powers.

Hahn, Rune, Raja and Seth can wear bands.

LTHR-BAND  - 'A forehead patch made of sand worm skin.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

70 MST       Hahn begins with this head protection.
             Also available at Mile and Aiedo Armour Stores.

This poor defence should be replaced by a CIRCLET as soon as
             possible, and should not be worn again.

CIRCLET    - 'A forehead patch made of a carbon-based fiber.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

100 MST      Rune begins with this head protection.
             Also available at Zema, Krup, Tonoe and Aiedo Armour Stores.

The most useful band until the Land Rover is acquired, this
             should be equipped to both Hahn and Rune when possible.

PSY-CIRCLT - 'A steel forehead patch imbued with dfs-magic.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

1200 MST     Available at Termi Armour Store.

This band should replace the standard CIRCLET as soon as it
             becomes available, as it increases the wearer's MTL score.

SILVCIRCLT - 'A circlet made of low purity Laconia.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

3000 MST     Raja begins with this head protection.
             Also available at Ryuon and Tyler Armour Stores.

Although it does not provide as high a MTL bonus, replace the
             PSY-CIRCLT with this band when the party arrive on Dezolis.

LACOCIRCLT - 'A forehead patch made of high grade Laconia.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

9600 MST     Seth begins and Raja returns with this head protection.
             Also available at Reshel Armour Store.

This is the toughest band in the game, and should only be
             replaced by the DEZO-RING when Rune acquires it.

<a id="s13-4-3"></a>

### 13.4.3. Helms

Helms are domed objects constructed of a tough material, that are worn on
the head. They are the most durable of the head protection worn by humans,
but their heaviness only makes them usable by the stronger male characters.

Both Chaz and Gryz can wear helms.

LTHR-HELM  - 'A hat made of sand worm skin boiled in wax.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

80 MST       Chaz begins with this head protection.
             Also available at Mile and Aiedo Armour Stores.

This weak helmet should only be worn until a CRBN-HELM can be
             acquired, as it is a very poor defense.

CRBN-HELM  - 'A helmet made of a carbon-based fiber.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

200 MST      Available at Krup and Aiedo Armour Stores.

Although better than the LTHR-HELM, this helmet will only be
             of use until the party reach Tonoe.

TITN-HELM  - 'A helmet made of a titanium alloy.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

570 MST      Gryz begins with this head protection.
             Also available at Tonoe and Aiedo Armour Stores.

Buy one of these for Chaz as soon as possible, only replacing
             it when you can get hold of a CRMC-HELM.

CRMC-HELM  - 'A helmet made of ceramic.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

1800 MST     Available at Aiedo Hunters' Guild Armour Store.

A very effective helmet for quite a while, this should be
             kept until the party arrive on Dezolis.

SILV-HELM  - 'A helmet made of low purity Laconia.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

3800 MST     Available at Tyler Armour Store.

Replace the CRMC-HELM with one of these as soon as you can,
             as it will be of great value until the Air Castle quest.

SWIFT-HELM - 'Helmet that increases the wearers reactions.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

S            Found in Air Castle.
4000 MST
             This unique helmet increases the wearer's AGL by a few points,
             and can also be used as a single-target SANER Technique.

LACO-HELM  - 'A helmet made of high grade Laconia.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

13800 MST    Gryz returns with this head protection.
             Also available at Reshel Armour Store.

The best helmet, Gryz should keep it equipped, but Chaz should
             replace it with the ALGO-RING as soon as it is procured.

<a id="s13-4-4"></a>

### 13.4.4. Crowns

Crowns are the favoured head protection of female humans, as they are
lighter than helms and provide almost as strong a defence. They are bands
of tough material that are worn in the same manner as helms.

Alys, Rika and Kyra can wear crowns.

LTHR-CROWN - 'A woman's helmet made of sand worm skin.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

90 MST       Alys begins with this head protection.
             Also available at Mile and Aiedo Armour Stores.

This crown is the weakest of its kind, and should be replaced
             by a tougher CRBN-CROWN as soon as possible.

CRBN-CROWN - 'A woman's helmet made of a carbon-based fiber.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

150 MST      Available at Krup and Aiedo Armour Stores.

Keep this helmet on Alys' head until the TITN-CROWN is found,
             at which point make the usual exchange.

TITN-CROWN - 'A woman's helmet made of a titanium alloy.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

490 MST      Available at Aiedo Armour Store.

Part of the titanium collection, this crown should only be
             replaced when the GRPT-CROWN becomes available.

GRPT-CROWN - 'A woman's helmet made of sand worm skin.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

1000 MST     Rika begins with this head protection.
             Also available at Aiedo Hunters' Guild Armour Store.

This useful crown should replace the TITN-CROWN as soon as
             possible, and should be kept until the party reach Termi.

PSY-CROWN  - 'A steel helmet imbued with defensive magic.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

2800 MST     Available at Termi Armour Store.

This is the only crown to give a MTL bonus, and should be
             worn until the party touchdown on Dezolis.

SILV-CROWN - 'A woman's helmet made of low purity Laconia.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

5000 MST     Kyra begins with this head protection.
             Also available at Tyler Armour Store.

A very useful crown for the majority of the Dezolis excursion,
             this should only be replaced by a LACO-CROWN.

LACO-CROWN - 'A woman's helmet made of high grade Laconia.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

15000 MST    Kyra returns with this head protection.
             Also available at Reshel Armour Store.

This is the strongest crown, and should only be replaced when
             Rika has access to the MOTA-RING.
Gear are tough coverings that are attached to an android's head to provide
protection in the same way as helmets. They are generally slightly tougher
than helms, as an android's stronger physique allows for the gear's thicker
construction.

Both Demi and Wren can wear gear.

```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

S            Demi returns with this head protection.
2800 MST      
             The strongest of all the android gear, this defensive item
             should only be replaced when Wren obtains the PALMA-RING.
Similar to bands, rings are strips of material that are placed over the
head to protect it. Most of the rings are part of the set known as the
Rings of the Stars, but there is another ring that is available at the end

             as soon as it is acquired, and kept there until the end.

<a id="s13-5"></a>

## 13.5. Body Protection

Body protection is a character's main line of defence against enemies'
physical attacks. It varies in size, shape and material, and is designed to
deflect or cushion blows to reduce damage to the wearer. There are a fair
few types of body protection, each suitable for the different types of
character. There are light outfits for physically weaker characters, and
heavier suits for stronger characters.

This section gives a list of each item of body protection in order of DFS
bonus, split into the four different types. The symbols following the head
protection names indicate which characters can wear them:

Ch:Chaz, Al:Alys, Ha:Hahn, Ru:Rune, Gr:Gryz, Ri:Rika,
De:Demi, Wr:Wren, Ra:Raja, Ky:Kyra, Se:Seth


```
---------------------------------------------
```

<a id="s13-5-1"></a>

### 13.5.1. List


```
|Type  |Body Prot |Usable by            |DFS |MTL |AGL |STR |   Price   |
|------+----------+---------------------+----+----+----+----+-----------|
|Suits |LTHR-CLOTH|Ch,Al,Ha,Gr,Ri,Ky,Se |  +2|    |    |    |    160 MST|
|      |CRBN-SUIT |Ch,Al,Ha,Gr,Ri,Ky,Se | +10|    |    |    |    550 MST|
|      |GRPT-SUIT |Ha,Ri,Ky,Se          | +16|    |    |    |   1200 MST|
|      |CYBER-SUIT|Ch,Ha,Gr,Ri,Ky,Se    | +50|    |    |  +5|S 15000 MST|
|      |MAHLAYMAIL|Ha                   | +65|    |    |    |S 24600 MST|

|      |GUARDARMOR|De,Wr                |+108|    |    |    |S  6400 MST|
-------------------------------------------------------------------------
```

<a id="s13-5-2"></a>

### 13.5.2. Suits

Suits are simple tunics woven from special fabrics. They are lightweight
and easy to wear, but do not provide a great deal of defence. As such,
stronger characters prefer heavier mails to weak suits.

Chaz, Alys, Hahn, Gryz, Rika, Kyra and Seth can wear most suits, although
there are a couple of exceptions.

LTHR-CLOTH - 'Leather armor made of tanned sand worm skins.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

160 MST      Chaz, Alys and Hahn begin with this body protection.
             Also available at Aiedo Armour Store.

The weakest armour in the game, it should be replaced with a
             CRBN-SUIT as soon as they are available.

CRBN-SUIT  - 'Protective garb made of special carbon fibers.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

550 MST      Available at Zema, Krup, Tonoe and Aiedo Armour Stores.

A useful suit early in the game, this should be replaced by
             a better suit or some mail as soon as possible.

GRPT-SUIT  - 'Protective garb made of special graphite fibers.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

1200 MST     Rika begins with this body protection.
             Also available at Zema and Aiedo Hunters' Guild Armour Stores.

This suit should be equipped to Hahn until he leaves, but
             should be removed from Rika in favour of CRMC-MAIL.

CYBER-SUIT - 'A reinforced suit that enhances strength.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

S            Seth begins with this body protection.
15000 MST
             A wholly unique suit that can only be acquired from Seth, it
             increases the wearer's Strength by a considerable amount.

MAHLAYMAIL - 'Armor that Hahn created with his father.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

S            Hahn returns with this body protection. (Only usable by Hahn)
24600 MST
             The best suit in the game, Hahn should keep this equipped
             until the very end.

<a id="s13-5-3"></a>

### 13.5.3. Mails

Far heavier than suits, these body coverings are usually wrought of metal
or some other durable substance. They are very heavy, and only a few
characters can wear them comfortably, but they are a very good defence.

Chaz, Alys, Gryz and Rika can wear mails.

TITN-MAIL  - 'Armor made of a titanium alloy.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

1120 MST     Gryz begins with this body protection.
             Also available at Tonoe and Aiedo Armour Stores.

Although far stronger than the earlier suits, this is the
             weakest mail, and should be replaced as soon as possible.

CRMC-MAIL  - 'Armor made of ceramic, anti-heat,but heavy.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

3700 MST     Available at Aiedo Hunters' Guild Armour Store.

A very useful mail until the party reach Termi, this should
             replace the TITN-MAIL as it becomes available.


<a id="s13-5-4"></a>

### 13.5.4. Robes

Robes are thin sheets of fabric that wrap around the wearer to protect them
from harm. They are naturally defensively poor, so are often strengthened
by magic to increase their protection.

Rune, Raja and Kyra can wear robes.

WHITEMANTL - 'A mantle that is imbued with defensive magic.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

S            Rune begins with this body protection.

200 MST

The weakest robe in the game is only useful while Rune joins

the party temporarily, before leaving again in Tonoe.

PSY-ROBE   - 'A magician's robe imbued with defensive magic.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

S            Rune returns with this body protection.
1500 MST
             A stronger robe than the WHITEMANTL, it gives a high MTL bonus
             and should be replaced when the FRADEMANTL is acquired.

FRADEMANTL - 'Nothing is known about this item.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

S            Found in Ladea Tower.
2000 MST
             This robe is very useful until the party arrive on Dezolis,
             where it should be exchanged for a SILV-ROBE.

SILV-MANTL - 'A mantle woven from low purity Laconia fibers.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

7300 MST     Raja begins with this body protection.
             Also available from Ryuon Armour Store and Tyler Weapon Store.

This robe should replace the FRADEMANTL as soon as possible,
             as it will be of more use during the Kuran expedition.

PHANTAROBE - 'A robe that creates an illusion of the wearer.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

8400 MST     Available from Zosa Armour Store.

Replace the SILV-MANTL with this robe, as it has the unique
             property of increasing the wearer's Agility.

RFLC-ROBE  - 'A robe with hi-resist to techniques and magic.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

18400 MST    Kyra begins and Raja returns with this body protection.
             Also available from Meese and Jut Armour Stores.

This robe will come in handy for a considerable period, and
             should only be replaced with a GUARD-ROBE.

GUARD-ROBE - 'Nothing is known about this weapon.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

S            Found in Courage Tower.
14100 MST
             The most powerful robe is one-of-a-kind, and should be given
             to the character who will benefit most from it.

<a id="s13-5-5"></a>

> 🥉 **Alt-Transform-Delete** — Defeat a Lifedeletr that combines from Wiredine + Arthropod in Weapons Plant. _(RetroAchievements · 5 pts)_


### 13.5.5. Armour

Similar to gear, android armour is attached to the body to add increased
protection from external damage. It is extremely heavy and durable, so is
only usable by androids due to their tougher physique.

Both Demi and Wren can wear armour.

TITN-ARMOR - 'Armor for androids. Made of a titan alloy.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

S            Demi begins with this body protection.
1500 MST
             Although it has a very high DFS bonus compared to other body
             protection, this is the weakest of the android armours.

CRMC-ARMOR - 'Armor for androids made of ceramic.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

S            Found in Plate System.

2000 MST

Replace the TITN-ARMOR with this armour as soon as it is

> **found, and keep it equipped until Demi leaves the party.**

SPACEDARMR - 'Double-plated armor for androids.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

S            Wren begins with this body protection.
2500 MST
             This tough armour should be kept until it can be replaced by
             the ZIRCOARMER when found.

ZIRCOARMER - 'Armor for androids made of anti-heat-metal.'


```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

- S            Found in Kuran.
- 3000 MST
- Equip this armour as soon as it is found, and have Wren
- continue to wear it until he acquires the COMPO-ARMR.

```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
```

S            Found in Climate Control Centre.
3200 MST
             A strong armour, it should replace the ZIRCOARMER when found,
             and will protect him for a fair amount of time.
